# Skyrim:The Black Star

## Overview

This article is about the quest. For the item, see [The Black Star (item)](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star_(item) "Skyrim:The Black Star (item)").

| ID: | DA01Intro, DA01 |
| Suggested Level: | 8 |
| Difficulty: | Easy |

Shrine of Azura

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Go to the [Shrine of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Shrine of Azura").
2. Speak with [Nelacar](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelacar "Skyrim:Nelacar") in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold").
3. Go to [Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep").
4. Claim the [Broken Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Broken Azura's Star").
5. Give the star to [Aranea](/wiki/Skyrim:Aranea_Ienith "Skyrim:Aranea Ienith") or [Nelacar](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelacar "Skyrim:Nelacar").
6. Cleanse the star from within.

### The Twilight of the Future

[Aranea Ienith](/wiki/Skyrim:Aranea_Ienith "Skyrim:Aranea Ienith")

All over Skyrim, innkeepers will readily tell you about the Shrine of Azura, a monument built by the [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") after they fled Morrowind. Additionally, an [encounter](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") with the wandering Dunmer [Faldrus](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldrus "Skyrim:Faldrus") will point you in the same direction, so make your way to the shrine; it is located in the snowy mountains south of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). The gigantic statue faces south atop a mountain and a long staircase. The only remaining worshipper at the Shrine, the mage [Aranea Ienith](/wiki/Skyrim:Aranea_Ienith "Skyrim:Aranea Ienith"), will claim that your arrival was expected, as Azura herself foresaw it and transferred the knowledge to her.

The prediction involves a "fortress endangered by water, yet untouched by it" and finding an "elven mage able to turn the brightest star as black as night". Aranea will admit her description to be more cryptic than useful and will direct you to the snowy town of Winterhold for clues. In Winterhold, numerous people can help, directing you to talk to a mage named [Nelacar](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelacar "Skyrim:Nelacar").

Dialogue

| Name | "Is there an elven mage here that studies stars?" | Follow-Up Question (Option 1) | Response | Follow-Up Question (Option 2) | Response |

However, it's not necessary to speak with them, so it's fastest to simply go straight to the [Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") and talk to Nelacar directly.

### The Black Star

Nelacar will provide the information that you seek, while reluctant at first, thinking you another applicant for the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"). If you reveal yourself as an agent of Azura, you will have to pass an easy-level [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") or he will dismiss you outright. He will not say no to a bit of coin either, and will break down if you intimidate him (see [bugs section](#Bugs)).

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| A priestess of Azura sent me. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Azura? Gods, it's all finally coming back to haunt me. **Failed**: You're working with the Daedra? Right. Now tell me the one about the Argonian Maid and the lusty baron. | | | | **Passed**: Locate the Star **Failed**: Nothing |
| Look, I'm willing to pay. **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: A few coins for my soul? If only you understood the irony. **Failed**: I don't think you understand. I'm not answering questions. | | | | **Passed**: Locate the Star **Failed**: Nothing |
| I didn't agree to anything. Talk. **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Just calm down. I'll tell you everything. **Failed**: Do you think muscling me is going to work? I'm a wizard. An old. Elven. Wizard. Think about it. | | | | **Passed**: Locate the Star **Failed**: Nothing |
| I misspoke. Forget I asked. | That's for the best. | | | | Nothing |

Either way, he will quickly ask you what you know about [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") and provide a quick introduction, stating that they all break after use, except for one. He will then tell you the story of one [Malyn Varen](/wiki/Skyrim:Malyn_Varen "Skyrim:Malyn Varen"), a former teacher at the College, who examined the Daedric artifact [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star") along with a few colleagues and students. Nobody knew that Malyn was actually ill and dying and was using the Star to save himself. But by trying to make himself immortal, he lost his sanity in the process. One day, the experiment escalated to the point where Malyn killed a student and attempted to use her soul for research and, as a result, was banished from the College. He, along with a few loyal disciples, moved to the secluded depths of [Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep"). Nelacar will finish with a plea that you don't return the Star to Azura. His request will be left hanging, as you can do nothing but travel to Ilinalta's Deep and search for Malyn and the Star.

### Ilinalta's Deep

A fisherman without a soul

What turned Ilinalta into Ilinalta's Deep remains a mystery, as the entire fort suddenly sank into [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta") with only the rooftops sticking out of the water. According to local legend, the place is cursed and travelers are known to go missing. Upon entering, the earthly remains of a Fisherman, his bones still in shackles, will welcome you. Examine his knapsack for a [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Fisherman%27s_Journal_(Ilinalta%27s_Deep) "Skyrim:Fisherman's Journal (Ilinalta's Deep)") and some minor loot, then proceed forward and take a left at the waterfall. Not surprisingly, given the background story provided by Nelacar, the inhabitants include [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and their [Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead "Skyrim:Undead") allies, so be on the lookout for rare ingredients and [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). The fourth room, almost completely flooded, contains two necromancers and an underwater [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Two water-soaked sleeping areas follow, with the second one containing the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Breathing Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Breathing_Water "Skyrim:Breathing Water")* (floating or on the ceiling, in a side room whose entrance is underwater), and the last containing the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") skill book *[A Tragedy in Black](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Tragedy_in_Black "Skyrim:A Tragedy in Black")*, an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), along with a locked door hiding minor loot. The next area includes a necromage, who will use frost spells, and a resurrected [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") on the other side of a pond. Dispose of the opposition, locate a nearby chest for some treasure, then pull the chain on the wall. This not only lowers the bridge behind you, it also provides access to the second zone further ahead. Stairs down the east wall into the water lead to a locked door, behind which potions and a chest are to be found. Take the western exit, and consider unlocking the door for a few potions. Proceed forward, remove the bar from the door and reenter the very first chamber of the zone, this time on a different level. You can now easily gain access to the second zone through the northern door, and a new bridge leading downstairs will make future exploration much easier.

### Malyn Varen

The remains of [Malyn Varen](/wiki/Skyrim:Malyn_Varen "Skyrim:Malyn Varen")

Proceed carefully forward through the tunnel and you will overhear two necromancers having a conversation on how to find another soul for the insatiable Star:
*"More souls are needed for the Star. The last one died before he could be harvested."*
*"We can't take another villager from the surface so soon. I told you to prepare everything properly!"*
*"We can just sacrifice another disciple. Apprentice Haerlon will be no great waste."*
*"Yes. He'll do."*
Dispose of them and look around the area for a few [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") and the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill book *[The Doors of Oblivion](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Doors_of_Oblivion "Skyrim:The Doors of Oblivion")*. A few potions can be found behind the eastern door, while the western tunnel leads to an imprisonment area guarded by a skeleton and yet another necromancer. In the final chamber, a boss-level necromancer will quickly reanimate three skeletons; after the fight, head up the stairs where you will find a dead bandit lying in her own blood, the earthly remains of [Malyn Varen](/wiki/Skyrim:Malyn_Varen "Skyrim:Malyn Varen"), along with his revealing *[Grimoire](/wiki/Skyrim:Malyn_Varen%27s_Grimoire "Skyrim:Malyn Varen's Grimoire")*, a boss-leveled chest, and [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Broken Azura's Star"), currently broken due to Malyn's experiments. Taking the Star on the floor next to the dead bandit has no consequences, other than a choice: either bring the Star to [Nelacar](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelacar "Skyrim:Nelacar") in Winterhold or to [Aranea](/wiki/Skyrim:Aranea_Ienith "Skyrim:Aranea Ienith") at the Shrine.

### A Soul to Keep

If you return to the Shrine, you will speak to Azura. She will tell you that it is unusable until you have purged Varen's soul from the star. Likewise, Nelacar will tell you the same thing. The difference is the Star's use afterwards. If you bring it to Azura, you will be able to use it to trap any sized soul except for black souls (i.e., souls from [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs")). If you bring it to Nelacar, you will be able to trap all souls, including black, though Nelacar tells you that it can only trap black souls (see [bugs section](#Bugs)).

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| The Black Star  **Nelacar** When you return to the Frozen Hearth, Nelacar will be astounded that you managed to bring back the Star, but will soon realize the exact reason for the many disappearances in and around Ilinalta. Malyn Varen now resides inside the Star, but, to stay alive, needs more and more souls, which were provided by his disciples until now. After a bit of examination, Nelacar will see the opportunity to finish what he and Malyn started all those years ago, and will suggest that you cleanse the Star. If you accept, he will trap your soul and send you into the Star to confront Malyn. | Azura's Star  **Aranea** Head back to the Shrine of Azura, and an eager Aranea will immediately take the broken Star from you, then invite you to communicate with [Azura](/wiki/Lore:Azura "Lore:Azura"). Place your hands upon the altar, and Azura will speak from the planes of Oblivion. She will say how grateful she is to see the Star returned, but will also provide the bad news: due to Malyn's occupation of the Star, the artifact will be useless to you until you venture inside and banish Malyn's soul by defeating him. Once you are ready, Azura will promise to watch over you as you are transported inside the Star's realm. |

### Inside the Star

Malyn Varen inside the Star

Once you have made your choice, you will be transported [inside the star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star_Interior "Skyrim:Azura's Star Interior") to battle Malyn Varen. The interior of Azura's Star is a light-blue, surreal world with spikes and chiming sounds. Malyn will be waiting for you just inside, eager to feast on yet another soul; he will, however, quickly realize that something is wrong and rush further into the Star, throwing a few leveled [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") at you. The interior offers very little to hide behind, making stealth a difficult option for combat. It is not possible to fall over the ledges, so proceed forward and remember to collect the valuable [Daedra Hearts](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") from fallen enemies. Once you have defeated Malyn, depending on your earlier choice, the Star will turn either black or white and you will be returned to your mortal body in Skyrim. If you went with Aranea, you will be given the restored [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star"), capable of capturing White Souls. Additionally, Azura will set Aranea free and she may become a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"). If you went with Nelacar, you will receive [The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star_(item) "Skyrim:The Black Star (item)").

## Notes

- Upon completing the quest, two necromancers may hunt you down. One of them carries *[a scrawled note](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Scrawled_Note "Skyrim:A Scrawled Note")* that reads: *"Malyn Varen's death will not go unpunished. Find the holder of Azura's Star and enact vengeance, or it will be your souls I rend for my enchantments."*
- Some people will comment if you have Azura's star in your possession:
  - Guards react with awe, saying *"By Shor, is that... is that Azura's Star? How did you come to possess such a rare treasure?"*
  - Nelacar reacts negatively, saying, *"I don't like doing business with Azura's faithful... make it quick."*
  - The Azura-worshipping denizens of Solstheim, however, have no unique reactions.
- It is possible to defeat Malyn before he can flee further into the star by immediately exiting conversation with him and using an attack that paralyzes or staggers him, such as a [power attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Power_Attack "Skyrim:Power Attack"), a spell or poison with a [Paralyze](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralyze_(effect) "Skyrim:Paralyze (effect)") effect, or [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force"). This is especially useful if you are having trouble dealing with the magical damage this location's foes throw at you.
- It is possible to reach [Ilinalta's Deluge](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deluge "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deluge") by using Whirlwind Sprint at the highest rock nearby. If you retrieve Broken Azura's Star before starting the quest, you can give it to Nelacar but not Aranea Ienith.
- Once you kill Malyn Varen you will be pulled out of the star, so be sure to loot all desired items from him and the other foes as soon as possible.

## Bugs

- Nelacar's persuasion check compares against his own Speech skill instead of yours, and so will always fail, unless wearing the Amulet of Articulation.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- If you talk to [Dagur](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagur "Skyrim:Dagur") after you speak to Nelacar and inquire about a mage who studies stars, the quest will add an objective to talk to Nelacar. Since you already have, you can not get the quest to update that point because the proper options are already gone. It does not appear that this prevents you from progressing with the previously added objective of finding the star.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
- Despite the Black Star's supposed inability to collect white souls, it can actually collect any soul.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, addresses this issue. The Black Star will now be restricted to black souls ONLY.
- A boulder meant to prevent access to the second zone of [Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep") will occasionally still be present, even during the quest. The only known fix is to exit and reenter the ruin. **?**
- Even after completing The Black Star, this quest can be restarted and reenter the journal. If this happens, it cannot be completed, as talking to Aranea Ienith again at the Shrine will not advance it further.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
- If you are killed by a dremora in the Star after killing Malyn Varen, you might spawn at your last save with both the repaired Star and the broken Star in your inventory.
- When you approach Malyn Varen, you may not be able to pick up the star. Also, at the end of the quest, you may not be given the star.
  - Reloading a saved game should fix this.
  - The bug when approaching Malyn can also be fixed by adding a Black Star to your inventory via console (`player.additem 63b29 1`) and then dropping it. Once dropped, both the Black Star from your inventory and the Star stuck to Malyn should be next to each other.
- You can escape the dialogue with Nelacar right after the Persuade speech check but before advancing quest stage. It can then be repeated for leveling up Speech. **?**
- The large crystal on the upper right corner inside the star is not solid, allowing you to fall through it. **?**
- The Black Star may disappear from your inventory randomly after completing the quest. **?**
  - Might be fixed by reloading a prior save with the star, dropping it on the ground and picking it back up.

## Quest Stages

| Introduction (DA01Intro) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Visit the Shrine of Azura |
| The Black Star (DA01) | | |
| 10 |  | Aranea, a priestess of Azura, says I am destined to find "an elven man, who can turn the brightest star as black as night." She believes he is in Winterhold. *Objective 10:* Find the elven mage from Aranea's vision |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Speak to Nelacar |
| 30 |  | Nelacar has told me that his old mentor, Maylyn *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* Varen, was experimenting on Azura's Star. Malyn's last known location is Ilinalta's Deep. *Objective 30:* Find Azura's Star |
| 50 |  | I have Azura's Star, but it's been corrupted by Malyn Varen's magic. I could take the Star to either Aranea or Nelacar to have it repaired. *Objective 40 or 45:* Bring the Star to Aranea *or* Bring the Star to Nelacar |
| 61 |  | *Objective 60:* Speak to Azura |
| 62 |  | *Objective 62:* Tell Azura you're ready to enter the Star |
| 65 |  | *Objective 65:* Tell Nelacar you're ready to enter the Star |
| 70 |  | I am inside Azura's Star and must defeat Malyn Varen's soul in order for Azura to purify the Star and bring me out. *Objective 80:* Destroy Malyn Varen's soul |
| 75 |  | I am inside Azura's Star and must defeat Malyn Varen's soul in order for Nelacar to bring me out and complete the Black Star. |
| 85 |  | *Objective 80:* Destroy Malyn Varen's soul |
| 100 | ☑ | I have cleansed Azura's Star, the infinite Soul Gem. It is mine to do with as I see fit. |
| 110 | ☑ | I have completed the Black Star, an infinite Black Soul Gem. It is now mine to do with as I please. |
| 250 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table:
  - DA01Intro: 100.
  - DA01: 0, 25, 57, 58, 60, 80, 90, 95.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DA01Intro, DA01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DA01Intro, DA01`.

# Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring") |
| Location(s): | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Orphan Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan_Rock "Skyrim:Orphan Rock"), [Eldergleam Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldergleam_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Eldergleam Sanctuary") |
| Reward: | [Nettlebane](/wiki/Skyrim:Nettlebane "Skyrim:Nettlebane"), [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") Training |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | Sap way: 0→1 ([Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring")) |
| ID: | T03 |
| Difficulty: | Easy |

The Eldergleam

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Agree to help [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring") restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen").
2. Head to [Orphan Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan_Rock "Skyrim:Orphan Rock") and claim [Nettlebane](/wiki/Skyrim:Nettlebane "Skyrim:Nettlebane").
3. Return to Danica, who sends you to the [Eldergleam Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldergleam_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Eldergleam Sanctuary").
   - *(Optional)* Escort [Maurice Jondrelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Maurice_Jondrelle "Skyrim:Maurice Jondrelle") to Eldergleam.
4. Use Nettlebane to cut through the roots, then make a choice:
   - Activate Eldergleam to retrieve the [sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldergleam_Sap "Skyrim:Eldergleam Sap").
   - Let Maurice pray to the tree and obtain a [sapling](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldergleam_Sapling "Skyrim:Eldergleam Sapling").
5. Return to Danica to complete the quest.

### The Gildergreen

*"It's a shame, isn't it?"*

The only temple dedicated to [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth"), goddess of air, wind, and sky, is located in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and is being maintained by priestess [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring"). Just outside the temple grows the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen"), a tree planted in the earliest days of Whiterun and considered holy by worshippers of Kynareth. However, the tree was recently struck by lightning and has faded away, much to the dismay of traveling pilgrims and the citizens of Whiterun. Danica Pure-Spring, while willing to solve the problem with the sacred tree, has her hands full due to the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), so the tree is still dead. If you ask innkeeper [Hulda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda "Skyrim:Hulda") or local bard [Mikael](/wiki/Skyrim:Mikael "Skyrim:Mikael") for the latest gossip, they will both tell you about the state of the tree and point you towards Danica Pure-Spring. Danica sits under the tree every morning from 7am, trying to get someone to help her out; otherwise she will be in the temple tending to the sick and injured. When you talk to her, she will immediately complain about the situation, and explain what needs to be done to make it bloom again.

### Nettlebane

*"You'll have to deal with the Hagravens."*

The Gildergreen was grown from a cutting of the legendary [Eldergleam](/wiki/Lore:Eldergleam "Lore:Eldergleam"), an ancient tree said to be thousands of years old, from before the [Atmorans](/wiki/Lore:Atmora "Lore:Atmora") set foot in Skyrim. Danica claims that sap from the parent tree can be used to restore the Gildergreen to its former glory, but there is a catch. The Eldergleam can't be cut with a normal weapon, so you will have to deal with [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") and claim the dagger they made to kill [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"), named [Nettlebane](/wiki/Skyrim:Nettlebane "Skyrim:Nettlebane"). Danica then sends you off to [Orphan Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan_Rock "Skyrim:Orphan Rock"), a hagraven nest northeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").

As you approach Orphan Rock, you will find the surrounding area protected by four residing [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch"), two of them on the ground below the rock and two more witches near a camp further up the slope. They will attack you on sight and use lower-level [destruction spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells#Destruction_Spells "Skyrim:Spells") to keep you away from Orphan Rock and its unique treasure. The rock itself is accessed via a fallen-down tree stump and is protected by a single hagraven who will use fire spells on you. She can be difficult to deal with at lower levels, so it's advisable to try to kill the witches first before alerting her to your presence. Once you've disposed of the hagraven claim Nettlebane from the corpse, then loot Orphan Rock of valuables.

### An Angry Pilgrim

Back in the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth"), Danica has received a visit from a traveling pilgrim, namely [Maurice Jondrelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Maurice_Jondrelle "Skyrim:Maurice Jondrelle") who is understandably upset about the current state of the Gildergreen and now spends his time bothering the busy priestess:

*"What is it... what has happened to the Gildergreen?"*

**Maurice**: *"What is it... what has happened to the Gildergreen? I have traveled long here to worship beneath its branches."*
**Danica**: *"It was taken by a lightning strike. Wish I had time to deal with it, but it's hard enough with all these wounded from the war."*
**Maurice**: *"Please, don't just let it stay like this. It's disgraceful."*
**Danica**: *"I really don't have time to deal with you right now. Please just let me get back to my work."*
**Maurice**: *"But this is supposed to be your work."*

When you show Danica the dagger you acquired from the hagraven, she will be quite surprised but will refuse to touch it, leading to her asking for another favor. You are to travel to the [Eldergleam Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldergleam_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Eldergleam Sanctuary") and retrieve some of its sap. From his spot in the corner, Maurice Jondrelle will overhear the conversation and will quickly seek you out and ask if he can accompany you on the journey. He reasons that he always wanted to visit the tree of legend, so let him tag along for the ride. You can also refuse to let him tag along, but then you will miss out on some important opportunities later on.

Maurice is not your average [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") and can't be given orders. Additionally, he is overly aggressive for an unarmed pilgrim and will attack any enemy you encounter, even dragons. Save your game when leaving the temple (or see [notes](#Notes)), then travel towards the Eldergleam Sanctuary, located near the sulphurous pools and hot springs of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"), and slightly north from [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing"). Do your best to keep Maurice out of trouble, then enter the sanctuary.

### Eldergleam Sanctuary

The Eldergleam Sanctuary is a large, naturally-lit cave inhabited by [peaceful](/wiki/Skyrim:Asta "Skyrim:Asta") [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Sond_(bandit) "Skyrim:Sond (bandit)") of Kynareth and contains the legendary tree in all its glory, its roots twisting and turning across the chamber, effectively blocking the path to the tree itself. Maurice will be understandably impressed with the place but will be quite shocked when you pull out Nettlebane. Hack away at the four roots and watch them bend away from the path. When you reach the top, an important choice is to be made, as Maurice will walk up to you and accuse you of disrespecting a true miracle of Kynareth. You can either choose to hear him out, which will result in a peaceful solution – or you can choose to ignore him and use Nettlebane to extract the sap, and awaken the wrath of Kynareth.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [Maurice](/wiki/Skyrim:Maurice_Jondrelle "Skyrim:Maurice Jondrelle") praying to the Eldergleam  The Gildergreen Sapling  **A prayer to Kynareth** If you choose to listen to Maurice, he will reveal that he can solve Danica's problem without resorting to violence against the sacred tree. Agree to let him help and he will walk up to the tree, get down on his knees and pray silently to Kynareth. Moments afterward, a sapling will emerge from the ground and a happy Maurice will convince you that this is the correct solution, even if Danica will be unhappy: Danica will want to see that the true blessings of nature lie in renewal, not a slavish maintenance. Pick up the sapling and watch Maurice start a new life in the Sanctuary. Return to Danica in Whiterun, and tell her that you received a sapling instead of the sap. She will be skeptical about replacing the huge Gildergreen with a small sapling, but will eventually recognize it as the best solution. She will then finish the quest and will offer master [training](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"). The next time you visit Whiterun, the Gildergreen will be growing again (see [bugs](#Bugs)). | [Spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") attack  The restored Gildergreen  **Wrath of Kynareth** If you choose to ignore Maurice (assuming he came with you), he will stand back as you cut the tree to extract the sap. As soon as you have acquired it, he will turn hostile and attack. Additionally, several [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") will show up in the chamber, including a very powerful boss-leveled spriggan. They will usually kill the peaceful inhabitants and will obviously go directly after you. Dispose of Maurice (if he's there) and the spriggans. After the battle, receive the limited treasure from the now empty sanctuary and leave the same way you came. Back in Whiterun, Danica will be quite happy when you hand her the sap and will reward you with her services as a master level [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"). This will end the quest and return the Gildergreen to its original, glorious state the next time you visit Whiterun. |

## Notes

- The Gildergreen Sapling's burlap sack sticks up out of the ground slightly in Eldergreen Sanctuary.
- Maurice is an unusually aggressive fighter in spite of being unarmed, which puts him at a significant risk of being killed on the way to the Eldergleam Sanctuary.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, addresses this issue. Maurice's confidence value is lowered such that he won't be so inclined to charge into battle.
  - Regardless of whether you have the unofficial patch installed or not, the most fail-safe way to keep Maurice alive is by simply fast-travelling to the Eldergleam Sanctuary as soon as you both leave the Temple of Kynareth. However, this requires you to have already travelled towards the Sanctuary and marked it on your map *before* you bring Nettlebane to the Temple.
- Completing this quest counts towards the [Sideways](/wiki/Skyrim:Sideways "Skyrim:Sideways") [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements"), regardless of whether you bring Danica the sap or the sapling (i.e., quest stages 100 and 105 both qualify).
- Whiterun guards will comment after the quest is finished, regardless of whether you bring Danica the sap or the sapling (i.e., quest stages 100 and 105 both qualify).

## Bugs

- Maurice may not initiate the conversation asking to join you on your trip to the sanctuary. Returning to the temple may trigger a scene where he asks to join you.
- If Maurice does not run up to you after you have cut the last of the roots on the way, walking back down the path to him may cause him to initiate the required conversation.
- If you choose the sapling option, the Gildergreen in Whiterun will show the new sapling growing inside the frame of the old tree. This is because the old tree is not removed by the game. The sap option avoids this problem and allows Gildergreen to fully bloom over time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
  -  This can be fixed by using the following console commands: `prid 00046360` followed by `disable`.
- After Danica tells you to go to the Eldergleam Sanctuary, Maurice would still run his scene with her because the dialogue script evaluates his AI before stopping the scene.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.
- If you complete Battle for Whiterun ([Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Imperial)") or [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")) after doing this quest, the tree may disappear forever. Other times, it will disappear, but if you quick-save and quick-load, the tree will reappear again. **?**
- If you travel to the Sanctuary and clear out some of the roots, but then decide you'd rather have Maurice's help rather than fight the spriggans, when you return to the Temple he will confront you with the usual dialogue, except immediately afterwards he will jump to the "I had no idea you were a man of violence!" portion of the dialogue as if he were there to see you cut the roots. You will then have the conversation about what to do while still in the temple, and it will jump to "Follow Maurice" stage of the quest. He will run out of the temple and all the way to the Sanctuary. If you fast travel to the sanctuary he will already be standing next to the tree. **?**

## Quest Stages

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage T03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest T03`.

# Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Vampires.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Vampires.png) | **Fill the [Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:Bloodstone Chalice") from the Bloodspring at [Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatic after completing [Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline") and accepting Lord Harkon's Gift |
| Location(s): | [Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den") |
| Reward: | Access to the [Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:Bloodstone Chalice") in Castle Volkihar Vampire radiant quests and followers [CuSith](/wiki/Skyrim:CuSith "Skyrim:CuSith") and [Garmr](/wiki/Skyrim:Garmr "Skyrim:Garmr") become available Furnished Serana's room in Volkihar Keep Volkihar Clan Membership |
| ID: | DLC1VampireBaseIntro |
| Suggested Level: | 1 |
| Difficulty: | Easy |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline") (accept Lord Harkon's offer) | **Next →** [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Vampire) "Skyrim:Prophet (Vampire)") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline") (accept Lord Harkon's offer) | | → Next | [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Vampire) "Skyrim:Prophet (Vampire)") | | |

Salonia and Stalf preparing to attack you at the Bloodspring

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Garan Marethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Garan_Marethi "Skyrim:Garan Marethi").
2. Fill the [chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:Bloodstone Chalice") at [Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den").
3. Defeat [Stalf](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalf "Skyrim:Stalf") and [Salonia Caelia](/wiki/Skyrim:Salonia_Caelia "Skyrim:Salonia Caelia").
4. Return to [Garan Marethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Garan_Marethi "Skyrim:Garan Marethi").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Garan arguing with Vingalmo and Orthjolf

Having completed [Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline") and accepted [Lord Harkon's](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon") gift, speak to [Garan Marethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Garan_Marethi "Skyrim:Garan Marethi") to deliver Harkon's message. Though vague, he will understand and tell you about the [Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:Bloodstone Chalice"), an artifact able to increase the potency of [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") powers. He'll ask you to follow him to the artifact; along the way, you'll come across [Orthjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthjolf "Skyrim:Orthjolf") and [Vingalmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Vingalmo "Skyrim:Vingalmo"), whose interest in your task hints towards things to come.

:   **Garan**: *"Excuse us. I need to fetch the Bloodstone Chalice."*
:   **Vingalmo**: *"The Chalice? Why?"*
:   **Orthjolf**: *"What're you up to, Garan?"*
:   **Garan**: *"Lord Harkon's orders, Orthjolf. Calm yourself. Our friend here has been ordered to fill the Chalice."*
:   **Orthjolf**: *"Really?"*
:   **Garan**: *"Indeed. He/She's off to [Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den")."*
:   **Vingalmo**: *"Well, then... Best of luck to you."*

Continue on to the chalice room, where Garan will give you your detailed orders. You'll need to travel to Redwater Den and fill the Chalice from the Bloodspring there. Once that's done, you'll need to add the blood of a powerful vampire to it. Garan will warn you that Redwater Den is inhabited by "less reputable members of society", and send you on your way. You can now ask Garan for more information about the bloodspring, and he'll tell you that although it looks like blood, it unfortunately isn't, but still has powerful potential nevertheless.

Travel to [Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den"), a [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") trading hub. Approaching what looks like an abandoned shack, there are two [lookouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Lookout "Skyrim:Redwater Lookout") keeping watch, who will direct you downstairs, assuming you're there for skooma. After entering through the trapdoor in the back, you will have to pass by a [doorman](/wiki/Skyrim:Doorman "Skyrim:Doorman") who warns you to *"keep your weapons to yourself"* before allowing you to enter the door. Downstairs, you'll find a [Dealer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dealer "Skyrim:Dealer") behind a locked, gated counter, and past her, a corridor of booths set up for enjoying skooma. There are various NPCs through here who are currently under the effects of the [Redwater Skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Skooma "Skyrim:Redwater Skooma"), content to ignore you and get their fix. Walking along the corridor is an [attendant](/wiki/Skyrim:Attendant "Skyrim:Attendant") who will tell you *"That door is locked for a reason"* if you approach the locked gate at the end of the hall with him nearby. From this point there are two ways to continue on, both leading to the same destination:

- Pick the lock at the gate, turning the dealer and the attendant hostile should they see you. (Note: After finishing the quest, everyone left alive except the Dealer will be a vampire thrall on your return, some hostile. You may wish to kill them all ahead of time to avoid later inconvenience.) After dealing with them you will enter a large open area filled with various alchemy ingredients, vampires, and their thralls. Fighting your way up the large ramp will lead you past a bridge with a lever, then more corridors. Slowly the amount of enemies will lessen, and [Death Hounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound") will start joining the fights, until you reach a large open room filled with solely vampires and their hounds.
- Alternatively, if you approach the Dealer, you either have the option of buying some Redwater Skooma, or passing a persuasion check and getting a "free sample" from her. Either way, after drinking it your vision will go blurry, and you will wake up in a cage within large dim room filled with vampires. Unlocking the gate nearby will put you back on the same path as above, allowing you to continue forward from the same point. The cage has a copy of the Spell Tome - [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis").

Regardless of the option chosen, you will end up in a large open area full of vampires and thralls, who you can overhear discussing the spring:

:   **Thrall**: *"So why don't you just drink the blood from the spring? I mean, that seems easier than running a skooma den..."*
:   **Vampire**: *"The boss said it's some sort of profaned spring. It looks like blood, but it's not the real thing. Drinking it gives you strength, but it also gets you pretty messed up... That's why we thought of putting it in the skooma."*

Be careful during the fight against these vampires as there is a gate on the ground that is extremely hard to see due to the low lighting; if step on it, it will open—drop you in a spike pit below the room and require you to climb the spiral ramp back out. Continuing on, you will head up a ramp to the east which leads to a pull chain — opening the gate to your left as well as a door directly across from you. From here, you will follow through a fairly linear set of corridors and rooms lined with coffins, most patrolled by vampires and Death Hounds. If you see a Death Hound, there is a good chance it is closely followed by its master. Following along you will encounter [Venarus Vulpin](/wiki/Skyrim:Venarus_Vulpin "Skyrim:Venarus Vulpin"). Kill him and take the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Wellspring_Key "Skyrim:Redwater Wellspring Key") to the next door from his body, and finally you will reach the end of the dungeon—the Bloodspring.

Approaching the spring will prompt you to fill the Chalice; upon doing so, two vampires, [Stalf](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalf "Skyrim:Stalf") ‎and [Salonia Caelia](/wiki/Skyrim:Salonia_Caelia "Skyrim:Salonia Caelia"), will enter through the back door. After a short conversation between themselves, it becomes clear that you are to become the latest casualty in Vingalmo and Orthjolf's politicking. (Don't attack them without allowing them to argue, or that will make you a traitor in Lord Harkon's court.)

:   **Salonia**: *"It's really too bad, you know. The little accident you had here, completely unexpected..."*
:   **Stalf**: *"Yeah, too bad. Lord Harkon's new favorite, dead so soon after joining the family."*
:   **Salonia**: *"We're just lucky I was here to return the Chalice to Vingalmo, so he could make sure Harkon gets it back."*
:   **Stalf**: *"Wait, what? That's not what we agreed. We take it back together."*
:   **Salonia**: *"Idiot. You didn't really think I'd let you walk out of here either, did you? Vingalmo wants you both dead."*
:   **Stalf**: *"Well that's just fine. Orthjolf told me to finish off anyone who got in the way."*

The restored Bloodstone Chalice in Castle Volkihar

They will then become hostile towards you. Eliminate them both. Once dispatched, your quest journal will be updated with the objective to "Fill the chalice with the blood of an ancient vampire" which requires you to select one of the two you just killed, filling the rest of the Chalice with their blood. Take the door they entered from, which is now unlocked, and you'll find that it leads up to the main area of the skooma den, ending up leading through a hidden door in the stockroom behind the dealer's counter. Once back in the main room, whatever inhabitants are still alive will be vampire thralls. Make your way past these, and return to Garan to tell him what happened.

Garan will explain to you that Vingalmo and Orthjolf long for Harkon's throne, but can't make overt moves against him; this is why each sent an underling to kill you and return with the Chalice. Robbed of their servants, neither of them will be able to act against him through them any more. He comments on the politics of the court and warns you to be careful who you trust. He then informs you that Harkon wishes to speak to you himself, leading to the next quest.

## Notes

- After completing this quest, you will be allowed to take almost everything in the castle freely a without to hostility NPCs. Serana's room will be furnished as well, though you'll never see her roaming around in there.
- Although Garan tells you that you can either deal with the inhabitants or force your way through, there is no real choice but to force your way through.
- When you enter the Wellspring, the exit door to Redwater Den will be locked and require an unobtainable key. Neither the [Redwater Den Backrooms Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den_Backrooms_Key "Skyrim:Redwater Den Backrooms Key") nor the [Redwater Wellspring Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Wellspring_Key "Skyrim:Redwater Wellspring Key") will open it. You'll gain access once you fill the Chalice, defeat Salonia and Stalf, and add the blood from one of them to the Chalice.
- If you cause Salonia and Stalf to be disintegrated ([Dawnbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnbreaker "Skyrim:Dawnbreaker"), [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), etc.), you can still retrieve the vampire blood for the Chalice from their ash piles.
- During the quest, you can freely roam around [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") without danger to yourself. You can ask [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran") for information on the Dawnguard, you can ask [Agmaer](/wiki/Skyrim:Agmaer "Skyrim:Agmaer") and [Durak](/wiki/Skyrim:Durak "Skyrim:Durak") why they joined the Dawnguard, and you can ask [Celann](/wiki/Skyrim:Celann "Skyrim:Celann") about his history with Isran. Be warned, however, that everyone inside and the patrols in [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon") will be hostile once you finish the quest.
- You may [randomly encounter](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") a [Vampire Hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Vampire_Hunter "Skyrim:Dawnguard Vampire Hunter") after completing this quest.
- Drinking from the Bloodstone Chalice grants the [Blood of the Ancients](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_of_the_Ancients "Skyrim:Blood of the Ancients") active effect. The potency of this blessing can be increased up to four times by repeatedly doing the quest [Ancient Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Power "Skyrim:Ancient Power").

## Bugs

- When returning to the castle to complete the quest, everyone inside may turn hostile towards you for no obvious reason. This could be caused from attacking Salonia and Stalf before they turn hostile against you while fetching the chalice. Waiting outside for 24 hours before entering should make them friendly again.
  - Commit crime to any City and serve sentence to jail. After serving sentence in the jail, before entering to Volkihar Keep should make Vampires from Volkihar Clan friendly again.
  - If you are unable to start the quest after you have turned into a vampire and you try talking to Garan Marethi all he tells you is to go back to Lord Harkon and get changed back to a vampire, and you are unable to start the conversation with him.
  - To fix this do the following: open the console, and type  `player.setrace <race>racevampire`, replacing `<race>` with the name of your race (e.g., `player.setrace darkelfracevampire` if you are a Dark Elf).
- The dialogue may not trigger between Salonia and Stalf. **?**
  - Attack either vampire and the quest should continue as normal.
  - Alternative, reload saved game

## Quest Stages

| The Bloodstone Chalice (DLC1VampireBaseIntro) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |

| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Follow Garan |

After that, I need to add the blood of a powerful vampire and deliver the chalice to Garan Marethi. *Objective 20:* Take the Bloodstone Chalice to Redwater Spring |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1VampireBaseIntro stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1VampireBaseIntro`.

# Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Maramal](/wiki/Skyrim:Maramal "Skyrim:Maramal") |
| Location(s): | [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara"), [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") |
| Reward: | [The Bond of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bond_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bond of Matrimony"), a spouse |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =4 (Your spouse) |
| ID: | RelationshipMarriage |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** [The Gift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gift "Skyrim:The Gift") (finish [The Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice") first) | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [The Gift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gift "Skyrim:The Gift") (finish [The Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice") first) | | |

Wedding ceremony

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Maramal](/wiki/Skyrim:Maramal "Skyrim:Maramal") about marriage (Skyrim allows both same and opposite sex marriage).
2. Find a potential spouse who you wish to marry and who is willing to marry you.
3. Wear the Amulet of Mara and ask them to marry you.
4. Go to the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") and attend your wedding ceremony.
5. Select a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") for you and your new spouse to move into.

### Arranging an Engagement

Maramal performs a wedding at the temple in Riften

If you are interested in getting [married](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage"), you must first speak to [Maramal](/wiki/Skyrim:Maramal "Skyrim:Maramal") in the city of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). He can initially be found in [The Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb") tavern preaching to the locals and later at the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara"). Talk to him about marriage and he will instruct you to obtain an [Amulet of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Mara "Skyrim:Amulet of Mara"); a holy symbol of the goddess of love. At this point, you may purchase one from him for a small fee, or find one in random loot throughout the game. Any Amulet of Mara will do, so if you already have one before speaking to Maramal, there is no need to buy one.

Now you must find an NPC in whom you have an interest (A list of eligible NPCs can be found [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage#NPCs_available_to_be_married "Skyrim:Marriage")). The person that you wish to marry must have a high disposition towards you. This can be achieved by doing favors and completing quests for that character. When you have met your ideal spouse, you must approach them while wearing the amulet. This will give you new dialogue options concerning marriage.
Ask the person to marry you. If they agree, you will need to organize a wedding ceremony. Return to Maramal to tell him that you are interested in getting married at the Temple of Mara. He will be delighted and will announce that the wedding will take place the very next day; from dawn until dusk.

### The Ceremony

Early the next morning your spouse will be waiting for you in the Temple of Mara. Upon entering the building, you will walk down the aisle and take part in an age-old tradition between two people. You will be required to say your vows, with prompting by Maramal.
You are now legally married! The first decision you must make is where to live. You may live in your spouse's home or any [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") that you have purchased. This decision is *not* permanent; if at any time you want to change residences, choose the *"I'd like us to move somewhere else"* dialogue option.

## Notes

- You can call off the wedding during the ceremony if you no longer wish to get married. However, this will cause your guests, fiancé, and Maramal to be upset with you. Make amends with your spouse, and then speak to Maramal again. He's naturally distressed by your actions, but he'll agree to give you another chance. You'll also have a dialogue option with your now former fiancé to say "I never loved you anyway," which will cause you to be unable to marry that NPC thereafter.
  - Unlike other quests, once you schedule the wedding, you cannot actually have the wedding whenever you feel like it. If you do not attend the wedding at the time specified, you will fail the quest and upset everyone in attendance the same as if you had called off the wedding.
    - For best results, check the date and time frequently to make sure you're not late to the wedding. Also, stay in Riften and refrain from completing other quests until the ceremony is finished.
- You may be married only once. If your spouse dies, you will not have the option to marry again, although an unused script exists to allow remarriage. Remarriage is currently only possible with the Unofficial Skyrim Patch.
- The guests at your wedding include a number of people who have a high [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") toward you or your spouse; your friends will be seated on the northern row of pews, and your spouse's friends and family will be seated on the southern row of pews.
  - This can potentially include people you have never met before, e.g. Jarls who took the throne after you took over a hold in the Civil War.
- Potential spouses are not restricted by gender.
- You can also marry NPCs which not included Marriage candidate with console commands.

## Bugs

- Maramal says to meet back "tomorrow, from dawn til dusk". Technically this is incorrect; if you first asked him to host the wedding at 1am, he will conduct it at 11pm that night. Simply try waiting some hours until Maramal begins his wedding dialogue. You may also have to leave and then re-enter the temple if it still does not work.
- If a follower has been killed prior to this quest, they may drop through the ceiling of the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") at the same time that your spouse and their family (if they have any) arrive. This causes you to automatically fail your marriage attendance. You can talk to your spouse again and usually the wedding goes through without issues, though if you wish to avoid all this, you should not take followers on particularly risky adventures.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- During the wedding ceremony, guests may rush out the doors as soon as Maramal is finished speaking; they were intended to sandbox in the Temple afterwards, but the scene never started.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.
- When guests are already assembled and your fiance is present, Maramal may be inactive and an attempt to speak to him results in "This person is busy" dialogue option. **?**
  -  Using the console command `SetStage RelationshipMarriageWedding 100` helps to complete the wedding ceremony and triggers the next step.
- When guests are already assembled and your fiance is present, Maramal may already be at the altar and any attempt to speak to him results in a dialogue loop congratulating you on your marriage. **?**
  -  Using console command `Setstage 7404e 30` will allow you to trigger the dialogue with Maramal at the altar and complete the marriage ceremony if the "Attend Your Wedding Ceremony" step doesn't update. Then use console command `Setstage 7404e 100` to trigger dialogue with your spouse and complete the quest.
- Maramal may not give you the option to ask about marriage, regardless of whether you have an Amulet of Mara.

## Quest Stages

| The Bonds of Matrimony (RelationshipMarriage) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Speak to Maramal about arranging your wedding |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Attend your wedding ceremony |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 5, 10, 15, 100, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage RelationshipMarriage stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest RelationshipMarriage`.

# Skyrim:The Book of Love

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu") |
| Location(s): | [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") |
| Reward: | [Agent of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Agent_of_Mara "Skyrim:Agent of Mara"), [Amulet of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Mara "Skyrim:Amulet of Mara") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 0→1 (Fastred, Fastred's chosen man, Calcelmo, Faleen, Dinya) |
| ID: | t02 |
| Difficulty: | Easy |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** [Spread the Love](/wiki/Skyrim:Spread_the_Love "Skyrim:Spread the Love") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [Spread the Love](/wiki/Skyrim:Spread_the_Love "Skyrim:Spread the Love") | | |

[Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu") wants you to help the cause of love throughout Skyrim

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu") in the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
2. Help [Fastred](/wiki/Skyrim:Fastred "Skyrim:Fastred"), in [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), with her love interest.
3. Help [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") with his love.
4. Help [Ruki](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruki "Skyrim:Ruki") with her love.

## Detailed Walkthrough

[Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu") is a [priestess](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest") of the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), devoted to spreading the word and acts of the [Divine](/wiki/Lore:Divines "Lore:Divines"). When you speak with her inside the temple, asking for Mara's blessing, she will explain that earthly services on Mara's behalf are first required. When you are ready to go forth, bearing Mara's light, Dinya explains the visions that Mara has given her, and asks you to act in Mara's name to aid those who are having trouble with their love.

### Fickle Love: Fastred

Boti and Jofthor have differing opinions about their daughter's future.

Dinya will first tell you of a young woman, confused and overwhelmed by her new found feelings. She will send you to [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") to speak to [Fastred](/wiki/Skyrim:Fastred "Skyrim:Fastred"), the conflicted girl. Fastred will tell you that she is in love with [Bassianus Axius](/wiki/Skyrim:Bassianus_Axius "Skyrim:Bassianus Axius"), but her parents will not let them be together; she will ask you to speak to them in that regard. Her mother, [Boti](/wiki/Skyrim:Boti "Skyrim:Boti"), will reveal that she is not against the relationship, and even if Fastred were to run away with Bassianus, she would do her best to handle her husband's ire. Fastred's father, [Jofthor](/wiki/Skyrim:Jofthor "Skyrim:Jofthor"), on the other hand, will make it clear that he does not want his daughter to leave town. He believes she is merely infatuated with Bassianus and will soon change her mind, just as she did with her previous interest, [Klimmek](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek "Skyrim:Klimmek").

If you encourage Bassianus, he and Fastred will move to Riften.

At this point, you can choose to talk to Bassianus, informing him of Boti's silent approval, or Klimmek, suggesting to him that he be more bold in regard to Fastred. The man you speak with will then proceed to meet with Fastred; they'll have a brief conversation which you must observe to advance the quest and ensure Mara's work is done. When the quest is completed, Bassianus will leave for Riften regardless of having favored him or not, though he will take Fastred with him if you favored him. In either case, return to Dinya Balu at the Temple of Mara to inform her of your success.

### Embers in Stone: Calcelmo and Faleen

Yngvar the Singer's poetry can melt hearts.

While Dinya is pleased with your work in Ivarstead, there is more to do. Dinya next will send you to [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to speak to [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo"). Calcelmo is a great Scholar of [Markarth](/wiki/Lore:Markarth "Lore:Markarth"), [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") researcher, and powerful [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer"). But for all of his worldliness and knowledge is simply undone by [Faleen](/wiki/Skyrim:Faleen "Skyrim:Faleen"), a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") and [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl"). Speaking directly to Faleen about Calcelmo reveals that she doesn't really have much of an opinion about the scholar. To confound the issue, Calcelmo is afraid of speaking to Faleen. He doesn't know what to talk about and worries that he'll make a bad impression by raising the wrong topic. Clearly, some type of intervention is needed. Calcelmo asks you to find out more about Faleen from her friend, [Yngvar the Singer](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvar_the_Singer "Skyrim:Yngvar the Singer"), who is quite the lady's man himself. He can usually be found inside the [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") during the day or in the [Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House") at night. You can tell Yngvar that Calcelmo is interested in Faleen, or choose to keep Calcelmo's identity a secret. In either case, Yngvar will be happy for his friend and eager to help, for a price. He will offer a [romantic poem](/wiki/Skyrim:Love_Poem "Skyrim:Love Poem"), ostensibly written by Calcelmo for Faleen, for two hundred gold. When you have completed the transaction, deliver the poem to Faleen. She will be touched and write Calcelmo an [encouraging letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Faleen%27s_Letter_to_Calcelmo "Skyrim:Faleen's Letter to Calcelmo") in response.

Calcelmo and Faleen confessing their love to each other.

Give the letter to Calcelmo and he will run off to meet her. Follow him to see them express their mutual affection in person, and the quest will complete.

**Note:** If you complete this quest after the Stormcloaks have claimed Markarth, Faleen will have been relocated to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). This will cause Calcelmo to run all the way from Markarth to Solitude to speak to her. If that happens, fast-travel to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") to witness their conversation and complete the quest.

### Withstanding Storms: Ruki and Fenrig

Ruki waiting at Gjukar's Monument.

When you return, Dinya Balu will congratulate you on helping both young and seasoned love find its way. However, she has a final challenge for you; to reach beyond death to reunite a couple torn apart by war. For this Dinya will give you an [Amulet of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Mara "Skyrim:Amulet of Mara"), which you will need to have equipped in order to see the couple. You will need to travel to [Gjukar's Monument](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjukar%27s_Monument "Skyrim:Gjukar's Monument"), a stone monument commemorating an ancient battle southeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). Here, the ghost of a woman named [Ruki](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruki "Skyrim:Ruki") is futilely searching the remnants of a battle that only she can see. She thinks that she is still alive and is looking for her love, [Fenrig](/wiki/Skyrim:Fenrig "Skyrim:Fenrig"). She had word that the battle did not go well, but she has been unable to find his body.

Ruki and Fenrig ascending into the sky.

Fenrig turns out to be quite far from Gjukar's Monument; he can found a short distance directly northwest of [Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor"), and south of the small body of water at the head of the river on the world map. Similar to his wife, he believes he is still alive and camping with the rest of Gjukar's army on the eve of the battle. His dialogue hints that he was killed in an enemy raid of the camp the night before the battle. When you give him word that Ruki has come looking for him, he will agree to follow you. Bring him back to Ruki and they will be confused, but happy to be reunited as they ascend into the sky and eventually disappear.

### A Higher Comprehension

Return to Dinya Balu where she will bestow Mara's blessing upon you as well as the [resist magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Resist Magic") [active effect](/wiki/Skyrim:Powers#Abilities "Skyrim:Powers"), Agent of Mara. You may also keep the Amulet of Mara given to you, to aid you in [finding a spouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").

## Notes

- After choosing which suitor succeeds for Fastred you must follow him to her and observe the conversation between the lovers, otherwise the quest will not update and you can't receive the next quest in the chain.
- If you leave the area after choosing Bassianus Axius for Fastred's companion and then return before seeing Dinya Balu, the parties involved may all act as if Fastred and Bassianus have left town together, despite still being there.
- It is possible to avoid mentioning Calcelmo entirely while talking to Yngvar about the love poem, yet his name will still appear on the poem - "from Calcelmo to Faleen".
- If you have completed the civil war quest line for the Imperial Legion after giving Markarth to the Stormcloaks in [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), Yngvar the Singer will be in Windhelm with the other captured Stormcloak supporters. Simply go in the Palace of the Kings and he will be at the table before the throne.
- If you watch carefully as Ruki and Fenrig are lifted into the sky, you can notice that they will experience a sudden drop before becoming invisible.
- Unlike the "Agent of Dibella" reward, this quest reward is listed as "Resist Magic" in Active Effects rather than "Agent of Mara".

## Bugs

- [Yngvar the Singer](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvar_the_Singer "Skyrim:Yngvar the Singer") or [Faleen](/wiki/Skyrim:Faleen "Skyrim:Faleen") may not give you their respective letters, preventing you from advancing through the quest.
- [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo")'s dialogue about the letter for Faleen doesn't drop away properly due to checking for a nonexistent quest stage.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- [Fenrig](/wiki/Skyrim:Fenrig "Skyrim:Fenrig") may vanish after asking you to lead the way to [Ruki](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruki "Skyrim:Ruki") and never reappear. If you then either fast travel or run to Ruki, she has the quest marker indicating to talk to her next, but she does not respond.
  -  Advance the quest using the console command `setstage t02 100`. Another console solution is using `prid 38288` and then using `enable`. This will bring [Fenrig](/wiki/Skyrim:Fenrig "Skyrim:Fenrig") back and he will follow you.
  - Provided no followers are with you, after speaking to Fenrig, when he responds stating: "If she's come this far from home..." exit the conversation and quickly fast travel to Ruki's location at the monument. Fenrig will have already joined your party and travel with you. Upon arrival, the scripted conversation between the two occurs and the quest updates as normal.
  - If the other suggested fixes do not work for you after trying them try reloading before the quest. Speak to Ruki then when you talk to Fenrig simply allow him to finish his lines. If he seems to disappear do not panic. Just walk back to Ruki (not fast travel) and the scene when they talk and float into the air should happen normally.
  - Remove the amulet of Mara after speaking to Fenrig, and travel back to Ruki. If Fenrig disappears and you are unable to interact with Ruki, enter the items menu, remove the amulet and then exit the menu. The quest should update and inform you to equip the amulet and Ruki should disappear. If you then re-equip the amulet and wait a few moments, Ruki will appear again and move to interact with Fenrig, who also should have appeared nearby.
- If Ruki or Fenrig get in a fight with a dragon while they have the quest marker, they may become unresponsive.
  -  Advance the quest using the console command `setstage t02 95`.
  - Fast traveling away and then coming back may reset the dialogue menu, allowing you continue with the quest.
- Both Ruki and Fenrig can ascend into the sky and then fall. After that, they ascend a few feet off of the ground and stay there.
  - Simply reload the last known save before both meet to fix the issue. Waiting for one hour may also fix the problem.
  - Fast travel to Riften to fix the issue.
- Picking up extra Amulets of Mara may cause you to be unable to equip the one that is given to you, which is required to progress the quest. This will prevent you from completing the quest.
  - Remove the extra Amulets from your inventory before the specific one is given to you.
  -  PC players can use the following console commands to work around this bug: `stopquest t02`, then `resetquest t02`, and finally `setstage t02 100`. Return to Dinya Balu to finish the quest.
  -  As an alternative that allows quest continuation, PC players can use the console to drop all Amulets of Mara in possession and then pick up only the quest item. If 3 or more Amulets are in possession, the non-quest Amulets will stack, allowing for easy identification of the quest Amulet. Use the command: `help "amulet of mara"` to get the item ID code (marked "ARMO"), then `player.drop (ID) (#)` where (ID) is the item ID code from the previous command, and (#) is the numeric number of Amulets of Mara possessed by the player. For example: `player.drop 000C891B 3`. Finally, pick up one of the Amulets of Mara and put it on, and if the proper quest Amulet has been identified the quest will resume.
  - Console players can have interactions with authorities. Steal a different amulet of Mara to add to you list. Then get a guard to remove your stolen goods. The reorder should put the required amulet to the top.
- If you equip the Amulet of Mara well before you first approach Gjukar's Monument, the quest marker may be floating in the air near the monument, but Ruki herself will not appear. **?**
  - Unequipping and re-equipping the Amulet of Mara should make Ruki appear. You can then speak to her and continue as normal.
- Calcelmo and Faleen are supposed to meet for breakfast and dinner each night after their portion of this quest is completed, but don't.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.5, addresses this issue. Their packages were not set up correctly to allow this to happen at the appropriate time.

## Quest Stages

| The Book of Love (t02) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've agreed to help the Temple of Mara help the cause of love throughout Skyrim. *Objective 10:* Talk to Fastred |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Talk to Fastred's parents |
| 25 |  | *Objective 25:* Talk to Bassianus or Klimmek |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Return to Dinya Balu |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Talk to Calcelmo |
| 45 |  | *Objective 45:* Get advice from Yngvar |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Deliver poem |
| 55 |  | *Objective 55:* Deliver Faleen's letter |
| 70 |  | *Objective 70:* Return to Dinya Balu |
| 80 |  | *Objective 75:* Put on the Amulet of Mara |
| 90 |  | *Objective 90:* Find Fenrig |
| 95 |  | *Objective 95:* Bring Fenrig to Ruki |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Return to Dinya Balu |
| 200 | ☑ |  |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 80:* Talk to the long-dead lover |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage t02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest t02`.
