# Skyrim:The Break of Dawn

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Daedric.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Daedric.png) | **Find [Meridia's Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Meridia%27s_Beacon "Skyrim:Meridia's Beacon") and use its light to cleanse her [temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins") of undead.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Meridia](/wiki/Skyrim:Meridia "Skyrim:Meridia")  (after finding her Beacon or Statue) |
| Location(s): | [Statue to Meridia](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_to_Meridia "Skyrim:Statue to Meridia"), [Kilkreath Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins") |
| Reward: | [Dawnbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnbreaker "Skyrim:Dawnbreaker") |
| ID: | DA09 |
| Required Level: | 12 |
| Suggested Level: | 24 |

Lady of Infinite Energies

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find [Meridia's Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Meridia%27s_Beacon "Skyrim:Meridia's Beacon") or find the [Statue to Meridia](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_to_Meridia "Skyrim:Statue to Meridia").
2. Take Meridia's Beacon to the Statue to Meridia.
3. Replace the Beacon.
4. Guide Meridia's Light through the [temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins").
5. Destroy [Malkoran](/wiki/Skyrim:Malkoran "Skyrim:Malkoran").
6. Retrieve [Dawnbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnbreaker "Skyrim:Dawnbreaker").

### The Beacon of Light

The Lady of Infinite Energies, [Meridia](/wiki/Lore:Meridia "Lore:Meridia"), is a [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") associated with the energies of living things. She is known for her hatred towards the undead of any kind. While the shrines for most other Daedric Princes in Skyrim have been hidden away in remote areas, Meridia has been given an accessible and fully intact shrine with a temple underneath. Recently, a foul darkness desecrated the temple and as such, Meridia is looking for a new champion. There are two ways to begin the journey towards becoming her champion: either find Meridia's Beacon or find the shrine.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Meridia's Beacon  **Find the Beacon** The Beacon can spawn randomly in any boss chest in the game—including those added by [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") and [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")—amounting to over one hundred fifty possible locations. If you happen to find this beacon, as soon as you put it in your inventory you will hear Meridia's voice say, *"A new hand touches the Beacon. Listen. Hear me and obey. A foul darkness has seeped into my temple. A darkness that you will destroy."* Meridia's voice will then go on to give the location of her statue. | Darkness  **Find the Statue** The Statue is located on Mount Kilkreath [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-94076&y=99077). As you ascend the steps to the Shrine, Meridia's voice will ring out saying, *"A new supplicant approaches. Listen. Hear me and obey. A foul darkness has seeped into my temple. A darkness that you will destroy. But first, you must restore to me my beacon. I shall guide you unto it. Find it and return here. And great shall be your reward."* This will add a marker to your map showing the randomized location of the beacon. |

### Meet Meridia

Meeting Meridia

When you arrive at the shrine with the beacon in hand, the otherworldly voice will echo through the woods once again, saying, *"Look at my temple, lying in ruins. So much for the constancy of mortals, their crafts and their hearts. If they love me not, how can my love reach them? Restore to me my beacon, that I might guide you toward your destiny."* Place the beacon in the gem pedestal as instructed and a giant ray of light will shoot towards the sky, transporting you high above Skyrim. Meridia will then show herself in her true form—a blinding ball of light—and will speak to you:

*"It is time for my splendor to return to Skyrim. But the token of my truth lies buried in the ruins of my once great temple, now tainted by a profane darkness skittering within. The Necromancer [Malkoran](/wiki/Skyrim:Malkoran "Skyrim:Malkoran") defiles my shrine with vile corruptions, trapping lost souls left in the wake of this war to do his bidding. Worse still, he uses the power stored within my own token to fuel his foul deeds. I have brought you here, mortal, to be my champion. You will enter my temple, retrieve my artifact, and destroy the defiler. Guide my light through the temple to open the inner sanctum and destroy the defiler."* At this point it is possible to ask about the artifact, but in any case Meridia will send you towards the ground with the words: *"Malkoran has forced the doors shut. But this is my temple, and it responds to my decree. I will send down a ray of light. Guide this light through my temple and its doors will open."*

The unlocked entrance to the temple can be found lower down on the base of the rock pillar that the statue of Meridia stands upon. The door is on the side opposite from the additional globes of light outside the locked doors and the chest located to the west.

### Ray of Light

Follow the Light

Light Combined

Once inside the [Kilkreath Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Temple "Skyrim:Kilkreath Temple"), the profane darkness is palpable everywhere -- a thick, black fog oozes through the corridors, and two burned [desecrated corpses](/wiki/Skyrim:Desecrated_Corpse "Skyrim:Desecrated Corpse") welcome you. As you proceed through the first corridor, you'll find another desecrated corpse in an alcove along the left wall, accompanied by several [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Urn "Skyrim:Containers"). Shortly after, there will be a locked door on your left, behind which is a handle that opens the adjacent gate, giving access to a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Chest "Skyrim:Containers") and some minor loot on the other side. Take the eastern path and face the first huge chamber. Meridia's ray of light will shine down through the ceiling onto a pedestal. Activate the pedestal and the beam of light will be directed onto a device placed above the eastern tunnel. Note, there are two lootable desecrated corpses in the southeast corner of this room, past the pedestal, and a patch of [white cap mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") is growing along the right-hand wall in the corridor leading to the next room.

When you follow the light, however, enemies will start to emerge. Dark shadows called [corrupted shades](/wiki/Skyrim:Corrupted_Shade "Skyrim:Corrupted Shade") will attack in hordes, trying to prevent you from bringing light to the temple. Dispose of them and enter the next chamber, then activate the pedestal to direct Meridia's light further into the depths of the ruin. A [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") and a [candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items#Dishes_and_Tableware "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items") can be located on the table and bookshelf on the left, just past the pedestal. There is also a lootable urn near the eastern passage. The eastern path is blocked, however, so locate the narrow tunnel to the south, and dispose of even more corrupted shades. There are two lootable urns along the left-hand wall. Open the wooden door, and follow the tunnel until you see a chest. There will be a desecrated corpse in the large bowl to the right of the entry door. On the left are two lootable urns and a [healing potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") on a low shelf. Now, take a left and enter yet another huge chamber with multiple paths and levels, with more corrupted shades to dispatch. In the middle of the lower level, a desecrated corpse is slumped against the table. The beam of light and the pedestal for this room are located above, so head up the set of stairs along the eastern wall. At the top, as you continue along, you'll find an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") straight ahead and another lootable urn to your right. Immediately nearby, there is also an expert-locked door, behind which is a lever to open the alcove grate to its left, containing a chest. Cross the nearby stone bridge to find the pedestal. Upon activating it, the light will open a previously locked door to the south that has lootable urns to each side. You can either jump across the small gap or use the southern staircase to reach it. In this newly accessible corridor, there are two burial urns in a left-side alcove, an urn behind a rock pile on the right, a desecrated corpse straight ahead, and another door. Simply continue through the door to get a breath of fresh air on [Kilkreath Balcony](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins#Kilkreath_Balcony "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins").

### Dawn is Breaking

A Look Outside

Once outside, you will notice your efforts have made six pillars light up, but there is still work to do. Make your way across the balcony, and you'll find a staircase leading up, with an expert-locked chest to its right. Go through the door at the top of the staircase to re-enter [Kilkreath Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins"). At the top of the stairs here, there will be a lootable urn to your left. On the right, you'll find the entrance to a huge chamber with multiple levels and more corrupted shades. Kill the opponents and start your investigation by heading left into the chamber. The ground level has a few urns, and in the southwest corner, there is an altar with another desecrated corpse. On a table to its right, there is a lootable burial urn, a [ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#Rings "Skyrim:Clothing") on top of a plate, and some loose [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). At the southern end of the chamber, note the locked door (key required). Head back to the stairs near the chamber's entrance, along the eastern wall. At the top of the stairs, on the right, is yet another door that needs a key, so go ahead and activate the first pedestal. This will open the eastern door behind you, and there are a couple potions on the shelves to its left. In the first room down the corridor, there is a corrupted shade, scattered lootable urns, and a chest with some minor loot. Hidden in the shadows on the right is a [spear-trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") door. A desecrated corpse lies in the doorway, and the room contains an urn, some potions, assorted minor loot, and a chest of minor loot. The main passage will lead the way to a lever (beware of the [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") with [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") on your way). Pull the lever and go south over the bridge. Follow it until you reach an intersection, then take a right turn. This leads you to an alcove in the northwest corner, where you'll find a corrupted shade, a desecrated corpse, and a chest. On the nearby shelves, there are also some potions and other assorted loot, including the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") skill book *[Battle of Red Mountain](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Red_Mountain "Skyrim:Battle of Red Mountain")*.

Backtrack to the intersection and make a running jump to the pedestal. Activate it, see the light shine towards a platform above, then jump back to the intersection. Make a running jump towards the now open western door (with an urn to its right), and follow the tunnel to battle even more corrupted shades. You are now in a room with stairs leading up on both sides, and there are several urns and desecrated corpses scattered around the room. The western staircase leads to a potion on a [weight sensitive plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate"), the eastern one leads to a tunnel containing a few burial urns. Follow the eastern tunnel, and you will reach a lighting pedestal, with a desecrated corpse slumped at its base. Activate this light, and it opens a final door at the southern end of the ground floor of the chamber, which will lead you to [Kilkreath Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Catacombs "Skyrim:Kilkreath Catacombs").

### A New Day is Dawning

Malkoran is waiting

Once in the catacombs, in a room at the end of the initial corridor, you'll find the final pedestal on a raised dais. Make your way to the pedestal and activate it. This will turn on the final beam of light, open the nearby door, and awaken Malkoran, the necromancer responsible for Meridia's wrath. You'll want to loot this room before leaving, as there will be no turning back once you enter the next chamber. At the base of the dais, you'll find a desecrated corpse, along with some loose gold. Along the right wall is another desecrated corpse, and in the northeast corner, there's a healing potion. In the southeast corner of the room, just beyond the dais, you'll find a chest, a magicka potion, and some burial urns, along with another desecrated corpse. Upon leaving the pedestal room, your journal will update when you reach the final chamber, and it is now your objective to kill Malkoran. He is protected by six corrupted shades and is a strong opponent who uses [frost spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage") from a distance, so use the columns to your advantage. When Malkoran is dead, be aware you will also have to face his shade. When all is said and done, Meridia will speak: *"It is done. The defiler is defeated. Take Dawnbreaker from its pedestal."* Be sure you loot the room before you retrieve the sword, as you will be transported outside as soon as you take it. In addition to the many urns and desecrated corpses scattered throughout the chamber, there is a healing potion to the left of the entryway. On a table along the left-hand wall, there is a poison bottle hidden in a bowl, and there is a second poison bottle tucked under a broken table on the right-hand side of the room. When you finally retrieve Meridia's powerful sword, everything will turn into light, and you will find yourself high above Skyrim once again, facing Meridia: *"Malkoran is vanquished. Skyrim's dead shall remain at rest. This is as it should be. This is because of you. A new day is dawning. And you shall be its herald. Take the mighty Dawnbreaker and with it purge corruption from the dark corners of the world. Wield it in my name, that my influence may grow."* Should you choose to obey her wish, you will get the polite final words from Meridia: *"May the light of certitude guide your efforts."* Should you respond that you won't spread her message, Meridia will tell you: *"It matters not. The plant cares nothing for the rays that bring it the warmth of the sun. As you carry Dawnbreaker, so will my light touch the world."*

## Notes

- If [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed, some radiant locations may be on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). If you are in Skyrim, you will not receive a quest marker pointing you to the quest location, but must travel to Solstheim first (at which point any quest markers you have to quests in Skyrim will disappear).
- There were additional lines recorded if you had found and acquired the Beacon, lost it, and then found it again. As the Beacon is a quest item, this dialogue will not be heard under normal conditions.
  - *"Do you prefer heedlessness to my luminous glory? Go! Take my beacon to the mount above Kilkreath."*
  - *"Can you not hear me? Are your ears full of hate? The defiler waxes! Go now, with haste. Take my beacon to Mount Kilkreath."*
  - *"Fool! He is perverting my Light. A Light that could illuminate Skyrim and her people."*
- Sometimes speaking to Meridia will not show a map marker for the beacon. This is because the beacon is in an area you do not have access to yet, such as [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary") or the [Katariah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Katariah "Skyrim:The Katariah"). The beacon still exists and finding it will advance the quest. On PC, `movetoqt DA09` will place you at the chest that contains the beacon.
- Even if you are a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism"), Meridia will still recruit you for this quest and declare you her champion, despite her hatred for the undead.
- There are 43 desecrated corpses throughout Kilkreath Ruins that contain large amounts of gold. If you loot them all, you can get an amount of gold in the range of 1075-5375.
- It is possible to kill Malkoran and the corrupted shades from the bottom of the staircase into the final chamber, or lure them out by firing area-of-effects through the open door from the top of the stairs. This can help to even the odds of taking on a large number of enemies at once.
- Meridia will teleport you outside the temple for your final dialogue with her, and at the end she will deposit you on the platform in front of her statue. Any followers you may have (this also includes thralls of any type, such as Dead Thralls or Atronachs) will remain inside the temple. To get them back quickly, go to the door of the temple, enter it, and exit again. When you again appear outside, your follower should have rejoined you. Alternatively, if you have Serana as a follower, fast traveling to Fort Dawnguard will usually cause her to catch up with you.
- Although the beacon will spawn in a specific location, that location will be changed the first time you enter an area that has a boss container after you reach level 12. This makes it very likely that you will find the beacon shortly after that time. The original location will only be used if you approach the statue before entering an area with a boss container.
- Although the game pushes the quest onto the player at level 12, it is useful to delay the quest if you plan on soul-trapping the Corrupted Shades. These enemies level with the player, and can fill grand soul gems if you wait to level 38 or higher.
- Although you can't re-open the double doors in the Catacombs after the quest, there is a workaround: use the plate and Whirlwind Sprint combo, and you'll regain access to Malkoran's chamber, but you won't find anything in there except for the Desecrated Corpses from before. To get out, you'll either have to reload or use the same combo again.
- You must level up via skill increases to or beyond level 12 for the quest to be eligible to start. You cannot be console-commanded to an arbitrarily high level and start the quest.
- Once you have the beacon in your inventory (either from being asked by her to get it, or finding it in a chest), the beam of light at Meridia's Shrine can be seen as far away as [Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto") in [Whiterun hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") and other areas of the map that have a view of the mountains around Solitude.
- Standing in the light path can cause you to take both lightning and Magicka damage.

## Bugs

- Meridia's Beacon may disappear from your inventory after you pick it up.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.6, fixes this bug.
- You can obtain a duplicate Dawnbreaker by knocking it off its pedestal with an area-of-effect spell during the battle with Malkoran. Retrieve the sword on the ground prior to the sword in the stand to keep both.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.3, fixes this bug.
- When you hang in the sky during the time you are supposed to be talking to Meridia after acquiring the sword, there's a strong possibility that nothing will happen and you will be left dangling in the sky, unable to complete the quest, or move anywhere.
- When you hang in the sky while talking to Meridia, she may suddenly drop you and you die when you hit the ground before the teleportation triggers.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  - This is often caused by carrying too much weight. Try dropping a few things before taking the sword.
  - Walk towards Meridia as soon as she has lifted you into the sky, thereby dropping onto the area at the base of the statue instead of a longer drop further back.
  - Skip through the dialogue with her and you will be able to adjust your position before the fall begins. You need to land on the upper area of her pedestal.
  - The warp takes some time to activate. Try and position yourself over the lowest altitude position you can to maximize your fall time. The road to the southwest is a good choice.
  - In the Windows version, a simpler and foolproof approach is to open the console when the fall starts, click on the background twice, so that no objects are selected, and enter `TCL` (or `ToggleCollision`), and exit the console. This stops the free-fall. After the teleport, open the console and type `TCL` again.
- If a dragon appears (or is already present) while you are being raised into the sky it will continue to attack, and you will be stuck in the air, as Meridia will not talk while under attack.
  - You will need to reload a save game. If it was a random dragon it may not reappear. If it was the dragon from the nearby word wall, you will need to kill it first.
- Killing Malkoran in the hallway before the chamber and/or while he is paralyzed may cause his ghost to fail to spawn, making it impossible to finish the quest. Retry from a savegame, or simply wait for the paralysis to wear off before landing the final blow. **?**
- If you have used [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow") to block out the sun there will be two suns after you give Meridia the stone. **?**
- When fighting Malkoran's Shade, using the Unrelenting Force shout or werewolf power attacks will cause the shade to stop fighting. Unfortunately, it also ceases to take damage (the frozen shade can still be damaged by the Fire Breath shout and with Destruction magic). The shade just floats there, preventing the completion of the quest.
- If you have backed Malkoran into a corner at the side of the dais killing him, his Shade may spawn inside the wall where you cannot strike him. You can use Area of Effect spells to finish him off, but you cannot loot the Shade.
- Sometimes, when you return Meridia's beacon it will appear on the pedestal, but the Beacon will stay in your inventory forever. **?**
  -  Use the `player.removeitem 4e4e6` console command to remove the Beacon from your inventory.
- Standing in the beam of light will slowly drain your magicka, but if you have an [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") armor spell active (Oakflesh/Stoneflesh/Ironflesh, etc) then you will gain Alteration skill XP.
- It is possible for the two Meridia speeches to overlap each other.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, addresses this issue. A delay has been inserted into the trigger script to prevent this from happening.
- If you have finished the Dark Brotherhood quest line, the quest marker can appear where the boss chest was in the Dawnstar Sanctuary, but the chest will have disappeared.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. The location must be in a dungeon.
- It is possible for Meridia's Beacon to spawn in an [innacessible cell](/wiki/Skyrim:Inaccessible_Cells "Skyrim:Inaccessible Cells") named testL. This bug only happens with the Dawnguard DLC installed. **?**
- This quest may fail to stop the randomizer for Meridia's Beacon if you find it before visiting Mount Kilkreath.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug.
- The double doors in *Kilkreath Catacombs* that lead to Malkoran's lair were never supposed to close and lock themselves once you open them and make your way across. As a result, the plate trick mentioned above is your only way back in.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.5, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| The Break of Dawn (DA09) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 50 |  | An otherworldly voice coming from Mount Kilkreath is commanding me to find a beacon and return it. *Objective 5:* Find Meridia's beacon |
| 100 |  | I've found a strange gem. An otherworldly voice is commanding me to bring it to Mount Kilkreath. *Objective 10:* Bring Meridia's beacon to Mount Kilkreath *(After listening to Meridia's speech)* |
| 150 |  | *Objective 15:* Replace the beacon |
| 300 |  | Meridia has commanded me to enter Kilkreath Ruins, destroy Malkoran, and retrieve the artifact Dawnbreaker. I will need to guide a beam of light through the ruins which will open the way for me. *Objective 20:* Guide Meridia's Light through the temple |
| 350 |  | *Objective 30:* Destroy Malkoran |
| 410 |  | *Objective 40:* Retrieve Dawnbreaker |
| 500 | ☑ | I have entered Kilkreath Ruins, destroyed Malkoran, and retrieved the artifact Dawnstar *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*, which Meridia has bestowed upon me for my service. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 200, 400, 450.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DA09 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DA09`.

# Skyrim:The Bulwark Jail

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Jail: The Bulwark Jail ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=The+Bulwark+Jail)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2RRBulwark02 | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") | |

The Bulwark Jail

**The Bulwark Jail** is the jail in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"), built directly into [the Bulwark](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bulwark "Skyrim:The Bulwark").

Escape tunnel leading to Coldcinder Cave

For historical information on the Bulwark, read *[History of Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock")*.

### Exterior

The Bulwark stands at the east end of Raven Rock, with its exterior nearly buried in ash. A short timbered tunnel burrows through the ash to the city's main gate, with the unlocked entrances to the garrison ("the Bulwark") and the jail facing each other just inside the gate. Two [Redoran guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard "Skyrim:Redoran Guard") are posted outside these two entrances.

### The Bulwark Jail

The entrance leads into a narrow room running from west to east, with the expert-locked cell door dividing the space in two. Outside the cell, along the north wall are two unusable barrels, the prisoner belongings chest sitting on a grate showing an area below, two crates, a chair and a small table holding a bottle of [shein](/wiki/Skyrim:Shein "Skyrim:Shein"), a bottle of [sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sujamma "Skyrim:Sujamma"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a [cooked beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Beef "Skyrim:Cooked Beef") steak, a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), and three food barrels next to the cell door. A single inattentive Redoran guard acting as jailor usually sits at the table.

Inside the cell, along the north wall is a set of shelves holding a bottle of [matze](/wiki/Skyrim:Matze "Skyrim:Matze"), a bottle of sujamma, an [ash yam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam"), a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), and copies of *[Bone, Part I](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone,_Part_I "Skyrim:Bone, Part I")* and *[Bone, Part II](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone,_Part_II "Skyrim:Bone, Part II")*, followed by a large unlit fireplace with five pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") covering a novice-locked grate to an escape tunnel. Along the south wall is an open box, a chair, an owned single bed, and another chair and a small round table holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two ash yams, a loaf of bread, and a [charred skeever meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Meat "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Meat"). The tunnel below the fireplace leads to the grate under the prisoner belongings chest, as well as another grate in the floor connected to a natural tunnel with a door to [Coldcinder Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Coldcinder_Cave "Skyrim:Coldcinder Cave").

## Bugs

- Several items in the cell don't have their ownership set. This erroneously causes them to be marked as stolen.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:The Bulwark

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

The Bulwark

**The Bulwark** is an imposing stone wall created to protect [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") from ash storms, with the city's garrison and [jail](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bulwark_Jail "Skyrim:The Bulwark Jail") both built directly into the wall.

For historical information on the Bulwark, read *[History of Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock")*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Captain Veleth](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth")  [Redoran Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard "Skyrim:Redoran Guard") |

## Related Quests

- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

### Exterior

The Bulwark stands at the east end of Raven Rock, with its exterior nearly buried in ash. A short timbered tunnel burrows through the ash to the city's main gate, with the unlocked entrances to the garrison ("the Bulwark") and the jail facing each other just inside the gate. Two [Redoran guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard "Skyrim:Redoran Guard") are posted outside these two entrances.

### The Bulwark

The Bulwark interior

The entrance leads into a long narrow room running from east to west and turning to the northwest toward the end; the garrison comprises only this room. Starting from the entrance and moving west, along the north wall are three food barrels and eight unusable barrels, a large fireplace with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit"), an owned single bed, two owned cots, a chair, the evidence chest, another owned single bed, and a chair and a table holding a bottle of [flin](/wiki/Skyrim:Flin "Skyrim:Flin"), a bottle of [matze](/wiki/Skyrim:Matze "Skyrim:Matze"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a [cooked beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Beef "Skyrim:Cooked Beef") steak, an [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox"), and a copy of *[The Axe Man](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Axe_Man "Skyrim:The Axe Man")*. Along the northwest wall to the left of the table at the end of the room is another owned single bed.

Starting again from the entrance and moving west, along the south wall are four chairs and two small round tables holding a bottle of flin, a bottle of [sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sujamma "Skyrim:Sujamma"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), an [ash yam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a cooked beef steak, a [horse haunch](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Haunch "Skyrim:Horse Haunch"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), and a [notice](/wiki/Skyrim:Posted_Notice "Skyrim:Posted Notice") from [Captain Veleth](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth") reminding the guards that [emberbrand wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Emberbrand_Wine "Skyrim:Emberbrand Wine") and similar contraband are off limits. West of the chairs and tables is a row of five weapon racks holding a selection of [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons"), and [elven weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Weapons "Skyrim:Elven Weapons"), followed by a sideboard holding three bottles of matze, two bottles of flin, two bottles of sujamma, a bottle of [shein](/wiki/Skyrim:Shein "Skyrim:Shein"), a bottle of alto wine, and a copy of *[The House of Troubles](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Troubles "Skyrim:The House of Troubles")*, with a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on the floor to the left of the sideboard. West of the sideboard is an open box containing five ash yams, followed by two owned single beds. Northwest of the beds at the end of the room is a set of shelves holding a bottle of flin, a bottle of matze, a bottle of sujamma, a complete set of [bonemold armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemold_Armor "Skyrim:Bonemold Armor") including the [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemold_Helmet "Skyrim:Bonemold Helmet"), [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemold_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Bonemold Gauntlets"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemold_Boots "Skyrim:Bonemold Boots"), and [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemold_Armor "Skyrim:Bonemold Armor"), and copies of *[Confessions of a Dunmer Skooma Eater](/wiki/Skyrim:Confessions_of_a_Dunmer_Skooma_Eater "Skyrim:Confessions of a Dunmer Skooma Eater")*, *[The Red Year, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Year,_Vol._I "Skyrim:The Red Year, Vol. I")*, *[Bone, Part I](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone,_Part_I "Skyrim:Bone, Part I")*, and *[Bone, Part II](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone,_Part_II "Skyrim:Bone, Part II")*.

# Skyrim:The Burglary Job

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Rpeh](/wiki/User:Rpeh "User:Rpeh"), [Dwarfmp](/wiki/User:Dwarfmp "User:Dwarfmp"), checked by [Riliane](/wiki/User:Riliane "User:Riliane") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Steal a special item from a wealthy home.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#The_Pay_Out) |
| ID: | TGRBE |

Vex asks you to steal something—possibly this Golden Ship Model

## Quick Walkthrough

1. After joining the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), talk to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") about burglary jobs.
2. Steal the item she assigns.
3. Return it to Vex for a reward.

### Vex

Vex is a life-long thief longing for the glory days of the Guild. When speaking with her she will tell you that she handles all the burglary, [shill](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shill_Job "Skyrim:The Shill Job"), [sweep](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sweep_Job "Skyrim:The Sweep Job") and [heist](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heist_Job "Skyrim:The Heist Job") jobs. Through these extra thievery jobs, Vex hopes to increase the cash flow into the Guild; with dreams of restoring the Ragged Flagon to what it used to be.

### The Break In

Inquire about a burglary job. Vex will tell you of an item that she knows of, a client that needs an item procured, or just a piece that has sparked her interest. However, you cannot kill anyone to get the item; it's up to good old-fashioned larceny. Upon accepting the gig, your journal and map will be updated. Occasionally, Vex will send you off with a stern warning to work first and get drunk second.
The possible items are:

- [Golden Ship Model](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Ship_Model "Skyrim:Golden Ship Model")
- [Golden Urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Urn "Skyrim:Golden Urn")
- [Jeweled Candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Candlestick "Skyrim:Jeweled Candlestick")
- [Jeweled Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Flagon "Skyrim:Jeweled Flagon")
- [Jeweled Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Goblet "Skyrim:Jeweled Goblet")
- [Jeweled Pitcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Pitcher "Skyrim:Jeweled Pitcher")
- [Ornate Drinking Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ornate_Drinking_Horn "Skyrim:Ornate Drinking Horn")

The location can be any of the twenty-nine wealthy house in Skyrim. You may be assigned the same location more than once.

| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Nepos's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos%27s_House "Skyrim:Nepos's House") [Ogmund's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund%27s_House "Skyrim:Ogmund's House") [Smelter Overseer's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Smelter Overseer's House") [The Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House") | [Aerin's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin%27s_House "Skyrim:Aerin's House") [Bolli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House") [Marise Aravel's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel%27s_House "Skyrim:Marise Aravel's House") [Romlyn Dreth's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth%27s_House "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth's House") [Snow-Shod Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Manor "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Manor") [Valindor's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor%27s_House "Skyrim:Valindor's House") | [Addvar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") [Evette San's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)") [Jala's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala%27s_House "Skyrim:Jala's House") [Vittoria Vici's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici's House") | [Amren's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") [Carlotta Valentia's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia%27s_House "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia's House") [Heimskr's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Heimskr's House") *(See [Bugs](#Bugs))* [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born") [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") [Belyn Hlaalu's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House") [Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea") [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") |

The item that needs to be stolen is not added to the house until the quest is started. You must not be caught and sent to jail while the quest is active, for any reason, otherwise you will fail the quest.

### The Pay Out

Once you have the item return it to Vex for a leveled gold reward.
If you are having any trouble successfully stealing, using [strategies that modify your stealthiness](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealth#Sneaking "Skyrim:Stealth"), and items, potions, or spells (such as [Muffle](/wiki/Skyrim:Muffle_(spell) "Skyrim:Muffle (spell)")) that fortify your [sneak skill](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") can help. Making yourself [invisible](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility_(effect) "Skyrim:Invisibility (effect)") can obviously be very effective. See [crime](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime") for detailed information about stealing items.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |
| 16-20 | 200 |
| 21-26 | 250 |
| 27-31 | 300 |
| 32-36 | 350 |
| 37-41 | 400 |
| 42+ | 500 |

## Notes

- If one of the house's occupants dies for any reason while the quest is active (even if you are not responsible), you will fail the quest.
- If you are witnessed breaking into someone's house, you can use the [become ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout. You can then continue as if you had not been seen.[*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:The_Burglary_Job)*]

## Bugs

- If you have already participated in the quest [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") it becomes impossible to enter some homes in Whiterun, namely Heimskr's House and Severio Pelagia's House. However, they can still be assigned as possible quest destinations.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Quit the job and retake it for another location (you can load a previous save to avoid a failed quest if you wish).
  -  You can use the console command `coc`, followed by the editor id of the house.
- When you quit a job the item you were meant to steal remains, and when you receive another quest to steal an item from the same house, there may be more than one item in the same space. This can make the item hard to pick up since the extra item is impossible to pick up, you will have to find an angle to pick up the item required for the job.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| The Burglary Job (TGRBE) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've been told to retrieve the <Alias=ItemToGet> from <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City>. I need to complete this job without killing any of the location's residents or getting caught and spending time in jail. *Objective 10:* Retrieve the <Alias=ItemToGet> from <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> |
| 50 |  | I've retrieved the <Alias=ItemToGet> from <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City>. *Objective 20:* Return the <Alias=ItemtoGet> to Vex |
| 200 | ☑ | I've successfully completed the job and received my share of the pay. |
| 250 | ☒ | By killing a resident at the task's location, I've failed this job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | During the course of this task, I was arrested and sent to the local jail. I've therefore failed the job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | Before the task could be completed, I decided to quit. I've therefore failed the job and forfeited any pay I might have received. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGRBE stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGRBE`.

# Skyrim:The Caller

## Overview

| The Caller (RefID: 0004D247) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep") | | |
| Race | [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") | Gender | Female |
| Level | Radiant (7-40) | Class | [Fire/Frost/Shock Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock_Mage "Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock Mage") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0004D247 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0004D246 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 175-500 | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 190-460 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 25-50 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")**, **[Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration")**, [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") | | |
| Class Details | [CombatMageElemental](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageElemental "Skyrim:CombatMageElemental") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Aggressive |
| Voice Type | [FemaleElfHaughty](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleElfHaughty "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleElfHaughty") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [WarlockFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:WarlockFaction "Skyrim:WarlockFaction") | | |

The Caller

**The Caller**, a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [elemental mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageElemental "Skyrim:CombatMageElemental"), is the leader of a band of mages in [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep"). Unlike the rest of her group throughout the dungeon, she will not outright attack you on sight. As explained by [Orthorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthorn "Skyrim:Orthorn") when you find him in the keep, The Caller is in possession of the three books that Orthorn stole from the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), namely *[Night of Tears](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_of_Tears "Skyrim:Night of Tears")*, *[The Last King of the Ayleids](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Last_King_of_the_Ayleids "Skyrim:The Last King of the Ayleids")*, and *[Fragment: On Artaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment:_On_Artaeum "Skyrim:Fragment: On Artaeum")*. He mentions that she was especially interested in one volume in particular, though he neglects to tell you which one.

As a key character in the quest [Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books"), she will remain standing at all times at her podium in the Fellglow Keep Ritual Chamber. She wears [blue mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0006b46c "Skyrim:Boots"). She knows a number of leveled spells from the schools of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction"), and [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration").

## Related Quests

- **[Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books")**: Find the books needed to identify the artifact found in [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal").

### Hitting the Books

Upon entering the final chamber of Fellglow Keep and meeting The Caller during the quest Hitting the Books, she will immediately engage in dialogue with you:

:   *"So, you're the one who barged into my home and laid waste to my projects. How nice to meet you."*
:   **Who are you?**
:   *"Names no longer matter. You may refer to me as The Caller. Now, do you have a reason for making such a mess?"*
:   **I'm here for the books from the College.**
:   *"So you're just one of [Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren")'s lackeys? That's disappointing. You show real promise. You come here, kill my assistants, disrupt my work... You've annoyed me, so I don't think I'll be giving you anything."*

You then have several options of response:

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Perhaps we can come to an arrangement.** | **Passed**: *"An arrangement? After you've destroyed so much? Fine. Leave me the elf. You may go with your books."* **Failed**: *"I'm afraid you don't have anything worth trading. Now, you can go back to your College and leave me be, or I can kill you. Your choice."* | | | | **Passed**: Leave Orthorn, take the books **Failed**: Nothing |
| **Let me leave with the books, and there won't be any more trouble.** *(Persuade)* | **Passed**: *"Fine. Take them and be gone. Never return here, or else you'll face my full wrath."* **Failed**: *"Are you attempting to threaten me? After I've been so hospitable? Well, then you won't be leaving here at all."* | | | | **Passed**: Leave with the books and Orthorn **Failed**: The Caller attacks |
| **May I please have the books?** | *"Oh, now we're all please and thank you, are we? I'm afraid we're well beyond pleasantries. I'll allow you the opportunity to turn around, walk out that door, and never come back. I suggest you move quickly."* | | | | Nothing |
| **I've had enough of this.** | *"How dare you!"* | | | | The Caller attacks |

If you tell The Caller that she can have Orthorn:

:   **It's a deal. You can have Orthorn.**
:   *"Fine. Take your books and leave at once. If you ever come back, I won't be so gracious."*

Upon taking the books, if you go up to her and attempt to talk to her again, she will simply say:

:   *"You have what you came for. Now leave."*

If she becomes hostile with you after the conversation with her, you will have to fight her and two [atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"). She will randomly teleport and swap places with the atronachs during the battle.

## Notes

- Her face and hairstyle are randomly chosen.
- Her dialogue suggests you've wiped out her entire band of mages whether or not you actually killed any of them.
- Even though she will teleport during battle with you (whether or not the atronachs are still alive), if you raise her afterwards with a raise dead spell (such as Dead Thrall), she will no longer teleport when engaging hostiles.
- Although all her mages wear enchanted black robes, she is the only one to wear hooded blue mage robes.

## Bugs

- Paralyzing The Caller immediately as you initiate combat (with a weapon that has a paralysis enchantment, must damage for the bug to occur) will cause her to teleport and appear with paralysis still in effect, and it will stay in effect. Weapons will not damage her, and allies in the area will not register her as being there. Using the weapon you used to paralyze, you can spam attacks onto her without damaging her, and this is a decent, if not exploitable, way of leveling up weapon skills. This was tested with melee weapons, not bows/arrows. When finished, either "talk" to her, or use a spell to damage her, and she will register to your allies, who will attempt to kill her. She will take damage from spells and possibly weapons with damaging enchantments only, or will teleport again, which starts the process over. She will never recover from her paralysis.
- Casting Dead Thrall on The Caller, and later attacking her in an attempt to remove the follower, may cause her to teleport to an undetermined location. If this occurs, you may not be able to get rid of her as a Summoned Thrall (regardless if you have two other conjured followers), and as such people will always act as if you have an active zombie follower.
  - It is possible that The Caller may have teleported back to Fellglow Keep where you first encountered her. If so, returning there and summoning another creature will dismiss her.
- Casting Dead Thrall on The Caller after killing her, and picking up a book from the pedestals, will cause her to become hostile to you. **?**
- The Caller can survive melee finishing moves if she teleports when they are triggered, even decapitations (she will continue to fight and cast spells despite being headless).
- The game client freezes if you [sneak attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak#Sneak_Attacks "Skyrim:Sneak") The Caller with a ranged attack and kill her too quickly, due to how the fight is scripted.
  - The risk of this happening can be reduced by avoiding using a sneak attack, as well as using less powerful weaponry and/or spells. Be sure to save prior to initiating combat.

# Skyrim:The Cause (quest)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project"). |  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Investigate the activities of the [Mythic Dawn](/wiki/Lore:Mythic_Dawn "Lore:Mythic Dawn") cult.** |

|  |  |

The Mythic Dawn are seeking a Great Welkynd Stone

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Await news from a courier.
2. Read *[Stranger's Plea](/wiki/Skyrim:Stranger%27s_Plea "Skyrim:Stranger's Plea")*.
3. Go to the Shrine of Stendarr.
4. Defeat the two [Mythic Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Mythic_Dawn "Skyrim:Mythic Dawn") assassins.
5. Read *[Skorvild's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Skorvild%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Skorvild's Journal")* and *[Mythic Dawn Orders](/wiki/Skyrim:Mythic_Dawn_Orders "Skyrim:Mythic Dawn Orders")*.
6. Search for clues in the [Mythic Dawn Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Mythic_Dawn_Camp "Skyrim:Mythic Dawn Camp").
7. Search [Rielle](/wiki/Skyrim:Rielle "Skyrim:Rielle").
8. Read *[Janus' Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Janus%27_Journal "Skyrim:Janus' Journal")*.
9. Retrieve the four [Ayleid Elemental Shards](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause_Items#Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:The Cause Items").
10. Locate the Ayleid Elemental Shard Holders and place the Ayleid Elemental Shards.
11. Take the [Great Welkynd Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Welkynd_Stone "Skyrim:Great Welkynd Stone").
12. Kill [Norion the Undying](/wiki/Skyrim:Norion_the_Undying "Skyrim:Norion the Undying").
13. Read the *[Vigilant Enforcer's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_Enforcer%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Vigilant Enforcer's Journal")*.
14. Locate the Oblivion Gate.
15. (Optional) Wear a set of Mythic Dawn robes.
16. Defeat [Vonos](/wiki/Skyrim:Vonos "Skyrim:Vonos").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Ambush at the shrine

The Mythic Dawn camp

This quest will start once you reach level 46. (but actually get to level 46 don’t cheat levels. This will make the quest nearly impossible.) A courier delivers the *[Stranger's Plea](/wiki/Skyrim:Stranger%27s_Plea "Skyrim:Stranger's Plea")* to you to read. It is a request to meet from Skorvild, an ex-Mythic Dawn cultist who turned away from the cult and needs help stopping their next nefarious plan.

Travel to [the Two Pillars](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Stendarr#The_Two_Pillars "Skyrim:Shrine of Stendarr"), which is near the center of Whiterun Hold's tundra, south of Swindler's Den and northeast of Broken Fang Cave. It is close to and within sight of the Shrine of Zenithar to the west.

Sadly for Skorvild, his former cult-mates will catch up with him before he can speak with you. Once you arrive at the shrine you will spot the body of [Skorvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Skorvild "Skyrim:Skorvild"), and two Mythic Dawn assassins will attack you. Once you have killed the assassins, loot their bodies for the *[Mythic Dawn Orders](/wiki/Skyrim:Mythic_Dawn_Orders "Skyrim:Mythic Dawn Orders")*, and then search Skorvild for his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Skorvild%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Skorvild's Journal").

You will then need to head to the Mythic Dawn Camp to investigate. The camp itself is found north of the [Alchemist's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemist%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Alchemist's Shack"). The camp has three hostile [Mythic Dawn explorers](/wiki/Skyrim:Mythic_Dawn_Explorer "Skyrim:Mythic Dawn Explorer"). Once they are dispatched you can pick up the *[Excavation Leader's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Excavation_Leader%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Excavation Leader's Journal")*. The journal explains that the Mythic Dawn are attempting to reopen an Oblivion gate, and have been excavating across the valley to the south in the Jerall Mountains for a powerful artifact that will help them do it.

### Varlais Cavern and Rielle

Vanus and the other dead Mythic Dawn

Travel to [Varlais Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Varlais_Cavern "Skyrim:Varlais Cavern"), which can be found south of [Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point"). As you enter the cavern, you will find an excavation site inside that has cracked open an entrance to the Ayleid ruins of [Rielle](/wiki/Skyrim:Rielle "Skyrim:Rielle"). There are [Ayleid casks](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Ayleid_Cask&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Ayleid Cask (page does not exist)") and [urns](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Ayleid_Urn&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Ayleid Urn (page does not exist)") that can be looted throughout the chambers. As you get deeper into the ruin, you will enter a large room with the corpses of cultists and the corpse of [Janus](/wiki/Skyrim:Janus "Skyrim:Janus"), there are [wights](/wiki/Skyrim:Wight "Skyrim:Wight") patrolling so be prepared for a fight.

After reading the journal, you will need to locate the elemental stones:

- [Elemental Shard - Wel](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause_Items#Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:The Cause Items"), found on the corpse of a Mythic Dawn Explorer
- [Elemental Shard - Sercen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause_Items#Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:The Cause Items"), carried by a Wight Lord
- [Elemental Shard - Nen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause_Items#Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:The Cause Items"), carried by a Wight Lord just before the door to [Rielle Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Rielle#Rielle_Crypt "Skyrim:Rielle")
- [Elemental Shard - Alata](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause_Items#Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:The Cause Items"), carried by a Wight Lord in Rielle Crypt

The shard holders

Once you have found all the shards, you will need to head deeper into the ruins to find the shard holders, take care to avoid the traps. When it comes to placing the elemental shards in the holders you need to place them in specific holders:

- Wel goes in the **North** holder
- Sercen goes in the **South** holder
- Nen goes in the **West** holder
- Alata goes in the **East** holder

Once you have placed the shards, a secret door will open and reveal a large room with a [Great Welkynd Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Welkynd_Stone "Skyrim:Great Welkynd Stone"). Take the stone and [Norion the Undying](/wiki/Skyrim:Norion_the_Undying "Skyrim:Norion the Undying"), an [Ayleid Lich](/wiki/Skyrim:Ayleid_Lich "Skyrim:Ayleid Lich") with as much power as a [Dragon Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest"), will burst out of his coffin. Beware his minions, including two [Wight](/wiki/Skyrim:Wight "Skyrim:Wight") archers who sleep in the coffins upstairs on either side of the room. Once Norion is killed you can search his body for the [Staff of Ehlno Ede](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ehlno_Ede "Skyrim:Staff of Ehlno Ede") and the [Rielle key](/wiki/Skyrim:Rielle_Key "Skyrim:Rielle Key"). You will be directed to defeat Norion once you take the Great Welkynd Stone even if you have already noticed Norion and woke him with a rune spell to defeat him early.

Go back to the room where you placed the four stones. At the south part of that room there is a small dead-end room where you can find a switch that opens the way out.

Head back into the main area of Rielle, where you will see Vigilants of Stendarr (including Vigil Enforcers if the [Vigil Enforcer Armor Set](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Enforcer_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Vigil Enforcer Armor Set") Creation has been installed) fighting with Mythic Dawn agents. You can aid the Vigilants against the Mythic Dawn. Once you get back to the entrance of Rielle, there is a corpse of a Vigil Enforcer that has a [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_Enforcer%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Vigilant Enforcer's Journal"), read the journal and you will find out that the location of the Oblivion gate is in [Red Scar Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Scar_Cavern "Skyrim:Red Scar Cavern").
Note: If you choose to wear Mythic Dawn Robes while exiting Rielle, the Vigilants outside will mistake you for a Mythic Dawn member and attack. If you do not wear the robes, they will let you pass.

### Red Scar Cavern

Vonos

There is a Mythic Dawn Guard outside of the cavern that can be tricked if you wear a set of Mythic Dawn robes, if you wish to avoid fighting. This will also work on the cultists inside. Continue through the cavern and you will eventually reach a door to the [Mythic Dawn Temple](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Mythic_Dawn_Temple&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Mythic Dawn Temple (page does not exist)"). Once inside the temple, you will see an inactive Oblivion gate, you will then have to kill [Vonos](/wiki/Skyrim:Vonos "Skyrim:Vonos"). Once you kill him however, the Oblivion gate will open, the quest will finish and [The Consequences](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Consequences "Skyrim:The Consequences") will begin.

## Bugs

- The quest may start the first time you get a courier.
- Norion the Undying may be triggered before you take the Great Welkynd Stone, which allows you to kill him and prevents moving forward past objective 150. Bug confirmed on [Switch](/wiki/Skyrim:Switch "Skyrim:Switch") Anniversary Edition. **?**
  -  On Switch, grab the stone in sneak mode before attacking Norion. When you need to read the journal, read it while looting the corpse.
  - Either revert to a previous save or reset to a previous stage.
  - Save before you enter Rielle Crypt; if you see the Wight Lord near the entrance and not *waiting* to wake up when you approach, you have triggered the bug.
- If you leave the second area of Rielle or Rielle altogether without finishing the quest, the pressure plates in the floor won't activate for the Ayleid doors to slide open.
  - Solution to above: Use the console command `tcl` on PC to walk through the gate, then use it again to turn collisions back on. A button to raise the gates is found inside the main room. Your followers, if any, will now be able to accompany you to fight against Norion and the other enemies.
  - On console, use two platters (one for each gate) and Whirlwind Sprint/Sprint to clip through the gates. Hold the platter to slightly above waist height (press and hold the interact button to move objects) to be flush with the gate, and then use Whirlwind Sprint. The platter will not phase through the gate with you and you can not pick it up from the other side, so if you do this with only one platter you will become stuck in the middle of the two locked gates indefinitely.
- Attempting to read the Excavation Leader's Journal causes a CTD and in addition the entrance to Rielle appears to be missing if you go to the location to skip reading the journal.
- Varlais Cavern marked as completed on the map before entering and clearing the instance. Cavern entrance also not visible at the location. **?**
- If you don't read the Janus journal before reaching the Great Welkynd Stone, the stone might not be an object you can take when you find it, blocking the final stages. **?**
- If before you take the Great Welkynd Stone, you trigger Niron's attacking by casting a rune spell on his crypt or attacking one of the wights in the open coffins, then after you defeat Norion and take the Great Welkynd Stone, the objective to defeat Norion will reappear and it will be impossible to remove from your journal until the quest has been completed by killing Vonos.
- The door to enter the Rielle Crypt as well as the option to open the gate behind will not show an option to enter or open. **?**
  - Solution to above: Deleting the Skyrim-Patch.bsa file from the Skyrim Special Edition\Data folder corrects the issue.
- The cave entrance may glitch with a large boulder in its place, typical of vanilla. The Mythic Dawn guard will hover inside the rock face and may emerge to fight. **?**
  - Solution to above: use the console command `tcl` on PC which allows you to disable collisions, retype it to to reactivate collisions
- It is possible to enter Red Scar Cavern and kill Vonos before initiating the quest. By heading to the back of the cavern with the un-interactable door and inspecting the door's handle, a prompt to open it may appear. This will take the player to the room with Vonos and the gate, where killing him will immediately begin [The Consequences](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Consequences "Skyrim:The Consequences"). The Oblivion Gate will remain open when the quest is begun, but the player may not be able to proceed with the quest as the oblivion gate cannot be interacted with.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE067_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE067_Quest`.

# Skyrim:The Chief of Thirsk Hall

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), checked by [Roger](/wiki/User:Roger "User:Roger") |
