[Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to the [Riekling Chief](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Chief "Skyrim:Riekling Chief").
2. Lure [Bilgemuck](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilgemuck "Skyrim:Bilgemuck") back to [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall").
3. Bring ten [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") to the chief.
4. Kill the [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord").
5. Speak to the chief, and defend yourself.

### Thirsk Mead Hall

The legendary [Thirsk](/wiki/Lore:Thirsk "Lore:Thirsk") Mead Hall has a long, violent history and is over 300 years of age, although rumors claim it to be closer to 700. Founded in the [Third Era](/wiki/Lore:Third_Era "Lore:Third Era") by [Hrothmund the Red](/wiki/Lore:Hrothmund_the_Red "Lore:Hrothmund the Red") of the [Skaal](/wiki/Lore:Skaal "Lore:Skaal"), the hall was initially built for [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") warriors who wished to live and fight in the wilderness, the old way. Numerous legends of heroic acts surround the hall, but also stories about the chieftains getting killed by their successors. In true Nord tradition, the mead hall was also about downing [mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") around the clock and telling old tales. In the Fourth Era, the comforts of the mead hall had made the residing warriors too lazy, and, as a result, the hall was an easy target for a group of invading [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling") who overwhelmed the warriors and exiled them to a snowy camp south of their former home.

### The Riekling Chief

*"You strong. Help tribe-kin."*

When you pay [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall") a visit, you will find rieklings gathered outside the entrance, with one of them actively seeking you out. For reasons unknown, the riekling can speak a little bit, saying: *"You. Fol. Low. Me."* You can ask him a few questions, but it turns out he only knows that one line. Follow him into the mead hall, where the interior reflects the presence of the disorganized rieklings, with chairs turned over, bones scattered around, and several tents put up in the corners. You will be led to the [Riekling Chief](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Chief "Skyrim:Riekling Chief") who sits in his throne, saying: *"You strong. Help tribe-kin."* You can then choose from three different options, although the chief is not exactly well-spoken:

:   **Where did you live before you were here?**
:   *"Tribe-kin live all places. All of world within great water."*
:   **Who are you?**
:   *"You. You strong. Help tribe-kin."*
:   **Why did you take over Thirsk?**
:   *"Hot fire. Cold dizzydrink. Happy tribe."*

The middle option is the only one that will get you anywhere, and will provide two more options. Choose the 'what is going on here' option and he will respond: *"We family. We strong, you stronger."* At this point you can back out, or you can suggest that he may be asking for help. The latter will make him explain: *"Bilgemuck run. Prize beast, run. Fool tribe-kin, chase away. Bilgemuck fear. You bring, he follow you. Yes?"* The Chief will then keep you guessing, but it turns out [Bilgemuck](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilgemuck "Skyrim:Bilgemuck") is a prize beast as he will repeat: *"Bilgemuck prize beast. You find, he follow. Bilgemuck love meat. Give meat, he follow. You go."*

### Bilgemuck

[Bilgemuck](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilgemuck "Skyrim:Bilgemuck")

As instructed, find yourself a piece of meat and locate Bilgemuck, a named [bristleback](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback "Skyrim:Bristleback") that hides on the other side of the lake from the hall. When you locate Bilgemuck, he will greet you with a **snort** but will be peaceful and await your next action. He will accept many types of meat including [clam meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat"), [dog meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog_Meat "Skyrim:Dog Meat"), [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat"), and [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), but excluding [boar meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boar_Meat "Skyrim:Boar Meat"), [crab meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Crab_Meat "Skyrim:Crab Meat"), [nix-hound meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound_Meat "Skyrim:Nix-Hound Meat")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound "Skyrim:Nix-Hound"), [ash hopper meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Hopper_Meat "Skyrim:Ash Hopper Meat"), and [human flesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Flesh "Skyrim:Human Flesh"). Once he's finished eating, he will readily follow you back to the hall and find his spot in the pen behind the house. Enter the mead hall for yet another encounter with the demanding chief: *"Bilgemuck follow you. Bilgemuck know strength. Tribe-kin stronger. You stay, help more."*

### Redgrass

For your next task to strengthen the tribe, the chief wants you to gather plants, saying: *"Tribe-kin missing redgrass. Need for godspeak dance. You bring redgrass, we dance."* When you ask him to translate, the chief will show you a sample of [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw"), the reddish plant growing all over Solstheim: *"Here, like this. Go, bring two hands of redgrass. Be friend of tribe-kin."* After a quick farewell dance he will return to his throne and await your return. Scathecraw is one of the most common plants and it is quite easy to gather ten samples from [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"), where they can be picked from all over the main road, all the way down to the field behind [Ienth Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ienth_Farm "Skyrim:Ienth Farm"), which is full of them. You will not receive a quest update so once you have ten, return to the chief who will comment: *"Good redgrass. Later, we burn. Now, final task."*

### Kill the Nords

For the final task, the Riekling Chief has something very specific in mind, and far more serious than the previous tasks: *"Bad Nords. Say Thirsk theirs. Live by water, bother tribe-kin. We fight. You strong. You help. No more bad Nords."* When asked if he wants you to commit murder, the response will be: *"Bad people. They come, fight us. We fight back now."*

**NOTE**: At this point, it is still possible to abandon the quest and instead help the former inhabitants reclaim Thirsk Mead Hall. Choose the dialogue option *"I'm not sure about this"* and leave the building. Head to [Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat") and speak to [Bujold the Unworthy](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold_the_Unworthy "Skyrim:Bujold the Unworthy"). Agreeing to help her will fail this quest and instead start [Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk"). Otherwise, continue the walkthrough below.

As soon as you agree to help the Rieklings, the Chief will jump down from his throne and rush out to the front door. When you come outside, the rest of the rieklings will be gathered and ready to fight, and the chief will prepare them for battle:
**Chief**: *"Froo ha cawasy jo la. Karoo taray pelfrik?"*
**All**: *"Hawah!"*
**Chief**: *"Felgir paw tuwani barj. Goora! Goora! Goora!"*
**All**: *"Goora!"*

*"Stab and run! The tribe-kin way."*

With the soldiers prepped for fight, the chief will lead them in an eastern direction towards the hiding place of the mead hall's former inhabitants, [Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat"). You can choose to run ahead and take care of the Nords yourself, let the rieklings help you with the battle, or let the rieklings do all the fighting (they will dispatch the Nords).

### The Tribe-Kin Way

After all of the Nords at the camp are dead, the riekling soldiers will begin to walk back to the mead hall while the chief turns on you, convinced you will take over his spot on the throne and become the new chief: *"You strong! All tribe-kin stronger with you. But... maybe you too strong. Too strong, want be chief."* This leaves you no choice but to fight the hostile chief. If the other rieklings are nearby, they will attack the chief, or if they have returned to the mead hall, you can lead the chief back to them and they will attack him. Note that the rieklings can injure the chief only to the point that he will drop to one knee; it falls to you to deal the killing blow. Ending this quest allows you to have a riekling as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers#Dragonborn_Creatures "Skyrim:Followers"). A group of up to three rieklings may now also occasionally show up to aid you during random fights, be it on Solstheim or in Skyrim.

## Notes

- The number of Nords living in the camp will be either five or seven, as [Herkja](/wiki/Skyrim:Herkja "Skyrim:Herkja") and [Sirkjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Sirkjorg "Skyrim:Sirkjorg") will be working around the clock at the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak") until you have completed [At the Summit of Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha").
- This quest will make you kill the quest giver for [Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk"), so you can only do one or the other.
- Killing [Elmus](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus "Skyrim:Elmus") will silently remove [Elmus Favor Quest (mead)](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus_Favor_Quest_(mead) "Skyrim:Elmus Favor Quest (mead)") from your journal if you have started, but have not completed it.
- If you first bring Bilgemuck back to the Rieklings and then later turn on them, Bilgemuck is stuck hanging around the mead hall.

## Bugs

-  On [Switch](/wiki/Skyrim:Switch "Skyrim:Switch"), the journal may say that you've only killed five Nords, even if you've killed all seven. This leaves the quest impossible to be finished.
- Occasionally after killing the chief, rieklings still won't be available as followers.
  - Despite the rieklings not taking up the humanoid follower slot, this bug may be circumvented by dismissing your humanoid follower and recruiting them again after recruiting the riekling.
  - Try going into Thirsk Mead Hall and interacting with a riekling after defeating the Chief. You should get dialogue for it to follow you. Oddly enough, there is only one dialogue option which automatically has it follow you, so try backing out of the dialogue with the cancel button if you decide to not have it follow you, or just immediately dismiss it.
- Conversely, after killing the chief, one to three riekling warriors may randomly appear in any given location, even though they're not following you. They may or may not have the dialogue option to follow you from that point if you wish.
- If you choose "Let's go!" when the chief asks you to kill the Nords, the quest objectives do not update, still indicating that you need to gather 10 scathecraw, even though the chief runs off to battle.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
  - Tell the chief you're unsure first, then talk to him again and say "Let's go!"
  - Make sure you've collected the 10 scathecraw first, *before* he asks for them. Once he asks for them, agree and keep the dialogue box open. Then select the new option that you have all of them. Once the option to attack the Nord is available, select it. Once the Chief is outside the hall and finishes his short speech to the other rieklings, it should update on-screen that the 10 scathecraw have been collected, then immediately update with the objective to attack the Nord camp and kill the members of the Nord camp as soon as he starts heading there.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2MH02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2MH02`.

# Skyrim:The Chill

## Overview

|  |  |  |

Entrance to the Chill

**The Chill** is the [jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Jails "Skyrim:Jails") for [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), located on an island north-northeast of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") and northeast of [Septimus Signus's Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus%27s_Outpost "Skyrim:Septimus Signus's Outpost"), across the sea.

If you are arrested by a [Winterhold guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Guard "Skyrim:Winterhold Guard") and sent to jail, you will be imprisoned here.
The location of The Chill [is not marked on the map](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places "Skyrim:Unmarked Places"); consequently, it cannot be selected as a destination for fast travel. There is only one zone, *[The Chill](#The_Chill)*.

### Exterior

The Chill is located on a mineral-rich island, with the [ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") listed below. The island is inhabited by several leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") in addition to a few [horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker"), which can include [snow bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear "Skyrim:Snow Bear"), [snowy sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowy_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Snowy Sabre Cat"), and [ice wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf "Skyrim:Ice Wolf"). One of the animals is normally found near the corundum ore vein to the northwest, and another is normally found near the iron ore veins to the northeast. The leveled animals and horkers may end up fighting each other, resulting in the victors being found injured near the corpses of the defeated.

- Two [gold ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") among the rocks above The Chill (see [bugs](#Bugs)).
- One [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") to the southeast.
- Four [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"): three to the northeast, and one on the far southern tip.
- One [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") to the northwest.

### The Chill

Interior

The interior of the cave is guarded by a [frost atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Frost Atronach"). There are three cages with adept-level locks; each contains a bedroll. A further three small empty cages hang from the ceiling. There are lootable skeletal remains in two of the locked cages. The third cage is the one you are sent to, and has a lit lantern on the floor. There are also ten [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels in the cave.

If you are sent here, you will keep all of your equipment, including stolen items, making escaping the jail the easiest in Skyrim. Upon entering The Chill, regardless of whether you were jailed or entered of your own free will, the frost atronach inside and three others outside will all spawn. Upon exiting, the three aggressive frost atronachs outside will attack you on sight.

## Notes

- A map marker for The Chill was added by the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:USKP "Skyrim:USKP"), version 1.3.1.
- When arrested in Winterhold, if you choose to go to jail, the [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Guard "Skyrim:Winterhold Guard") will respond with *"Ha, enjoy the Chill."*
- If you escape from The Chill, you do not incur the 100 gold bounty that you would normally receive from escaping jails in other holds.
- All the containers in The Chill (which are only barrels) are [respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning"), and therefore unsafe to store items in.
- If entering The Chill by walking to the entrance without a bounty instead of being sent to jail, the Frost Atronachs will still be hostile.

## Bugs

- You may not be able to interact with some of the ore veins. **?**
  - Entering and exiting The Chill again may resolve this.
- When entering The Chill from the outside, the cage you would be put in if you were arrested in Winterhold may not spawn, leaving the door floating in space. **?**

## Maps

- 

  The Chill

# Skyrim:The Consequences

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project"). The portal

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Inspect [Vonos](/wiki/Skyrim:Vonos "Skyrim:Vonos")' corpse and retrieve his journal.
2. Read [Vonos' Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Vonos%27_Journal "Skyrim:Vonos' Journal").
3. Enter the Oblivion Gate.
4. Defeat [Valkyn Methats](/wiki/Skyrim:Valkyn_Methats "Skyrim:Valkyn Methats") and [Valkyn Gatanas](/wiki/Skyrim:Valkyn_Gatanas "Skyrim:Valkyn Gatanas") and gather [Torment](/wiki/Skyrim:Torment "Skyrim:Torment") and [Scourge](/wiki/Skyrim:Scourge "Skyrim:Scourge").
5. Return to [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim").
6. Escape [Red Scar Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Scar_Cavern "Skyrim:Red Scar Cavern").

## Detailed Walkthrough

The portal is open

While delivering the killing blow to the leader of the [Mythic Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Mythic_Dawn "Skyrim:Mythic Dawn"), Vonos, you feel something has gone wrong. His death has triggered the opening of the Oblivion Gate. Search his body to find his journal and read it to uncover the whole story and find you've been used to become the unwitting instrument of [Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Lore:Mehrunes_Dagon "Lore:Mehrunes Dagon"), resulting in the final opening of the gate. Enter the [Deadlands](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadlands "Skyrim:Deadlands") by the portal to put an end to all of this.

In the Deadlands, aside from a strange flora and Fire Atronachs, you'll come across two powerful [Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra") wielding equally powerful artifacts, [Valkyn Methats](/wiki/Skyrim:Valkyn_Methats "Skyrim:Valkyn Methats") carries [Torment](/wiki/Skyrim:Torment "Skyrim:Torment"), [Valkyn Gatanas](/wiki/Skyrim:Valkyn_Gatanas "Skyrim:Valkyn Gatanas") carries [Scourge](/wiki/Skyrim:Scourge "Skyrim:Scourge") and [Daedric Gauntlets of Negation](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause_Items#Daedric_Gauntlets_of_Negation "Skyrim:The Cause Items"). They can be found by taking either of two forks in the road where it spans the lava pools. Beware the Spiddal Sticks flanking the right-hand path where it crosses the lava, as the poison Spiddal gas is difficult to avoid here.

Kill Valkyn Gatanas and his [Daedric Horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Horse "Skyrim:Daedric Horse") (at the end of the left path) to retrieve Scourge. In one of the containers behind them is the Summon Daedric Horse spell tome.

Kill Valkyn Methats and his Flame Atronachs (found at the end of the right path, past the Spiddal Stick "gate") to retrieve Torment. This will put a stop to the invasion. Return to Tamriel and find a way out of Red Scar Cavern. This will complete the quest.

On your return to Tamriel, the Vigilants will be raiding the cavern and battling the Mythic Dawn a second time. If you attack either faction, they will become hostile.

## Notes

- After the quest is complete, the Oblivion Gate still remains open, allowing you to return and harvest the new flora. The surviving Vigilants will stay guarding the place to make sure nothing comes out or any Mythic Dawn comes back.

- After exiting the cavern, weight changes for no reason.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE067_Quest2 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE067_Quest2`.

# Skyrim:The Cure for Madness

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Confront the traitor among the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Gabriella](/wiki/Skyrim:Gabriella "Skyrim:Gabriella") |
| Location(s): | [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary") |
| Reward: | [Shadowmere](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmere "Skyrim:Shadowmere") [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") as a follower (if spared) |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =3 ([Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") if spared) |
| ID: | DB07 |
| Suggested Level: | 8 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security") | **Next →** [Recipe For Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security") | | → Next | [Recipe For Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster") | | |

Arnbjorn injured outside the Dawnstar Sanctuary

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid").
2. Find [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero")'s journal and take it to Astrid.
3. Behold Astrid's horse, [Shadowmere](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmere "Skyrim:Shadowmere").
4. Travel to the abandoned Brotherhood sanctuary outside [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").
5. Choose to either kill or spare Cicero.
6. Return to Astrid.

### Cicero

Cicero feigning injury deep inside the Dawnstar Sanctuary

When you return from completing the [Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security") contract, Gabriella will inform you that there was an incident with [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") and directs you to discuss it with Astrid.
Astrid reveals that Cicero attempted to murder her and the other members of the Dark Brotherhood, grievously wounding [Veezara](/wiki/Skyrim:Veezara "Skyrim:Veezara") in the process. [Arnbjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnbjorn "Skyrim:Arnbjorn") pursued Cicero as he fled from the sanctuary. She asks you to search Cicero's room for clues as to his whereabouts. Inside the room you find five [journals](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Cicero's Journal"), with the final journal indicating that Cicero might be headed for the long-abandoned [sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary") outside [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").
Astrid will grant you use of her horse, [Shadowmere](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmere "Skyrim:Shadowmere"). Immediately outside the sanctuary he will rise from the black, bubbling liquid. Mount him if you wish, and head to Dawnstar's abandoned Brotherhood sanctuary.

### Dawnstar Sanctuary

You will find an injured Arnbjorn outside the sanctuary. He reveals that he and Cicero seriously wounded each other before Cicero escaped into the safety of the sanctuary and instructs you to *"just follow the blood"*.
A pass phrase is needed to enter the sanctuary; it can be found in the final volume of Cicero's journal (*"Innocence, my brother"*).
Once inside, Cicero will begin to speak to you, taunting, as you search for him.
At this point, summon [Lucien Lachance](/wiki/Skyrim:Spectral_Assassin "Skyrim:Spectral Assassin") for a bit more on the story. He strongly suggests that the [Dread Father](/wiki/Lore:Sithis "Lore:Sithis") would not want you to kill Cicero.
While the sanctuary is abandoned, it is not unoccupied. It is inhabited by [ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanctuary_Guardian "Skyrim:Sanctuary Guardian") of the previous Dark Brotherhood residents, who will attack on sight. The elusive [Udefrykte](/wiki/Skyrim:Udefrykte "Skyrim:Udefrykte") also resides in one of the sanctuary's caves; it may be advisable to simply sneak by the troll when discovered.
As you make your way along, the second room is a circular chamber with another room below and a bridge. The spike trap can be avoided by avoiding the bridge and crawling along the left-hand wall; there is enough of a ledge to allow this.
Across the bridge at the foot of the stairs, you will find two skill books: *[Fire and Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_and_Darkness "Skyrim:Fire and Darkness")* and *[The Marksmanship Lesson](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Marksmanship_Lesson "Skyrim:The Marksmanship Lesson")*.

### Keeper of The Old Ways

At the end, you will find Cicero curled up in a fetal position, apparently injured. Cicero cautions you that the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") will not be happy if you kill him. At this point it is your choice whether to kill him or not. If you attack him he leaps to his feet, obviously unhurt, and gleefully screams *"Haha! Behold the final trick of the Fool of Hearts! You think me near death? Haha! Think again."*
If you decide not to kill him, he returns to serve and tend to the Night Mother after you complete [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!"). He will also be a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers").
Whatever your decision, the quest is now complete. Speak to Astrid to begin your next mission.

## Notes

- If you spare Cicero by leaving the Sanctuary, and then immediately re-enter, Cicero will already have disappeared.
- The quest objective to "Behold Shadowmere" is numbered 666.

## Bugs

|  |
| --- |
| **To meet our site's higher standard of quality, this article or section may require cleanup.**  **The user who placed this here had the following concern:** needs another cleanup, or at least a few confirmed bugs To leave a message about the cleanup for this article, please add it to this article's [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:The_Cure_for_Madness). |

- If you raise Cicero from the dead before you report back to Astrid, she won't talk and you will never be able to finish the quest even if you kill your Cicero zombie. Cicero's armor will respawn on your Cicero zombie every time you go through a loading screen, meaning you can loot an infinite set of Cicero's armor.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- After you finish the quest, the blood outside of the Dawnstar Sanctuary is never cleaned up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes, when you come back after completing the Breaching Security quest, Astrid will only say *"You're back. Good. You'll want to hear this."*
- If you attempt to pickpocket Cicero while he is lying on the floor and you fail, he will get up and start attacking you.
- Sometimes, on Special Edition (might be Xbox only), if one of the Sanctuary Guardians walks over the tripwire that drops fire pots onto the oil (even though they can't actually trigger the tripwire), the game will freeze indefinitely. **?**
- Sometimes, on Special Edition (might be Xbox only), if you fast travel back to the Falkreath Sanctuary, the black door will have despawned. You can walk through where it would be, but nothing is behind it but rocks. Fast traveling far enough out for a cell reset then fast traveling back in may fix this, but it might take a few tries. **?**
- If you strike Cicero while he is saying *"Do what you will... In the end, Sithis will judge us both"*, he will start to jump up and attack you, but then lay back down to finish his sentence, and will stay there after he finishes talking. **?**
- If you attack Cicero with Lightning Bolt, he will stand up when shocked, then lie back down again, repeating this each time you shock him. He will not attack you, even after he says *"Haha! Behold the final trick of the Fool of Hearts! You think me near death? Haha! Think again."*
  - This also appears to work with a crossbow[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard").
- There is a glitch where the barred door outside Cicero's chamber will open and still show the barred door message. If you walk up to it and jump onto the bar you can skip Udefrykte.
- If you have a follower with you and you enter the tomb, he or she will not follow you once inside or once you leave. You may have to reenter the sanctuary if your follower does not follow you out. Once you enter, your follower will follow you once again. **?**
- On rare occasions, you will hear the animation and see the bubbles, yet Shadowmere will not appear.
  - To fix this, load to a previous save, or during [Death Incarnate](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate"), coax enemies near the pool to lure Shadowmere out via his aggressiveness. You can also try fast traveling to all the stables until you see Shadowmere for a split second afterwards, and then fast travel back to the sanctuary's pool to see if he has been untrapped.
  -  Open the console and enter `prid 0009ccd8` followed by `enable` and then `moveto player` and Shadowmere should appear in the pool as normal
- Cicero's journals may fail to load when entering the sanctuary. **?**
  - Reloading an earlier save may fix this.
- Cicero does not leave the Falkreath Sanctuary before you enter and will stand in his room with only one dialogue option to tell you about himself. **?**
  - If Gabriella does not meet you at the entrance walk out and walk back into the Sanctuary.
- If there is a hostile creature near the sanctuary, Arnbjorn may make a spontaneous recovery and try to participate in the combat. He will return to his expected position afterwards. **?**
- Cicero can start attacking without any dialogue options upon entering last room. To fix this, use console command `tdetect` until the end of the conversation.
- If you save before talking to Arnbjorn outside the Dawnstar Sanctuary, loot all the animal corpses in Udefrykte's lair, and then reload, the animal corpses may be empty even though you're reloading from a save before you entered the sanctuary. **?**
- While killing the ghosts under the bridge, there is a ghost that can be pickpocketed for a bow and a large amount of arrows. **?**
- It is possible to pick up the weapons used by the ghosts, but they are difficult to find and disappear very quickly. The weapons are dropped in the same manner as any other NPC's weapon when killed. Since you only have a couple of seconds, it may be easier to tap the action button repeatedly and follow the weapon as it falls out of the ghost's hand. **?**
- With the [Perfect Touch](/wiki/Skyrim:Perfect_Touch "Skyrim:Perfect Touch") perk, sets of [Shrouded Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Shrouded Armor") can be pickpocketed from the Sanctuary Guardians. **?**
-  Beheading Cicero can cause his hood to stay attached to his body instead of his head. **?**

## Quest Stages

| 200 | ☑ | After learning that Cicero went berserk and tried to kill Astrid, I was ordered to go to the Dawnstar Sanctuary, find him, and end his life. The matter has now been resolved. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 20:* Locate Arnbjorn |

# Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe

## Overview

| --- |

| Required Level: | 9 |
| Suggested Level: | 32 |
| Difficulty: | Medium |

*"Yamarz was a coward and a weakling."*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. (Optional) Hear rumors that something is happening in [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur").
2. Help the [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") of Largashbur repel a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") attack.
3. Speak to [Atub](/wiki/Skyrim:Atub "Skyrim:Atub").
4. Bring a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat") and a [daedra heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") to Atub.
5. Observe Atub's ritual.
6. Speak with [Chief Yamarz](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Yamarz "Skyrim:Chief Yamarz").
7. Meet Yamarz at [Fallowstone Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Fallowstone_Cave "Skyrim:Fallowstone Cave").
8. Protect Yamarz as he journeys to the [Giant's Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Grove "Skyrim:Giant's Grove").
9. Defeat the giant.
10. Take [Shagrol's Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Shagrol%27s_Warhammer "Skyrim:Shagrol's Warhammer") back to Largashbur.
11. Place Shagrol's Hammer on the shrine in Largashbur.
12. Collect your [reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Volendrung "Skyrim:Volendrung").

### Giant Attack

A giant attacking the Orcs at Largashbur

The [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") camp is located in [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") southwest of Riften. As you approach the town for the first time, a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") will be actively attacking the Orcs at the gate. It's advisable to hurry in and help distract the giant, as it will kill unnamed Orcs left and right and may kill potential followers such as [Ugor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ugor "Skyrim:Ugor"). After defeating the giant, Ugor and a caster named [Atub](/wiki/Skyrim:Atub "Skyrim:Atub") will begin bickering. Atub will apologize to you and explain that their tribe and leader have been cursed. She has a ritual that may be able to remove it, but needs a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat") and a [daedra heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") to perform it. She'll ask you to retrieve them. Details on where to find them are provided on their individual pages, however the closest place to get both items is in the Jorrvaskr Living Quarters in Whiterun.

### Malacath's Ritual

*"Now, we begin the ritual..."*

After you bring the ingredients to Atub, she will enter [Largashbur Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Longhouse "Skyrim:Largashbur Longhouse") and speak with [Chief Yamarz](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Yamarz "Skyrim:Chief Yamarz") about performing the ritual. The Chief isn't thrilled about the ritual, but ultimately agrees to follow her out to the altar. Atub successfully reaches [Malacath](/wiki/Skyrim:Malacath "Skyrim:Malacath"), whose disembodied voice berates Yamarz for his weakness, abhorring Yamarz for being so weak that even giants openly attack his stronghold. Malacath demands that he kill the giant's leader and return with his club as an offering. Yamarz is irked and demands your assistance in his task, promising lots of gold for helping him.

### Hammer Time

*"I'll lead the way, but you'd better back me up."*

Yamarz will run off towards [Fallowstone Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Fallowstone_Cave "Skyrim:Fallowstone Cave"). If you fast travel there you'll meet him at the entrance and avoid the long trek. He leads the way through the cave, which is remarkably spacious, but rather straightforward. [Bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") and [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll") dwell in the cave and pose some threat, but the giant in the huge main chamber should be far enough away to be avoided entirely. Yamarz will charge down several ledges following the flow of a stream to a pool on the lowest level. He will continue to follow the stream deeper into the cave out of the main chamber and into a smaller cavern occupied by a second giant that can't be so easily avoided. Continue down the tunnel to the southeast as it wends its way around to a final small chamber littered with bones, likely from the predation of the two bears that make it their home. After dealing with them, follow the quest marker up the path to the left and out to [Giant's Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Grove "Skyrim:Giant's Grove").

### Yamarz's Fork

Once in the grove, Yamarz will offer to pay you even more gold if you kill the giant yourself and let him take credit. Either way, you're left fighting the giant in a very small area.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| "Of course, I can't let you leave here alive. Wouldn't want anyone finding out."  **Help Yamarz** If you agree, or if you just kill the giant on your own, he will betray you afterwards, saying that no one can ever know the truth of what happened here. He is extremely well-armored and has tremendous blocking ability, but doesn't hit hard. After killing him, Malacath will praise you for removing both the giant and the conniving, weakling chief. He asks you to take [Shagrol's Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Shagrol%27s_Warhammer "Skyrim:Shagrol's Warhammer") back to Largashbur and whip the other Orcs back into shape. | "This should only take a second."  **Honor Malacath's Wishes** If you persuade Yamarz to perform his duty, he'll be killed almost immediately by the giant and you'll be left to kill the giant anyway. Malacath will again deride the fallen weakling Chief and send you back to Largashbur. |

After defeating the giant, the only way out is back via Fallowstone - only this time you get to the entrance via a long ledge. Just after you enter back into the cave, take the tunnel almost immediately to your left, and follow the ledge round to the left, past the locked chest (unlock and loot, if you've not done so already). Keep going until you see the waterfall ahead of you, then jump down and cross the stream just in front of the waterfall, then follow the route back to the cave entrance.

### Claiming Volendrung

A gift from Malacath

Once you return, speak with Atub and tell her of Yamarz's fate. Malacath will speak once more, naming [Gularzob](/wiki/Skyrim:Gularzob "Skyrim:Gularzob") the new chief. He will command you to place Shagrol's Hammer on the shrine, where it transforms into the fearsome [Volendrung](/wiki/Skyrim:Volendrung "Skyrim:Volendrung"), the Hammer of Might. Make sure you take it from the shrine where it rests in the skull's antlers.

## Notes

- Quest stage 10 is never set. It suggests this quest could have originally been started by getting a rumor, but no such rumor exists in the final game or its files.
- Unused dialogue for Atub and Yamarz suggests a slightly different start to this quest, with Atub sending you to speak with Yamarz, and him sending you to an unknown location known as "Malacath's Shrine". Only after conversing with Malacath there, would Atub perform a ritual at the stronghold, which likely would have resulted in the final task for Yamarz, although what this would've entailed is unknown, although it seems likely that the quest from there on would remain the same. An unused talking activator internally known as `DA06Shrine` seems to be the only remnant of this shrine.
- After you finish the quest, you can recruit [Lob](/wiki/Skyrim:Lob "Skyrim:Lob"), [Ogol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogol "Skyrim:Ogol"), and [Ugor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ugor "Skyrim:Ugor") as followers. Be warned, however, that they can die even before you arrive and can die after you finish the quest (see bugs).
- After you complete this quest, you will become [Blood-Kin](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin "Skyrim:Blood-Kin") to the Orcs if you were not already.
- If you leave the area without picking up Volendrung, it will be lying on the ground behind the altar upon your return.
- You will need to level up via skill increases to or beyond level 9 for the quest to be eligible to start. You cannot use console commands to get an arbitrarily high level and start the quest.
- Yamarz's quick death against the giant appears [scripted](/wiki/Skyrim:Scripted_Deaths "Skyrim:Scripted Deaths"), and only happens if you *don't* say you'll fight the giant yourself. If you say you'll fight the giant, but then get Yamarz involved in the fight afterwards, he will have his normal Health and can be used as a decoy of sorts.
- Fallowstone Cave can be visited and cleared prior to this quest. However, accepting this quest turns it into a giant-themed zone.
- You cannot fast travel directly from Giant's Grove back to Largashbur. You must manually backtrack through Fallowstone Cave via the main entrance. You can fast travel once you exit.

## Bugs

- Triggering combat in Largashbur can block quest progression.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- Even after completing this quest and gaining Malacath's forgiveness for the tribe and ridding them of the curse, giants will still attack them after enough time has passed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
- Atub and Garakh were apparently intended to be merchants after the quest (apothecary and blacksmith respectively), but do not function as merchants themselves.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, addresses this issue. They were assigned the wrong settings. Once fixed, they will be affected by [Master Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Trader "Skyrim:Master Trader"), but not [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor").
- Upon arriving at Largashbur, the giant may be attacking but the gate may be closed and locked. Ugor may also have been killed by the giants.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
  - To get around this, proceed west from the gate along the stronghold's wall and turn left at the end. You can jump over the wall from the slanted support poles between the wall and the adjacent rocky mountain base. The NPCs will then behave as if the gate had been unlocked. Speak to Atub to initiate the quest. She is usually located atop the guard tower next to the gate.
  - If you arrive at Largashbur before level 9, the giant will not be attacking. If you then fast travel there later with a follower, ready to fight the giant, you may be able to save Ugor if you kill the giant fast enough.
- Sometimes if you tell Yamarz to kill the giant, the giant will not respond to Yamarz's attacks and will be killed. When you talk to Yamarz he will behave as though you killed the giant for him and attack you. When you strike back he will die instantly.
  -  If you notice this happening before the giant dies, use the [Console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and select the giant, then type `disable`, hit Enter, then type `enable`. This should reset the giant and get him to attack.
- It is possible to complete the quest without Yamarz dying by killing the giant yourself and using a [Pacify](/wiki/Skyrim:Pacify_(effect) "Skyrim:Pacify (effect)") effect on Yamarz on your way back to Largashbur. The objective for protecting Yamarz remains marked as incomplete, but the quest will still complete. The pacified Yamarz will continue his normal routine at his longhouse. However, every time you revisit the stronghold, you will have to pacify him as he will turn hostile.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, addresses this issue. Yamarz has been made immune to Pacify effects.
- If [Gularzob](/wiki/Skyrim:Gularzob "Skyrim:Gularzob") is killed before the quest ends, Malacath will still name him the new chief as if he was alive.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, addresses this issue. He is essential until after completing the quest.
- If you kill the giant without making a deal with Yamarz, Malacath will incorrectly say that the giant took care of Yamarz.

  **Mod Notes**: The check is only if Stage 100 is completed, which only occurs if you actually make a deal with Yamarz.
- If you kill the giant and Yamarz, Malacath may say that *"Giants took care of Yamarz"*, and if you allow the giant to kill Yamarz, Malacath may say that you took care of both "giants" and Yamarz.
- After placing Shagrol's Hammer on the shrine, Volendrung may not appear. Try loading a previous save and attempting again.
- It seems that transforming into a werewolf renders you unable to transform back while in Giant's Grove, which can make the fight against the giant (and potentially Yamarz as well) much more difficult. Once you leave Giant's Grove, you can use the wait function (1-2 hours is enough) to transform back; until that point, attempting to wait will give you a "you can't wait in this location" message.
- Unlike most companions in quests, if you hit Yamarz by mistake even once at any point during the quest (before he attacks you), it may count as an assault and earn you a 40 gold blood price owed to the Orcs. You can yield and pay Yamarz right away, though the gold won't be found on him when he dies. If this occurs in front of witnesses, however (such as during a random encounter passing through [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften")), you will also get a bounty in [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"). **?**
- If you attack Yamarz early, then kill the giant you have to kill in the quest, then return to the stronghold you can finish the quest but if you wait a few days or so Yamarz will return. Both he and Gularzob will act like they're the chief.
- Sometimes after bringing the required items to Atub for her to complete the ritual, she will walk up her tower and do absolutely nothing.
  -  A workaround on PC is to stand at the longhouse door and use the `moveto.player` console command on Atub.
- It is possible that Yamarz will be on the upper ledge when entering the cave.
  - You can climb the cliff to the ledge he is on and bypass most of the cave to arrive in Giant's Grove.

## Quest Stages

| The Cursed Tribe (DA06) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've heard rumors there's some kind of problem in the Orc settlement of Largashbur, southwest of Riften. *Objective 10:* Find out what's happening in Largashbur |
| 50 |  | The orcs of Largashbur are besieged by giants, and have been forbidden to leave their stronghold. Atub, the wise woman of the tribe, has asked me to find her Troll Fat and a Daedra Heart so that she may contact Malacath for guidance. *Objective 50:* Bring Troll Fat and a Daedra Heart to Atub |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Observe Atub's ritual |
| 70 |  | Malacath has spoken to his followers and expressed disappointment in them. He is angry they allowed his shrine to be desecrated, and has commanded the chieftain of Largashbur, Yamarz, to return to the shrine and reclaim it. *Objective 70:* Speak with Yamarz |
| 80 |  | Despite being specifically instructed by Malacath to see to it himself, Yamarz wants my help in defeating the giants that have overrun Fallowstone Cave and the shrine of Malacath. He's promised to pay me in exchange for making sure he arrives there safely. *Objective 80:* Meet Yamarz at Fallowstone Cave |
| 90 |  | *Objective 90:* Protect Yamarz |
| 100 |  | After Malacath ordered him to retake the shrine in Fallowstone Cave, Yamarz insisted that I escort him there to make sure he arrived safely. Now he has offered to pay me even more in exchange for killing the giant myself, to which I have agreed. *Objective 100:* Defeat the giant |
| 110 |  | After escorting Yamarz to Fallowstone Cave and proving myself more worthy, Malacath has commanded me to return to Largashbur and deliver Shagrol's Hammer there. *Objective 110:* Take Shagrol's Hammer back to Largashbur |
| 120 |  | *Objective 120:* Place Shagrol's Hammer on the shrine in Largashbur |
| 200 | ☑ | The curse placed on the Orcs of Largashbur is lifted. The tribe's leader, Yamarz, was revealed as a shiftless weakling in Malacath's eyes, and I have redeemed his actions by defeating the giant that had taken over the shrine in Fallowstone Cave. Malacath has named Gularzob as the new chief, and has named me his new Champion. |
| 255 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 20, 30, 40.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DA06 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DA06`.

# Skyrim:The Dainty Sload

## Overview

This article is about the quest. For the ship, see [Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Frame a [ship's](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload") captain to get revenge for a [jilted merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") |

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | Five [Thieves Guild Special Jobs](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Special_Job_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") in Solitude | | |

The Dainty Sload

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
2. Find out the mission details from [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").
3. Acquire [Balmora Blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Balmora_Blue "Skyrim:Balmora Blue") from [Sabine Nytte](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabine_Nytte "Skyrim:Sabine Nytte").
4. Travel to the [Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload").
5. Plant the Balmora Blue.
6. Return to Erikur.

### A Special Job

Once you've completed five [jobs](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Special_Job_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") in the city of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), speak to [Delvin](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") to receive a special job. Delvin explains that he has received word from Solitude about an opportunity. [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur") is an influential [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") and businessman in Solitude. Apparently, he is *"lookin' to run some kind of a [shill job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shill_Job "Skyrim:The Shill Job")"*. Completing this job will not only earn you a reward, it is a chance for the Guild to regain some influence in the city. Travel to Solitude and speak with Erikur, who can be found during the day at the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace").

When you speak to Erikur, he explains the story behind the job: *"Nothing raises my ire more than having an agreement broken. It's bad for business and it wastes time. Captain Volf of the [Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload") has decided to test my patience on this matter by neglecting to honor a trade agreement we had established."* Your job is to frame Volf for possession of an illicit substance by acquiring some very rare, very illegal [Balmora Blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Balmora_Blue "Skyrim:Balmora Blue") and planting it in his footlocker.

### From One Pirate to Another

Sabine's Footlocker, hidden beneath the dock leading to the Red Wave.

Your contact for the contraband is a crew member aboard the pirate ship, the [Red Wave](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave"). The Red Wave is docked outside the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse") just outside Solitude. Your contact, [Sabine Nytte](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabine_Nytte "Skyrim:Sabine Nytte"), will be on deck, waiting for you. Tell her what you're looking for, and she will ask for 1,500 gold for some Balmora Blue, claiming that she's the only person in Tamriel who can obtain it. If you accept her price, she gives you the key and directs you to the contraband, which is in a locked chest directly under the docks adjacent to The Red Wave. If you do not wish to pay such inflated prices, sneak into the bottom deck of the ship and locate the Red Wave Safe, which is guarded by a Master-level lock. Inside, you will learn from a note that the contraband is located "under the Wave", leading you to Sabine's Footlocker (though reading the note is not necessary for you to loot the contraband). Swim down below the docks and pick the Expert-level lock to the chest and take the Balmora Blue. Note that both locks can be skipped by pickpocketing the corresponding keys off of Sabine first.

### A Pirate Breaks the Law

Make your way out to the Dainty Sload, anchored near [Solitude's Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse"). There are two [corsairs](/wiki/Skyrim:Corsair "Skyrim:Corsair") guarding the entrance to the interior of the ship. One remains looking out to sea, while another roams the deck. Engage them or sneak below deck through the unlocked door. Inside, there are more corsairs to deal with. Whether by sneaking or defeating the corsairs, head down the stairs into the bottom of the ship, then back up again until you reach the Captain's room.

The ship's [first mate](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Mate "Skyrim:First Mate") guards the area and has a high detection level. The Captain's Chest is your target and you can pick the adept lock, or you can kill the First Mate and take the key. On the table is an [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") and the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill book *[A Dance in Fire, V6](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v6 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v6")*. Plant the Balmora Blue and make your way back to the entrance.

### Revenge is Sweet

Travel back to Erikur at the Blue Palace (or at his home), who is very pleased with the fruits of your labor. He'll reward you with a random [spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes") for a novice or apprentice level Destruction or Illusion spell, and the assurance that he will re-open any doors in Solitude to facilitate the Guild's return.

Report back to Delvin. He'll give you your pay, and will compliment you on your actions, *"Erikur assures me that Captain Volf will spend pretty much the rest of his life clapped in irons. Best of all, he's also pledged to open doors for us in Solitude and to get things rollin' again"*. He then points out that the added infamy you earned the guild has attracted a new merchant to The Ragged Flagon.

## Notes

- If the Dainty Sload has been cleared of its inhabitants prior to starting this quest, the ship and its inhabitants will be fully reset, including the First Mate.
- When the quest is completed, you can retrieve more Balmora Blue from the chest.
- After completing this quest, three [Thief Cache](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_Cache "Skyrim:Thief Cache") barrels will appear around Solitude.
- Despite Erikur and Delvin mentioning that Captain Volf will spend the rest of his years in Solitude Jail, he cannot be found in any of the cells and in fact does not appear in the game at all.
- You can kill the crew of the Dainty Sload, including the First Mate, without any repercussions.

## Bugs

- Erikur may have glitched off the map. This usually occurs in games where a lot of days have passed.
  -  Type into console: `prid 000198A9` (this selects Erikur) followed by `moveto player` (this moves Erikur to your current location).
  - He can be reached by getting underneath the regular map. To do so, hop onto the Angeline's Aromatics roof and use Whirlwind Sprint to reach the lower roof of Bits and Pieces. Head west along the roof and hop into the space that joins to the roof of Radiant Raiment, then navigate to Erikur's quest marker.
- Sometimes Sabine Nytte will get stuck inside the Red Wave and not come out. This is problematic as you are considered to be trespassing when inside the ship.
  -  One way get around the bug is to type `setcellownership solituderedwave` into the console.
  - Another way to fix it is to pickpocket Sabine and get caught. She will then get up to attack you, followed by her fellow shipmates. Run outside and they will follow. Lower your weapons to surrender and she and her shipmates will stop fighting and walk towards the entrance to the ship. Before they get there, talk to Sabine and ask her about the illegal substance.
- The Dainty Sload ship may not render correctly, causing you to fall through the floor and become unable to enter the ship.
  - Reloading a previous save fixes this.
- The Balmora Blue may not drop into your inventory after you've taken it from the chest.
  - Balmora Blue may drop in your inventory in food selection instead of potions selection.
  - Reloading a previous save fixes this.
  - If you do not have a previous save available, it is impossible to complete the quest. Which makes the achievement "One With the Shadows" also impossible to obtain.
- Sometimes Delvin Mallory will talk to you about starting the quest, however the quest will not start and the option about the job will not appear again in Delvin's dialogue options.
  - Reloading a save before speaking to Delvin about the quest may fix this.
  -  Type into console: `setstage TGTQ02 10`. This will start the quest.
- The Balmora Blue that you need to plant in the Captain's Chest on the ship is never removed from the chest after planting it there. The Balmora Blue also loses its quest item status afterwards, allowing you to take it back out of the Captain's Chest, which make no sense at all since it would be taken from there as evidence against Captain Volf.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| The Dainty Sload (TGTQ02) | | |

| 20 |  | Erikur has been cheated by Volf, captain of a trading vessel named the Dainty Sload. In order to frame Volf for a crime he didn't commit, Erikur is requesting that a substance called Balmora Blue be stashed on board in the captain's footlocker. *Objective 20:* Acquire Balmora Blue |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Plant the Balmora Blue |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Return to Erikur once the Balmora Blue is planted |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 25.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGTQ02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGTQ02`.

The Night Mother's sarcophagus

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Approach the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother").
2. Speak with the contact.
3. Kill the target.

### Keeping the Faith

After the events of [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!"), the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") has new headquarters to improve and maintain. As the Listener, your responsibility is to heed the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") and continue to fulfill contracts.
For this recurring quest, approaching the Night Mother will initiate a dialogue: another child has prayed to their mother and performed the [Black Sacrament](/wiki/Lore:Night_Mother "Lore:Night Mother"), securing another contract for the Brotherhood.
Travel to the specified location and speak to the client who will give you a name and location of a generic NPC that he wants eliminated. The client will pay you the money up front. Travel to the location and complete the contract. Return to the Night Mother for another contract as needed or desired.

### Contact the Client...

The client will be one of ten randomly chosen citizens who performed the Black Sacrament.
None of the contract givers exist prior to the quest:

|  |
| --- |
| - *"Speak with the [Blasphemous Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Blasphemous_Priest "Skyrim:Blasphemous Priest") at the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth"), in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). Accept his gold, then kill the target. Hail Sithis!"* - *"Speak with the [Corrupt Agent](/wiki/Skyrim:Corrupt_Agent "Skyrim:Corrupt Agent") at the [Penitus Oculatus Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Outpost "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Outpost"), in [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"). Accept his gold, then kill the target. Hail Sithis!"* - *"Speak with the [Desperate Gambler](/wiki/Skyrim:Desperate_Gambler "Skyrim:Desperate Gambler") at the [Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Barracks "Skyrim:Windhelm Barracks"), in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). So begins a contract, bound in blood."* - *"Speak with the [Dishonored Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Dishonored_Skald "Skyrim:Dishonored Skald") at the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College"), in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). So begins a contract, bound in blood."* - *"Speak with the [Unemployed Laborer](/wiki/Skyrim:Unemployed_Laborer "Skyrim:Unemployed Laborer") at the [Frostfruit Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostfruit_Inn "Skyrim:Frostfruit Inn"), in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). Accept his gold, then kill the target. So begins a contract, bound in blood."* |

### ...Now Find the Target

All contract givers share the same dialogue and will spawn a randomly chosen target from the following dialogue options:

|  |
| --- |
| - *"So you're the... the assassin? I need you to kill the [Visiting Noble](/wiki/Skyrim:Visiting_Noble "Skyrim:Visiting Noble") at [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach"), in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). Here's the gold. I... I hope it's enough."* - *"So you're the one from the... Dark Brotherhood? I need you to kill the [Big Laborer](/wiki/Skyrim:Big_Laborer "Skyrim:Big Laborer") at [Katla's Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla%27s_Farm "Skyrim:Katla's Farm"). Here's the gold for the kill. Make it painful."* - *"You must be the... assassin. I need you to kill the [Itinerant Lumberjack](/wiki/Skyrim:Itinerant_Lumberjack "Skyrim:Itinerant Lumberjack"), in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), at the logging camp. Here, this is all the gold I have."* - *"You're the assassin, right? Look, there's this [Reckless Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Reckless_Mage "Skyrim:Reckless Mage") in the [Frozen Hearth Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth"), in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). I want him dead. This gold should cover it."* - *"You're the one? From the... the Dark Brotherhood? Here's the gold..."* - *"You're here! I was wondering if that Black Sacrament even worked. You look the type. Listen, there's this [Grim Shieldmaiden](/wiki/Skyrim:Grim_Shieldmaiden "Skyrim:Grim Shieldmaiden") walking the streets of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). Kill her. Now take this gold, and go."* - *"Are you the assassin? From the...? Well, there's this [Traveling Dignitary](/wiki/Skyrim:Traveling_Dignitary "Skyrim:Traveling Dignitary"), in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). I need her... you know. This gold will cover it, right?"* - *"I'm glad you're here. I need you to kill a [Coldhearted Gravedigger](/wiki/Skyrim:Coldhearted_Gravedigger "Skyrim:Coldhearted Gravedigger"), tends to work in the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Windhelm) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Windhelm)") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). This is all the gold I have."* - *"Good, you're here. Look, in [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), there's this [Beautiful Barbarian](/wiki/Skyrim:Beautiful_Barbarian "Skyrim:Beautiful Barbarian"). I need her dead. Don't ask why. Just do it. This gold should cover it."* |

## Notes

- The targets that you are supposed to murder never sleep, and almost always stay in crowded areas. This can make it very difficult to kill them without incurring a bounty. One possible way to accomplish it is to hide a safe distance away (remain in sneak mode and make sure the eye is totally closed) and then send a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") to kill the target. Run outside the area in question while the crowd is retaliating against your follower, and then fast travel out of the hold. Your follower will fast travel with you.
- All targets have 50 health. Plan your assassination tools (such as poisons and weapon choices) with this in mind.
- If the recently killed target is reanimated and subsequently turned into an ash pile on their "second death", the next time they are randomly chosen as a target, both the NPC and the ash pile will appear. Attempting to search the ash pile will cause the NPC to speak. Sneaking and searching the ash pile qualifies as pickpocketing.
- Sometimes if you reactivate (or talk to) the contact while they are still talking it will cause you to get paid twice.
- Sometimes you can intimidate the target when talking to him. This can cause him to attack you, and the surrounding people will try to kill him. If they kill him, the quest will be complete and you will not have a bounty. The target can also try to flee; in that case, chase him into a secluded area, and then kill him.
- Pickpocketing a target will never work, no matter how high your Sneak and Pickpocket skill.

## Bugs

- Sometimes the contact will simply say, *"Look, I'm busy. Please go bother somebody else."* If you return after a few days, the contact will eventually give you information about the target. It will count as speaking to the contact but you will not receive payment. **?**
- [Deceiving the Herd](/wiki/Skyrim:Deceiving_the_Herd "Skyrim:Deceiving the Herd") can trigger its kill selection setup before you have been told to actually do anything. This can cause the quest to react to this one's target kills inappropriately.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.1, addresses this issue. Keep in mind though that using a Dark Brotherhood target for Deceiving the Herd is perfectly valid. All the fix does is prevent Deceiving the Herd from registering the kill until you're actually told to make one.

| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Speak with the contact |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Kill the target |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DBrecurring stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DBrecurring`.

# Skyrim:The Drunken Huntsman

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
