The Drunken Huntsman

**The Drunken Huntsman** is a [tavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") and hunting supply store in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). It is located across the street from [Breezehome](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome "Skyrim:Breezehome"),

and is co-owned by [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") brothers [Elrindir](/wiki/Skyrim:Elrindir "Skyrim:Elrindir") and [Anoriath](/wiki/Skyrim:Anoriath "Skyrim:Anoriath"). Elrindir tends the counter, buying and selling weapons, armor, food, and miscellaneous items 24 hours a day. It consists of one area only, *[The Drunken Huntsman](#The_Drunken_Huntsman),* that includes a main taproom and two small bedrooms, one downstairs and another upstairs.

The inn owes its name to a hunting incident between the brothers. On a moonlit night after consuming too much mead, Anoriath mistook his brother for a deer, shooting at him and piercing his rump with an arrow. They knew then they had come up with the name for their business.

**NOTE**: Like all other shops, The Drunken Huntsman has a number of fixed wares on display scattered around the main room. These can be bought from Elrindir and will disappear from the room when purchased. For a list of these special items, see [this section](#Displayed_Merchandise).

## Related Quests

- **[Battle of the Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_the_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of the Champions")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions"): A battle between two [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") champions is about to begin.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Ahlam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahlam "Skyrim:Ahlam")  [Anoriath](/wiki/Skyrim:Anoriath "Skyrim:Anoriath") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink") \*  [Elrindir](/wiki/Skyrim:Elrindir "Skyrim:Elrindir") (Owner) [Fletcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Fletcher")  [Jenassa](/wiki/Skyrim:Jenassa "Skyrim:Jenassa") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")  [Nazeem](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazeem "Skyrim:Nazeem") |

\* This person only sells goods at his market stall in the Plains District.

## The Drunken Huntsman

The Drunken Huntsman interior

.jpg)

The note added by [Civil War Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions")

There are two entrances to the Drunken Huntsman, although both lead you into the taproom. Elrindir stands at his counter in the western corner, providing his services around the clock. Hidden underneath the counter is a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") skill book *[The Black Arrow, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Arrow,_v2 "Skyrim:The Black Arrow, v2")*. Behind the counter is a storage alcove with a clothes wardrobe and a food barrel. A special [fish barrel](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Barrel "Skyrim:Containers") holds a variety of fish. If the [Civil War Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") is installed and you haven't yet joined either the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") or the [Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), a note named *[Battle of Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of Champions")* will appear on the counter, and you will be directed to read it to start the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_the_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of the Champions").

North of the counter is a small table for patrons, with a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"), two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). At an alcove table on the east side sits [Jenassa](/wiki/Skyrim:Jenassa "Skyrim:Jenassa"), a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") mercenary who can be recruited as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") for 500 gold. Her table has a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") and a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") in a bowl. In the center of the room are two [cooking spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") dangling over a burning fire, and along the northwestern wall is another table for customers, with a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a bottle of [nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a bottle of wine. [Olfrid Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfrid_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Olfrid Battle-Born") will often sit at this table to enjoy his meals. Another small table stands near the cooking spits with a bottle of ale. Underneath the ladder leading to the bedroom on the second floor, sits an [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and, on a food barrel, two bottles of ale.

The brothers' bedroom on the north side has two owned beds, although only Anoriath ever sleeps. The bed to the northwest has a food sack underneath it and a non-respawning unlocked chest containing leveled items at the bedhead. The [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger") of the Huntsman can be found atop a dresser, right next to a locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox").

The second floor consists of one bedroom reserved for regulars [Nazeem](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazeem "Skyrim:Nazeem") and his wife [Ahlam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahlam "Skyrim:Ahlam"), who sleep there every night despite owning [Chillfurrow Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillfurrow_Farm "Skyrim:Chillfurrow Farm") outside of town. At the foot of the owned double bed stands a respawning unlocked chest containing gold, and the wardrobe contains cheap clothing. Two end tables with clutter stand on either side of the bed, one with a copy of *[The Third Era Timeline](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Third_Era_Timeline "Skyrim:The Third Era Timeline")* on top, the other with a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and a bottle of alto wine.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example on the counter. They can be purchased from the merchant, or stolen. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

|  |
| --- |
| - **Weapons**: 1 [Imperial Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bow "Skyrim:Imperial Bow"), 2 [Iron Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") - **Apparel**: 1 [Leather Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") - **Food**: 2 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") |

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the Drunken Huntsman's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | Complete leveled set of heavy armor (unmatched, unenchanted; Ebony is best possible) |  |
| 1 | Complete leveled set of light armor (unmatched, unenchanted; Glass is best possible) |  |
| 1 | Complete leveled set of weapons (one of each type incl. bow except dagger; unenchanted; Ebony is best possible) |  |
| 4 | [Honningbrew Meads](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") |  |
| 50 | [Iron Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") |  |
| ~4 | [Leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather "Skyrim:Leather") or [Leather Strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") | Max 5 (5@75%) |
| ~4 | Leveled [Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") (unenchanted; Glass and Ebony are best possible) | Max 5 (5@75%) |
| ~23 | Leveled [Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows") (batches of 15; Ebony is best possible) | Max 30 (30@75%) |
| ~2 | Leveled [Bows](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") (enchanted; Ebony is best possible) | Max 3 (3@75%) |
| ~4 | Leveled [Bows](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") (unenchanted; Ebony is best possible) | Max 5 (5@75%) |
| ~4 | Leveled [Weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") (unenchanted; Ebony is best possible) | Max 5 (5@75%) |
| 1 | [Pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") |  |
| 1 | Random [drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") |  |
| ~5 | [Torches](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch") | Max 10 (10@50%) |

## Notes

- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the right of the entrance door.
- All dressers, end tables, and cupboards in the location are non-respawning.

## Bugs

- Investing here is impossible due to a missing global variant for the store.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.
- An Iron Arrow may be found on the floor just before Elrindir's counter, an Iron Dagger inconsistently shifts placement upon different playthroughs, and the [Do Not Delete](/wiki/Skyrim:Do_Not_Delete "Skyrim:Do Not Delete") chest may be accessed by clipping into the floor near Elrindir's counter as seen in [this video](https://imgur.com/a/hRJfTB4) .
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.6, addresses this issue. The arrow and dagger were also missing their ownership settings.

# Skyrim:The Dwarven Crown

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Gather all the components of a powerful Dwarven Crown from within a [forgotten Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Begins once you enter [Runoff Caverns, Vardnknd Gallery](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns#Vardnknd_Gallery "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns") |
| Location(s): | [Runoff Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns") |
| Reward: | [Dwarven Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Crown "Skyrim:Dwarven Crown"), [Dwarven Autumn Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Autumn_Visage "Skyrim:Dwarven Autumn Visage"), [Dwarven Spring Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spring_Visage "Skyrim:Dwarven Spring Visage"), [Dwarven Winter Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Winter_Visage "Skyrim:Dwarven Winter Visage"), and ability to forge [Dwarven Crown of Autumn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Crown_of_Autumn "Skyrim:Dwarven Crown of Autumn")/[Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Crown_of_Spring "Skyrim:Dwarven Crown of Spring")/[Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Crown_of_Winter "Skyrim:Dwarven Crown of Winter") |
| ID: | DLCDwarvenPuzzleDungeonCrownQuest |
| Added by: | [Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons") |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | |  | **Concurrent** [Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons_(quest) "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons (quest)"), [The Dwarven Horse](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dwarven_Horse "Skyrim:The Dwarven Horse") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Concurrent | [Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons_(quest) "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons (quest)"), [The Dwarven Horse](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dwarven_Horse "Skyrim:The Dwarven Horse") | | |

The hidden entrance to the area containing the Dwarven Winter Visage

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Enter the Vardnknd Gallery section of [Runoff Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns") and retrieve the [Dwarven Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Crown "Skyrim:Dwarven Crown") from [Elberon](/wiki/Skyrim:Elberon "Skyrim:Elberon")'s body.
2. Locate the [Dwarven Autumn Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Autumn_Visage "Skyrim:Dwarven Autumn Visage") in a side room the Autumn's Bells section of the dungeon.
3. Locate the [Dwarven Spring Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spring_Visage "Skyrim:Dwarven Spring Visage") down a long side passage in the Spring's Symphony section of the dungeon.
4. Locate the [Dwarven Winter Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Winter_Visage "Skyrim:Dwarven Winter Visage") in a hidden area in the Winter's Chimes area of the dungeon, accessible by means of a sloping pipe.

### Crown of Legend

You must travel to [Vardnknd Gallery](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns#Vardnknd_Gallery "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns"), the second section of [Runoff Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns"), a dungeon which will already be marked on your map. Once you enter this section of the dungeon, a wizard named [Elberon](/wiki/Skyrim:Elberon "Skyrim:Elberon") will be struck by lightning, dying instantly. This quest will then begin, prompting you to loot Elberon's corpse for his strange [Dwarven Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Crown "Skyrim:Dwarven Crown").

Once you've obtained the Crown, you will be prompted to search for three masks which can be slotted into the headpiece. All three of these can be found within the dungeon in their corresponding areas, although they are designed to be well-hidden and therefore may take a bit of exploration to find.

### Mask of Autumn

The [Dwarven Autumn Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Autumn_Visage "Skyrim:Dwarven Autumn Visage") is located in the [Autumn's Bells](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns#Autumn.27s_Bells "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns") section of Runoff Caverns. Head east after entering the main chamber until you find the bridge over the ravine; after crossing the bridge, go north along the brick road and it will lead you straight to the entrance to the corridor that leads to the mask.

### Mask of Spring

The [Dwarven Spring Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spring_Visage "Skyrim:Dwarven Spring Visage") is located in the [Spring's Symphony](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns#Spring.27s_Symphony "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns") section of Runoff Caverns. It is located at the end of a side hallway accessible through a door a short way into the chamber. However, the door is locked; the key is held by the [Blooming Spriggan Matron](/wiki/Skyrim:Blooming_Spriggan_Matron "Skyrim:Blooming Spriggan Matron") boss at the end of the section. The hallway is partially filled with a green miasma, so the [Dwarven Drone Fly](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Drone_Fly "Skyrim:Dwarven Drone Fly") you obtain in the room on your right just before you jump out of this section might prove useful.

### Mask of Winter

The [Dwarven Winter Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Winter_Visage "Skyrim:Dwarven Winter Visage") is found in the [Winter's Chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns#Winter.27s_Chimes "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns") section of Runoff Caverns, in a hidden area that can be challenging to find. It is located in the second section, after you make the first jump. It is off the short hallway containing [Frosted Dwarven Spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frosted_Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Frosted Dwarven Spider"), through a Dwarven gate that is raised above ground level. The gate must be reached by climbing up a bank of snow and a sloped Dwarven pipe (as pictured above). From the gate, you must dive into the water through a short underwater passage to access the section. Once you have navigated to the chamber containing the mask, you will be attacked by a powerful [Frosted Dwarven Centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Frosted_Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Frosted Dwarven Centurion") which uses frost attacks.

### Forging the Crown

The masks can be worn on their own, but you can make their effects more powerful by affixing one to the crown. Take the crown, a mask, and two [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strip "Skyrim:Leather Strip") to any forge or anvil, and you can craft the [Dwarven Crown of Autumn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Crown_of_Autumn "Skyrim:Dwarven Crown of Autumn"), the [Dwarven Crown of Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Crown_of_Spring "Skyrim:Dwarven Crown of Spring"), or the [Dwarven Crown of Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Crown_of_Winter "Skyrim:Dwarven Crown of Winter"). You can only have one of these at a time, but you can swap them out with each other at a forge as often as you like, only costing you two leather strips each time.

## Notes

- There is no Dwarven Summer Visage.

## Quest Stages

| The Dwarven Crown (DLCDwarvenPuzzleDungeonCrownQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 1 |  | I've encountered a wizard wearing a strange looking Dwarven Crown. The slots in the facing suggest a separate piece can be attached. *Objective 0:* Find the Mask of Autumn  *Objective 1:* Find the Mask of Winter  *Objective 2:* Find the Mask of Spring |
| 2 |  | I've found all three masks for the Dwarven Crown. If I go to a forge, I should be able to add and remove them as I see fit. *Objective 3:* Use a forge to slot a mask into the Dwarven Crown  *Objective 4:* Retrieve the Dwarven Crown |
| 3 | ☑ | I affixed a mask to the crown. I should be able to change which mask is affixed at any forge. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLCDwarvenPuzzleDungeonCrownQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLCDwarvenPuzzleDungeonCrownQuest`.

# Skyrim:The Dwarven Horse

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Reassemble an ancient Dwarven [vamidium](/wiki/Lore:Vamidium "Lore:Vamidium").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Broken Dwarven Horse outside [Runoff Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns") |
| Location(s): | [Runoff Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns") |

| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | |  | **Concurrent** [Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons_(quest) "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons (quest)"), [The Dwarven Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dwarven_Crown "Skyrim:The Dwarven Crown") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Concurrent | [Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons_(quest) "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons (quest)"), [The Dwarven Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dwarven_Crown "Skyrim:The Dwarven Crown") | | |

The torso of a strange equine construct

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Activate the Broken Dwarven Horse outside [Runoff Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns").
2. Enter the Autumn's Bells section of the dungeon.
3. Locate the [Horse Right Front Leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Right_Front_Leg "Skyrim:Horse Right Front Leg") next to the dead [mercenary](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercenary "Skyrim:Mercenary") in the entrance hallway.
4. Locate the [Horse Left Back Leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Left_Back_Leg "Skyrim:Horse Left Back Leg") in the main chamber, near the field of White Molded Wheat.
5. Cross the bridge in the main chamber and locate the [Horse Right Back Leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Right_Back_Leg "Skyrim:Horse Right Back Leg") between the fields of Sickly Green Wheat and Orange-Encrusted Wheat.
6. Locate the [Horse Left Front Leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Left_Front_Leg "Skyrim:Horse Left Front Leg") up on a pedestal along the southern wall of the main chamber.
7. Place harvested samples of the six special wheat varieties in the depositors to open the chamber containing the [Conduit Control Gem](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Conduit_Control_Gem&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Conduit Control Gem (page does not exist)") and grab the [Horse Head](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Head "Skyrim:Horse Head") found within.
8. Return outside and activate the broken horse to obtain your own [Dwarven Horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Horse "Skyrim:Dwarven Horse") mount.

### A Broken Horse

Unlike most quests added by [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"), this one does not automatically begin upon installing [Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons"). Instead, you must travel to the entrance of [Runoff Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns"), which will already be marked on your map. Outside, you will find a "Broken Dwarven Horse", a metallic Dwarven torso lying partially submerged in a stream. Activate this object to begin the quest, which will task you with assembling the pieces to reconstruct this strange equine [construct](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons").

All of the parts are in the Autumn's Bells section of Runoff Caverns, which is found deep inside, within the Dwarven ruins of Vardnknd. You will need to traverse the entirety of the Runoff Caverns section of the dungeon to reach the hub area at Vardnknd Gallery. The entrance to Autumn's Bells is in this central chamber.

The horse head sitting on a pile of gold

### Exploring the Ruins

All of the Dwarven items needed to reconstruct the horse are zero weight due to being [quest items](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items "Skyrim:Quest Items"), so you needn't worry about getting them back out of the ruins. They will not be marked on your map until you get close, meaning you may need to scour the area to find them all. You will need to locate five in total:

- The first part of the horse is easy to find: it is the [Horse Right Front Leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Right_Front_Leg "Skyrim:Horse Right Front Leg") next to the dead [mercenary](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercenary "Skyrim:Mercenary") in the entrance hallway of Autumn's Bells. You will likely come across this mercenary while completing the [Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons_(quest) "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons (quest)") quest.
- The [Horse Left Back Leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Left_Back_Leg "Skyrim:Horse Left Back Leg") is in the main chamber, near the field of White Molded Wheat. It is on the east side of the collapsed tower (behind a chest).
- The [Horse Right Back Leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Right_Back_Leg "Skyrim:Horse Right Back Leg") is on the other side of the main chamber, which will necessitate crossing the bridge in the center. It's under a collapsed building to the south from the Sickly Green Wheat.
- The [Horse Left Front Leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Left_Front_Leg "Skyrim:Horse Left Front Leg") is up on a pedestal along the southern wall of the main chamber.
- The final piece of the horse will necessitate completing the Autumn's Bells puzzle. This can be done by harvesting samples of the six special wheat varieties found growing in the chamber and placing them in the depositors located back near the field of Glowing Red Wheat. Once all six wheat varieties have been deposited, the chamber containing the [Conduit Control Gem](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Conduit_Control_Gem&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Conduit Control Gem (page does not exist)") will be unlocked; the [Horse Head](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Head "Skyrim:Horse Head") lies on a pile of gold within.

### Reward

With all five pieces assembled, you can return to the surface and activate the broken torso once again. Doing so will create a functioning [Dwarven Horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Horse "Skyrim:Dwarven Horse"), which can be ridden as a mount. It takes no damage whatsoever; you can stay mounted on it and avoid all harm.

| 2 |  | I have found all the pieces of the Dwarven Horse and can now rebuild it. *Objective 6:* Return all the pieces to the Dwarven Horse's frame |
| 3 | ☑ | I found the intact remains of a Dwarven Horse. However, several pieces were missing from the set. After investigating the ruins of Vardnknd, I was able to find the pieces and reassemble the horse. |

# Skyrim:The Ebony Warrior

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [RIM](/wiki/User:RIM "User:RIM"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Locate and defeat the [Ebony Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Warrior "Skyrim:Ebony Warrior").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Ebony Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Warrior "Skyrim:Ebony Warrior") |
| Location(s): | Radiant [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities "Skyrim:Cities"), [Last Vigil](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_Vigil "Skyrim:Last Vigil") |
| Reward: | Several pieces of heavily enchanted ebony equipment, several valuable gems |
| ID: | DLC2EbonyWarriorQuest |
| Required Level: | 80 |

The Ebony Warrior

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Reach [level](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveling "Skyrim:Leveling") 80.
2. Locate the [Ebony Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Warrior "Skyrim:Ebony Warrior").
3. Defeat the Ebony Warrior.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Upon your reaching level 80, a [mysterious warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Warrior "Skyrim:Ebony Warrior") wearing a full suit of ebony armor will approach you in any [major city](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities#Major_Cities "Skyrim:Cities") and challenge you to a duel at his [Last Vigil](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_Vigil "Skyrim:Last Vigil").
After the conversation, the quest will then update to give the location, a camp northeast of [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall"). The Ebony Warrior will not attack you when approached, and will not speak. He will simply stand, brandishing his sword as a clear invitation. You must initiate the attack for the battle to begin. Make sure that you are prepared for one serious fight. It is advised to wear the strongest armor you can get and have plenty of potions at the ready. You may want to bring a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") as well.

The Ebony Warrior is arguably the toughest enemy in the game, and his high armor rating and multiple elemental resistances make him hard to kill for both mages and melee characters. He also has a number of perks to aid him in combat, including the top perks in the One-Handed, Archery, and Heavy Armor skills. He is the only non-Nord NPC capable of using certain [dragon shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") in combat. These shouts include [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force"), which may easily knock you off the edge of the nearby cliffs. The Ebony Warrior can also be harmed by falling damage, but you must damage him after he lands but before he stands back up for the damage to take effect, otherwise he can survive any fall and will actually be restored to full health after he gets back on his feet.

Whatever your tactics, once you have defeated the Ebony Warrior the quest will conclude and you may loot his body for his fully enchanted set of equipment and a few other treasures.

## Notes

- The Ebony Warrior only appears once you've reached level 80. You can delay the fight for as long as you like; it's not necessary to fight him right away.
- Since the Ebony Warrior does not attack until he is attacked, if you have the [Assassin's Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Assassin%27s_Blade "Skyrim:Assassin's Blade") perk, you can sneak behind him and easily kill him with a strong dagger.
- The Ebony Warrior is also not immune to poison (merely 50% resistant, like any other Redguard). You can use a strong poison (for example, one derived from [jarrin root](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarrin_Root "Skyrim:Jarrin Root")) to slay him quickly.
- The [Marked for Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Marked_for_Death "Skyrim:Marked for Death") shout can be very useful for making the fight easier.
- Because of the Ebony Warrior's Reflect Blows perk, striking him with a one-handed or two-handed weapon power attack can result in damage being reflected back and potentially killing you. Bow attacks do not incur this penalty and using a strong Fortify Archery potion and shooting him while sneaking can be an easier method for dispatching him quickly.
- A [Staff of Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Staff of Chain Lightning") always staggers enemies upon hit, unlike the regular spell. With lots of filled soul gems, he can easily be killed by using the staff then recharging it when necessary. Using the staff also keeps him at a distance, as he seems to prefer melee combat over archery. A high [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill and/or Fortify Destruction apparel will result in more charges of the staff and thus requires fewer soul gems.
- If the Ebony Warrior disarms you (or a low leveled follower through the Disarm Shout) of your weapon, be careful as it may roll all the way down the mountain, causing you to potentially lose unique weapons to the wilderness.
- You don't need to fight him on the mountain he awaits at; you can lure him down the hill and fight him on more level ground, which negates the very real danger of being swept off the steep hills yourself by his Unrelenting Force Shout. Trees and rock formations also give you more cover from his attacks.

## Bugs

- When the Ebony Warrior is killed, the game stats might count the death as a murder.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- There is a rare occasion where the Ebony Warrior will be hostile on sight to you when he initially spawns. This can be fixed by being sent to jail through submitting to the guard in the hold that he spawned in. **?**
- If the Ebony Warrior appears first, during one of the vampire attacks, he might get stuck in an endless animation loop of cowering in fear. This prevents him from talking to you, including to initiate the quest. **?**
  - Using the "resetAI" console command, on him fixes this: Face him, open console, select him with left-click, type and execute the command.
- If you use the Soul Tear shout to kill the Ebony Warrior and loot his body before he rises you can attack him again and he will gain a new set of ebony armor.
- If you run up the hill past the dead Frost Troll, the Ebony Warrior can get stuck behind one of the low rocks as he pursues you. **?**

## Quest Stages

| 100 |  | A warrior in ebony mail approached me in <alias=StartCity>. He has challenged me to fight him at his last vigil, wherever that is. *Objective 100:* Meet the Ebony Warrior at the Last Vigil |
| 200 | ☑ | I have defeated the Ebony Warrior. May his soul find rest in Sovngarde. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2EbonyWarriorQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2EbonyWarriorQuest`.

# Skyrim:The Edge of Ruin

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Find a madwoman's [legendary bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruin%27s_Edge_(item) "Skyrim:Ruin's Edge (item)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatically added after purchasing the [Ruin's Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruin%27s_Edge "Skyrim:Ruin's Edge") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") (does not appear in journal) |
| Location(s): | [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave") |
| Reward: | [Ruin's Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruin%27s_Edge_(item) "Skyrim:Ruin's Edge (item)") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE004\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Ruin's Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruin%27s_Edge "Skyrim:Ruin's Edge") |

A bow from the Shivering Isles is yours to claim

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave").
2. Take [Ruin's Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruin%27s_Edge_(item) "Skyrim:Ruin's Edge (item)").

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is an unmarked quest to recover [Ruin's Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruin%27s_Edge_(item) "Skyrim:Ruin's Edge (item)"), a fabled bow. The [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") boss in [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave") is in possession of the bow.

Defeat the bandit and claim it as your own to finish the quest. You'll also find many types of cheese on the bandit: an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), and [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"). You might want to bring a pickaxe to mine the ore here as well.

## Notes

- Ruin's Edge originally [appeared](/wiki/Shivering:Ruin%27s_Edge "Shivering:Ruin's Edge") in *[Shivering Isles](/wiki/Shivering:Shivering_Isles "Shivering:Shivering Isles")*. It was an enchanted [Dark Seducer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Seducer "Skyrim:Dark Seducer") bow given to you as a quest reward by [Lady Syl](/wiki/Lore:Syl "Lore:Syl"), Duchess of [Dementia](/wiki/Lore:Dementia_(place) "Lore:Dementia (place)").
- This quest would originally be added to your journal upon installing the [Ruin's Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruin%27s_Edge "Skyrim:Ruin's Edge") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). This was changed with the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition") update, allowing you to discover the bow through natural gameplay.
- The leveled list that adds cheese to the bandit boss is called `ccBGSSSE004_LItemCheeseForEveryone`, referring to one of [Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath "Skyrim:Sheogorath")'s favorite lines.
- With the [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, a unique [Bliss Bug in a Jar](/wiki/Skyrim:Bliss_Bug_in_a_Jar "Skyrim:Bliss Bug in a Jar") can be found in Stony Creek Cave. This appears regardless of whether or not you have the Ruin's Edge Creation installed.

Notes

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE004_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE004_Quest`.

# Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [JR](/wiki/User:JR "User:JR"), checked by [Jak Atackka](/wiki/User:Jak_Atackka "User:Jak Atackka") |

| [SR-qico-College of Winterhold.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-College_of_Winterhold.png) | **Reclaim the [College](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") and contain the Eye.** |

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus") | | → Next | [Aftershock](/wiki/Skyrim:Aftershock "Skyrim:Aftershock") | | |

Inside the Hall of the Elements with The Eye of Magnus at the center

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Breach the barrier around the college with the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus").
2. Confront [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano") in the [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements").
3. Defeat Ancano with the help of the Staff of Magnus.

### All Hell Has Broken Loose

Firstly, you'll notice that when attempting to fast travel back to the College is that it no longer has a map marker. You'll need to travel directly to the town of Winterhold, then travel on foot the rest of the way. When arriving back at the College, you will see that all is not well. [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") and the other college mages have been awaiting your return. A magical force field created by the [Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Lore:Eye_of_Magnus "Lore:Eye of Magnus") now surrounds the college and Tolfdir will tell you of [Mirabelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine")'s death. Looking to Tolfdir for direction, he will say, *"You're the one with the staff, my dear/boy. If it can help us get inside the College, and reach Ancano, we'll have to hope there's a way to stop all this."* That is your cue to equip the [staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus") and lead the charge into the College.

### The Staff and The Eye

Tolfdir tries to stop Ancano from activating the Eye of Magnus.

Aim the staff at the barrier and it will dissipate, allowing safe passage into the College. The quest now is to get to the [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements") where Ancano is trying to activate the Eye of Magnus. Ancano will proclaim that he has the power to destroy the world at his fingertips, and that he cannot be stopped. He has become connected to the Eye at this point and absorbs more and more power from it. Tolfdir will cast a [fire spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage") at Ancano, but to no avail.

The Eye of Magnus at full power

Tolfdir tells you to use the staff on the Eye. It will begin to crack open, then emit a blinding flash, and you will be briefly stunned. Both Tolfdir and your follower (if you have any) will be paralyzed and remain this way until Ancano is dead. When the Eye is fully open, it will spawn [magic anomalies](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Anomaly "Skyrim:Magic Anomaly") and Ancano will lose his connection with it. The Eye will emit a blinding light; after this happens, continue to use the staff on it until it fully closes again. Ancano is vulnerable at this time and he should be busy dealing with the magic anomalies. Start inflicting damage. If you take too long, Ancano may reopen the eye and become invulnerable again; in this case, simply repeat the procedure and he will eventually succumb. Tolfdir will assist in eliminating the anomalies.

It is not recommended that the staff be used for battle, as it can quickly run out of charge. Fortunately, you can recharge it with the soul gems dropped by the magic anomalies, though the staff requires almost two grand soul gems' worth to fully recharge.

### The New Arch-Mage

When Ancano is defeated, ask Tolfdir what you should do now. While he explains that he does not know how to contain the Eye, [Quaranir](/wiki/Skyrim:Quaranir "Skyrim:Quaranir"), of the [Psijic Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Psijic_Order "Skyrim:Psijic Order") will appear.
Quaranir will congratulate you, telling you that you have met their expectations. He will assure you that the Psijic Order will safeguard the Eye, which might otherwise destroy the College along with the rest of the world. He will observe that the world is not ready for the Eye, as Ancano just demonstrated, and declare you the new Arch-Mage of the college. Two additional members of the Psijic Order will appear, surround the Eye, and then vanish in a glow of light, taking the Eye with them.

Tolfdir will then affirm that you should be the new Arch-Mage, and give you the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch-Mage%27s_Quarters_Key "Skyrim:Arch-Mage's Quarters Key") to the [Arch-Mage's Quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch-Mage%27s_Quarters "Skyrim:Arch-Mage's Quarters") and the [Archmage's Robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Archmage%27s_Robes "Skyrim:Archmage's Robes"). Everything in the Arch-Mage's Quarters becomes free to take.

## Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest and finish the questline:

-  **The Eye of Magnus** (30 points/Silver)

## Notes

- This battle is an opportunity to farm [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). Magic anomalies will spawn whenever Ancano reopens the Eye after you've closed it with the staff, which can be [soul-trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)") in addition to the filled soul gems they drop when killed. Staying close to Ancano may encourage him to open the Eye sooner than if he is allowed to keep some distance while vulnerable.
- Ancano's paralysis spell can be blocked by a ward before hitting Tolfdir like he taught during First Lessons. This will allow Tolfdir to assist in the battle.
- It may be advantageous to keep the Staff of Magnus for the quest [Aftershock](/wiki/Skyrim:Aftershock "Skyrim:Aftershock"); however, it is not required.
- Despite what might be thought otherwise, the Magic anomalies spawned during the quest are still hostile to Ancano, despite him being the one who spawns them from the Eye in the first place. He might even choose to fight them instead of you, provided they are the closer targets.

## Bugs

**Note:** This workaround may resolve some of the following bugs: Exit the college and fast travel to another city. Tolfdir should follow you there and you should get a quest update stating that you have defeated Ancano. Fast travel back to the college and speak with Tolfdir to complete the quest. If he doesn't arrive with you, simply wait (up to a day or two) for him to return.

- You may get to the Hall of Elements only to have Tolfdir run in and bypass the cutscene, making the staff useless. If this happens, you cannot harm Ancano in any way. This may be a scripting error caused by obtaining 2 staves from the quest before. Tolfdir may also fail to follow you into the Hall of Elements, which prevents the completion of the cutscene and the start of the fight. If this happens go through one of the side doors near the entrance, then come back in. Should that fail to help, fast travel elsewhere and return to Winterhold. You may have to use the staff to gain access to the college again.
  - It is also possible that closing and reopening the iron gate inside the hall helps, triggering Ancano's taunt and starting the sequence. This has been necessary in Skyrim VR. **?**
  -  If the above fails to work, disabling Tolfdir for a second might skip the sequence ahead, allowing you to attack Ancano. To do so, open the console, select Tolfdir (or type `prid 1c1a1`), then type `disable`. Now exit the console and wait for Ancanco to start his taunt. Then open the console again and `enable` Tolfdir again.
  - To prevent Tolfdir from running into the hall and engaging Ancano prematurely, enter the hall. Make sure to save your game, ideally at the barrier before using the Staff to dissipate it. Stop at the door, move forward just enough to open the inner door and trigger Ancanos dialogue. Do NOT enter the hall, move back and stay at the doorway(to skyrim). Tolfdir should move up, say his dialogue, and trigger the fight with Ancano normally. You will know it is working if Tolfdir and any follower you have with you-are paralyzed by Ancano. At this point-move forward, use the Staff on the Eye and kill Ancano. The key is NOT to move forward with Tolfdir, but remain at the doorway, this should, hopefully, resolve the invincible Ancano problem without resort to elaborate workarounds. If this fails to work, use Unrelenting Force on Tolfdir.
  -  You can get rid of the additional staff by typing `player.removeitem 00035369 1` in the console.
  -  To stop Tolfdir from running in and starting the fight prematurely, use `TDetect` which will stop either Ancano or Tolfdir from attacking each other, allowing the script to progress normally. `TDetect` can be turned back on again once the Eye of Magnus opens.`
- You may also enter to find a member of the Psijic Order already present in the hall, skipping over the cutscene between Ancano and Tolfdir, preventing Tolfdir from finishing his cutscene. This makes the quest impossible to finish. You must reload a previous save before entering the college to continue.
- You may defeat Ancano and then speak to Tolfdir. After Tofldir's scripted speech, Quaranir might not appear in the scene. **?**
  -  To fix this, use `player.placeatme 0002ba3c` in the console to make Quaranir appear. This will cause the rest of the quest to proceed as normal.
- Tolfdir may run into a corner of the entryway to the hall and will not attack Ancano. Entering the Arcanaeum and waiting for a few hours before reentering the Hall may fix this.
- Tolfdir may run in and to the left, resulting in a pillar blocking his line of sight to Ancano. He never attacks and Ancano is invulnerable. Closing the gate and using Unrelenting Shout a few times will push him from behind the pillar. He will then do his dialogue and Ancano will attack. However, Tolfdir will not help until exiting and re-entering the Hall. **?**
- You can kill Ancano without having to use the staff to make him vulnerable. It requires you to sprint ahead of Tolfdir and wait until a half second after the speeches end. At this point Ancano is vulnerable, although very briefly, and can be killed with a high-damage or critical attack. **?**
- It is possible for Arniel to enter after killing Ancano and reanimate him to fight any remaining Magical Anomalies, causing him to stand up and immediately begin fighting you again, including the fight dialogue.
- Ancano may remain invulnerable after you close the Eye. If you have the Eye closed and cannot hurt him, you may need to reload an earlier save.
- While trying equip the staff of Magnus you may get the message "You cannot equip this item". This means you cannot enter the College and the quest becomes unfinishable.
  -  To fix this, use `player.equipitem 00035369 1` in the console to force-equip the staff from your inventory.
  -  If the above command fails, use `player.additem 00035369 1` in the console to add a new staff - one that you can equip.
- After defeating Ancano and receiving the objective Talk to Tolfdir, Tolfdir may no longer be in the Hall of Elements. He can usually be found walking along the road on the other side of the mountains South of Winterhold, but will not have the dialogue option required to complete the objective, making the quest unfinishable. Reloading a previous save from before entering the Hall of Elements for the final battle may resolve this problem. **?**

| 200 | ☑ | Ancano has been defeated. The Psijic Monks have removed the Eye of Magnus from the College, saying that the world is not ready for such a thing. With the crisis over, I have been named the new Arch-Mage of the College. |

# Skyrim:The Fallen

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Main.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Main.png) | **Capture and interrogate [an ally](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing") of [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin").** |

Odahviing yoked in the trap

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)"), [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir"), *or* [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern").
2. Talk to the Jarl of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
3. Prepare a trap for [Odahviing](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing").
4. Call Odahviing to [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").
5. Weaken and trap Odahviing.
6. Interrogate Odahviing.

### The Civil War

When you have defeated [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin"), he will fly off. You must track down one of his minions to find Alduin again. Speak with [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)"), [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir"), or [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern") to proceed. When the topic is discussed, they will all tell you that [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") was once used to [capture a dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_and_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Olaf and the Dragon"). If you decide to speak with Esbern, you will start the optional quest [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)"). Go to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and speak with the [Jarl of Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater"). Depending on your progress in the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), there are several options for what can happen next:

- If the civil war has not been settled for either side, the jarl will at first be hesitant and tell you he can't capture a dragon with the ongoing war threatening his hold. You have to get both sides to agree with a truce by speaking to both [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") and [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius"). This starts the quest [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), which will now have to be completed before you can proceed with The Fallen.

- If the civil war has been settled for either the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") or the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), the jarl will allow you permission upon speaking with him. This option actually becomes possible once either side of the civil war controls at least eight of the nine Holds: if you have joined the Stormcloaks, you must have started or completed the "Liberate Haafingar" objective of [Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim"); and if you have joined the Imperials, you must have started or completed the "Regain Eastmarch" objective of [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim").

- If you choose to complete [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)") by killing him before the peace negotiations, this will anger [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir") to the point where he refuses to talk to you. However, he will still agree to host the negotiations and talk to you only for the duration of the quest. Arngeir will comment on the loss of Paarthurnax during his standoff with the Blades.

### Dragon Captive

After the peace treaty negotiations have been completed (see the quest [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") for further details), you will learn that you can use a Shout to summon a dragon, as all dragon names are Words of Power. Esbern has uncovered the name of one dragon in their records, [Odahviing](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing"). Upon telling you the name of the dragon, you will automatically learn a new [Call Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Call_Dragon "Skyrim:Call Dragon") shout. If you did not have to do Season Unending, you are instead sent to [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)"), who provides you with the same information as Esbern, including the same Call Dragon shout. At the moment you learn the shout, your journal is updated to reflect Season Unending as complete, even if you had never actually started that quest.

Go to Dragonsreach to prepare and spring the trap with the help of [Jarl Balgruuf](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") or [Jarl Vignar Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Vignar_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Vignar Gray-Mane"), depending on the current allegiance of Whiterun. The area you need to go is located behind the throne room and up the stairs (you can just follow the jarl). Tell the jarl you're ready, then use the Call Dragon shout by holding it down for a moment. Odahviing will appear after a short delay and attack, being curious to test your power. Fight him, and draw him closer to the doors you came in through using the shout Dragonrend. Climb the stairs that start near the doors, or simply back up towards the rear of the room, and a large wooden yoke will drop down and snap around his neck, holding him in place. You can then interrogate him and he will start talking to you.

He will tell you where Alduin has gone; a former temple of the [Dragon Cult](/wiki/Lore:Dragon_Cult "Lore:Dragon Cult") called [Skuldafn Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuldafn_Temple "Skyrim:Skuldafn Temple"). Interrogate him further and he will reveal to you that it is impossible to get to Skuldafn without wings, but he will take you if you release him, as he, like the other dragons, has begun to question whether Alduin is fit to lead after your earlier defeat of him. Before you accept his offer, make sure you have everything you need for a long mission, as you will not be able to leave Skuldafn until after you have completed the next three quests. You cannot take any followers with you to Skuldafn. When you are ready, talk to a guard on the upper level to release Odahviing. He will not fly away, so talk to the now-freed Odahviing for the flight to Skuldafn.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest:

-  **The Fallen** (20 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- [Farengar](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") may come out and talk with Odahviing while you have him in captivity, and attempt to collect samples, resulting in a rather humorous scene.
- The [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Call_Dragon "Skyrim:Call Dragon") button must be pressed for a slightly longer time than previous shouts required, to get the name of the dragon out and actually cause him to appear.
- When Odahviing appears, your shout cooldown, which would normally be 300 seconds, is reset to zero. Any further shouts will be subject to the normal cooldown.
- If you have a small bounty when trying to release the dragon, all the guard will say is "Wait, I know you," and no other dialogue will appear. Simply pull the release chain yourself.
- If Odahviing kills the guard that is supposed to release him, just pull the chain yourself.
- Do not attack Odahviing when he is trapped. He will not respond, but when he is released, he will become hostile again.
- Followers may keep Odahviing busy with a skirmish where he lands, preventing him from walking into the trap.
- If you have started the Stormcloaks beginning quests, but gone no further in them, you may be unable to start a conversation with Ulfric or General Tullius until you get farther along in the quest line.
- At stage 50 of the quest (defeated Alduin), the quest [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)") will begin, though it will not be displayed in your journal.

## Bugs

- Odahviing may stop moving and become invincible once you get him through the doorway.
- When Odahviing is captured, he will not talk to you. There is no option of talking to him, and he remains an enemy. This occurs after Vignar Gray-Mane has become jarl but the Companions questline has not been started. Even after becoming jarl, Vignar spends most of his time in Jorrvaskr. Simply do the first Companions mission and Vignar will leave the building. Once you get back to the Porch to summon Odahviing, Vignar will be there and the dragon will be captured properly.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- Odahviing sometimes becomes hostile after releasing him. To fix this, simply exit the Great Porch, wait a few hours inside Dragonsreach, and return to Odahviing.
- After trapping Odahviing, you may fall through the ground and in turn be stuck under the map. This seems to be caused by standing under or near Odahviing when the trap is dropped into place. To fix this, simply fast travel, then come back.
- Farengar will not appear if you have killed him, but the NPCs present will still register him as being there, trying to obtain a blood sample or some scales from Odahviing. The NPCs will say their dialogue for this scene, but Farengar not be present to speak his lines.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
- Odahviing will only fly around Dragonsreach and it'll be impossible to attack or interact with him.
  - To solve this, exit the Great Porch, wait for 20 hours, then re-enter.
  -  Alternatively, use the console to kill the guard, which triggers the next phase as if the dragon had done it himself.
- After the fight with Alduin, Paarthurnax might not land, making the first objective of speaking to him impossible. Instead of going to Arngeir or Esbern to progress, use Dragonrend on Paarthurnax. He will land and not attack you, allowing you to quickly complete this objective. **?**
- Vignar may ask you to negotiate a truce for the Civil War even if you have completed the Civil War questline. When you talk to the Greybeards, Arngeir will agree to host the negotiations, but you will never get the Season Unending objectives to talk with Tullius and Ulfric to actually trigger the negotiations. **?**
  -  After talking to Arngeir and convincing him to host the negotiations, type the console command: `setstage MQ301 40`. This will complete the objective in The Fallen to get help from the Greybeards and allow the quest to continue normally.
- Odahviing might be invincible when he first appears after you call him. This happens mostly when Vignar is the Jarl and player starts the quest after reaching a high level. **?**
  - Since he becomes unbeatable in this case, using Dragonrend shout method is a better option to trap him

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 15, 18, 20, 21, 22, 27, 40, 125, 180, 230, 240.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MQ301 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MQ301`.

# Skyrim:The Fate of the Skaal

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Main 2.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Main_2.png) | **Find a way to free the citizens of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").** |

| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Frea](/wiki/Skyrim:Frea "Skyrim:Frea") |

A protective barrier shrouds Skaal Village

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").
2. Speak with [Storn Crag-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider").
3. Travel to [Saering's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Saering%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Saering's Watch") to learn a new [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").
4. Use the new dragon shout on the [Wind Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_Stone "Skyrim:Wind Stone").
5. Return to Storn.

### Skaal Village

After your encounter with [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)") during the quest [The Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:The Temple of Miraak"), a concerned [Frea](/wiki/Skyrim:Frea "Skyrim:Frea") suggests that you follow her to [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") for advice from her father, [Storn Crag-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider"). Follow Frea to the Temple's exit and towards the village. On the way she will tell you about the [Wind Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_Stone "Skyrim:Wind Stone") and how her people are working against their will. She notes hopefully that the magical barrier around Skaal Village still stands before heading into town. In the center of the village you will find Storn and town residents [Nikulas](/wiki/Skyrim:Nikulas_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Nikulas (Dragonborn)") and [Finna](/wiki/Skyrim:Finna "Skyrim:Finna") in deep concentration, all of them maintaining the magical shield. Frea will rush right up to Storn and talk to him:

*"Father! I have returned!"*

**Frea**: *"Father! I have returned! There is yet hope! "*
**Storn**: *"Frea! What news do you bring? Is there a way to free our people?"*
**Frea**: *"No, but I have brought someone who has seen things... He/She has confirmed that Miraak is indeed behind the suffering of our people."*
**Storn**: *"I feared that it would be so."*
**Frea**: *"But how is that possible? After all this time..."*
**Storn**: *"I fear there is too much we do not yet know."*
**Frea**: (to you) *"Please, tell Storn what has happened."*

When talking to Storn, it becomes clear that creating the magical shield is weakening him and that time is short. He will also tell the tale of the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak") and how [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") burned it to the ground in a huge battle long ago. Storn will conclude that dragons never managed to kill Miraak and that he has returned. He will shrewdly point out that you managed to see Miraak through the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Waking_Dreams_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Waking Dreams (book)") and will force you to admit being Dragonborn. He admits that he doesn't yet know whether you are meant to destroy or save his people. For now, he bids you go to [Saering's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Saering%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Saering's Watch") and learn the dragon word Miraak learned long ago, in hopes you will be able to break the spell cast upon the people of [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").

### Saering's Watch

[Saering's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Saering%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Saering's Watch") is the only [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") on Solstheim and is located in the northern part of the island, between [Castle Karstaag Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Caverns "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Caverns") and [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike"). It is inhabited by several leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and a leveled [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon"). The battle can be quite hard as the enemies tend to attack in groups, so approach with caution. When all is said and done, learn the first word for the shout [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") and claim the contents from the boss-leveled chest next to the word wall.
For an easier fight you can approach from the top of the mountain, where the dragon will busy itself attacking the draugr and not you. You can kill the dragon with ranged attacks before dropping down to learn the Word of Power.

### Here in His Shrine

Skaal villagers working on the Wind Stone

Travel to the [Wind Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_Stone "Skyrim:Wind Stone"), which is located across the bridge west of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"). Seven Skaal villagers surround the Wind Stone, mindlessly performing a synchronized chant with Miraak as they build a structure around the shrine. Due to a [bug](#Bugs), this is a good time to save your game. Use [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") on the Wind Stone to free the villagers and destroy the structure surrounding the Stone. As soon as you shout, the villagers will wake up from the trance and wander aimlessly around, claiming that they have just woken up from a nightmare. Before long, a dangerous [lurker](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker") is released. Defeat it to make sure that the villagers are truly safe from harm and check the surroundings for any casualties. The villagers will then return to Skaal Village, as should you to report back to Storn.

Back in the village, Storn has lifted the magical barrier and the inhabitants have returned to their daily duties. Storn will be waiting for you and greet you happily with, *"The air is different. We are safe, which means you have succeeded."* When you tell him that his people are free he will be pleased and name you an ally of the Skaal. For the next step in weakening Miraak, he will task you with cleansing the rest of the shrines all over Solsteim, thus starting the quest [Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones"). When you inform him that you need to stop Miraak, not just weaken him, he will order you to seek out knowledge on the Black Book you found in the Temple of Miraak. He advises you to visit [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth"), a wise dark elf living in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)") who has recently visited Skaal Village and showed another Black Book to Storn. This ends the quest and starts [The Path of Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Path_of_Knowledge "Skyrim:The Path of Knowledge").

## Notes

- Activating the Wind Stone after freeing the villagers will give you the power of [North Wind](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Wind "Skyrim:North Wind") until you use it. You can activate it to get the power at most once per day.
- The North Wind power granted by the Wind Stone works underwater.
- The Wind Stone will be marked as "clear" on the map once you cleanse it.
- If you activate the Wind Stone (or any of the other [All-Maker Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:All-Maker_Stones "Skyrim:All-Maker Stones")) before it is cleansed, you will be put into the same state as the rest of the villagers. However, unlike the rest, you can exert your will and break free from the trance.
- If you have no dragon souls when you kill the dragon at Saering's Watch, and have learned (but not unlocked) the first Word of Power of Bend Will, then Miraak will not appear and steal the dragon's soul.

## Bugs

- The quest may not start after the prerequisite quest. Storn will not commence dialogue and the quest will not be given.
- The Bend Will shout may not work on the Stone, only releasing the NPCs from their trance while the Stone remains the same and no lurker appears. This prevents advancement in the quest.
  - To fix, load a previous save, use the Stone, and wait until you've heard all of Miraak's chant before using the shout.
- Sometimes when you exit the Temple of Miraak, Frea will continue to stand at the exit, even though she should be leading you to Skaal Village. **?**
  - Load the previous save data. It will be auto-saved after you exit the Temple.
- Using Bend Will on the Wind Stone before Storn asks you to may cause the quest to glitch. **?**
  - Reload a previous save and be sure to get the quest from Storn before attempting to cleanse the Stone.
- Using Bend Will on the Wind Stone might not work if you've never been to the Stone before you acquired the Bend Will shout. **?**
  - If so, travel to the Wind Stone then travel to another location of your choice then back to the Wind Stone. You'll see that the Wind Stone is now glowing green, and Bend Will may now be used to cleanse it. All Stones must be glowing for Bend Will to have any effect.
- After using Bend Will on the stone, the next objective "Defeat the Lurker" takes several seconds to appear. If you kill the Lurker before the quest update, the quest will be blocked. Reload a previous save and wait for the objective before taking down the Lurker. **?**
- Frea sometimes won't show up in Skaal Village. **?**

## Quest Stages

| The Fate of the Skaal (DLC2MQ03) | | |

| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Talk to Storn Crag-Strider |
| 30 |  | Storn, the Skaal shaman, has suggested that my experiences on Solstheim mean I am connected to Miraak. To follow the path Miraak has taken and learn what he knows, I must travel to Saering's Watch and learn the Word of Power written there. *Objective 30:* Learn Word of Power |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Talk to Storn |

I must use this new knowledge to disrupt the activity at the Wind Stone, where the Skaal are working against their will. *Objective 50:* Use the "Bend Will" Shout on the Wind Stone |

| 70 |  | The Skaal have been freed from Miraak's control, and his minion has been destroyed. Now that Storn no longer needs to focus on keeping his people safe, he may be able to tell me more about how to find and defeat Miraak. *Objective 70:* Talk to Storn |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2MQ03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2MQ03`.
