## The Frozen Hearth

Inside the Frozen Hearth

Like many other taverns in smaller settlements, The Frozen Hearth consists of a huge taproom with a fireplace in the center and the counter at the opposite end of the room from the entrance. Several wooden tables are scattered around, all of them set with food and drink. In addition to the taproom, the inn also has three smaller rooms with single beds, one of them reserved for paying customers.

To the right of the front door, in the southern corner, is the first table which is dressed with two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") on wooden plates, an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), some [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), some [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and one bottle each of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). In the corner stands a single food barrel, while a similar barrel can be found in the adjacent corner to the east. Next to the barrels are another table with two loaves of bread, and more wine and alto wine, two bottles of each. The next table is where you can find local drunk [Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") around the clock. The table in front of him is dressed with three loaves of bread, two bottles of alto wine, and one bottle of regular wine. Next up is a set of shelves with two [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), six bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and [Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah")'s Satchel, needed for the quest [Hunt and Gather](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunt_and_Gather "Skyrim:Hunt and Gather"). The last table for paying customers can be found between the entrance door and the room for rent. It is set with two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), a bottle of wine, and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread").

[Nelacar](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelacar "Skyrim:Nelacar")'s room

The bar takes up most of the northwestern part of the taproom and Dagur can be found behind the counter 24 hours a day. On display is a wedge, a slice, and a wheel of eidar cheese, and the same of goat cheese, a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), along with a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"). Hidden on the shelves underneath the counter are five gold coins, an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), six bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a copy of the book  *[Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbane%27s_Bestiary:_Ice_Wraiths "Skyrim:Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths")*. In the western corner is a set of shelves with two bottles of alto wine and six of regular wine, along with four loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). Next to the shelves are two food barrels. Hanging from the ceiling, above the stairs leading down into the basement, are seven dead [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). Hanging next to the game are a few ingredients, including two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), some [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), and some [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam").

The room you can rent is the second room along the western wall, closest to the bar, and contains a single bed, a dresser with random [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), a chest with minor loot, and a copy of *[Walking the World, vol XI](/wiki/Skyrim:Walking_the_World,_Vol_XI "Skyrim:Walking the World, Vol XI")*. The neighboring room can be used by [Eirid](/wiki/Skyrim:Eirid "Skyrim:Eirid"), [Haran](/wiki/Skyrim:Haran "Skyrim:Haran"), and [Dagur](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagur "Skyrim:Dagur"). It contains a wardrobe with clothes, a copy of *[Nords of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nords_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Nords of Skyrim")*, a chest with some loot, and a bottle of [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"). With the [Nchuanthumz: Dwarven Home](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuanthumz:_Dwarven_Home "Skyrim:Nchuanthumz: Dwarven Home") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, *[Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts' Journal, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts%27_Journal,_v1 "Skyrim:Seeks-Ancient-Artifacts' Journal, v1")* can be found on the table in this room. Adjacent to these two rooms is another room, reserved for permanent resident and former [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") member, the wizard [Nelacar](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelacar "Skyrim:Nelacar"). It seems like he has been living there for quite some time and it resembles a small trading room, complete with a counter with a copy of the rare tome *[Words of Clan Mother Ahnissi](/wiki/Skyrim:Words_of_Clan_Mother_Ahnissi "Skyrim:Words of Clan Mother Ahnissi")* and two bottles of alto wine on display. On the shelves underneath the counter is the [staff of arcane authority](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Arcane_Authority "Skyrim:Staff of Arcane Authority") used for the quest [Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft"). Behind the counter is a set of shelves with Nelecar's personal library, several books on [Daedra](/wiki/Lore:Daedra "Lore:Daedra"), and a single bottle of alto wine. In the southeastern corner sits his owned bed with an empty chest at the foot. In the corner is a chair where Nelecar usually sits, and a table with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a medium coin purse, and four gold coins.

## The Frozen Hearth Cellar

The Frozen Hearth Cellar

Down the stairs from the taproom is the cellar where [Dagur](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagur "Skyrim:Dagur")'s wife [Haran](/wiki/Skyrim:Haran "Skyrim:Haran") sleeps next to their child, [Eirid](/wiki/Skyrim:Eirid "Skyrim:Eirid"). The door opens to the sight of three food barrels and a huge amount of cobwebs, hinting at the decline of Winterhold. In the sleeping area are two owned beds, one single and one double, whereas Eirid sleeps in the single bed, next to a basket with five [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"). In the corner is an end table with clutter, with two bottles of alto wine on top. At the foot of the double bed is a chest. In the corner sits another end table with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on top and, on the floor, four food sacks. There is also a wardrobe with some random [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing") and another food barrel. In the center of the sleeping area is a dinner table set with a healthy amount of food, including three [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), three green apples, an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), two [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), a wedge of [goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and two bottles of regular [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). Adjacent to the dinner table is a storage area with several inactive crates and three food sacks and, wedged between a crate and a pillar, the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") skill book *[The Exodus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Exodus "Skyrim:The Exodus")*. In the other end of the room, behind the empty table, are three more food sacks and a food barrel.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the Frozen Hearth's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 4 | [Honningbrew Meads](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") |
| 7 | Random [drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") |
| 10 | Random inn [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") |
| 1 | [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |

## Notes

- If you infect Haran with vampirism during the [New Allegiances](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Allegiances "Skyrim:New Allegiances")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") quest, a coffin will appear in the westernmost corner of the cellar and can be used to sleep and get the vampire rested bonus. Haran does not seem to use it however, and will still sleep in her old bed.
- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* mentions a character by the name of **Angwe** living here, although no such person exists, and is never even mentioned. There isn't even a trace of them to be found in the game data.

## Bugs

- Eirid's bed in the Cellar is scaled down too far, causing her to float above it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- If Haran becomes the publican here, she may not be seen standing behind the counter.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, addresses this issue. The two counter leaning markers used by the innkeeper faction were only owned by Dagur, so Haran could never use them.
- The staff may respawn an infinite number of times if you steal it, allowing you to fence it over and over again. **?**

# Skyrim:The Gardener of Men

## Overview

|  |  |

The Black Book, Epistolary Acumen

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the Black Book *[Epistolary Acumen](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Epistolary_Acumen_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Epistolary Acumen (book)")*.
2. Explore the book and learn the second word of the [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").
3. Defeat [Krosulhah](/wiki/Skyrim:Krosulhah "Skyrim:Krosulhah").
4. Talk to [Storn](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").
5. Learn the final word of Bend Will.

### Chapter I

The path opens

By reading the Black Book *[Epistolary Acumen](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Epistolary_Acumen_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Epistolary Acumen (book)")*, you are transported to the realm of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora"), [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(Epistolary_Acumen) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (Epistolary Acumen)").

If this is your first trip (not counting the one where you first meet [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)")), Hermaeus Mora will appear, floating above the platform as a tentacled eyeball. He will speak to you of Apocrypha's seductive wealth of knowledge.

Chapter I opens on a small platform. As is common in Apocrypha, if you approach the edges, tentacles may reach out of the water and whip you. Activate the scrye at the platform's center to lower a bridge to a moving corridor. Jump onto the moving passage, taking care not to fall into the dark water. The parts of the bridge that bend actually have porous walls; if you do not actively move with the bridge's flexing, you'll pass through these walls and drop into the poisonous water. Hop off at the platform on the far right, then activate a second scrye and lower a second bridge. Jump back into the moving passage and ride it back to that bridge. Read the book on the pedestal here to access Chapter II.

### Chapter II

Travel down the narrow pathway and activate another scrye. The corridor will unfurl to become the floor of a room, where you battle a [lurker](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker") and a couple of [seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker"). Once they are dealt with, activate a scrye on the eastern side of the room in order to open up the large gate to the west. To the southeast is a pod you can loot. Through the gate, to your right is another pod, and right in front of you is Chapter III.

### Chapter III

The start of Chapter III

Follow the pathway around and up several sets of stairs, eliminating the seekers as you go. To the left of your entry point, there is a font of magicka surrounded by a pool of poisonous water that will restore your magicka reserves. There is another one located at the top of the stairs, where you will also encounter a moving tunnel similar to the one encountered in Chapter I.

If you choose to get off at the closest platform, you will be greeted by a lurker, and two seekers will fire at you from a platform below. Drop down the far side of the lurker's platform to kill them, then activate a scrye around a corner to the southwest in order to return to the starting platform. The last and farthest platform contains two seekers and a pod full of loot, with a font of magicka hanging on either side. You will find there three skill books: [Death Blow of Abernanit](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Blow_of_Abernanit "Skyrim:Death Blow of Abernanit"), [Fire and Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_and_Darkness "Skyrim:Fire and Darkness"), and [Orsinium and the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orsinium_and_the_Orcs "Skyrim:Orsinium and the Orcs"); as well as a [Conjure Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Seeker "Skyrim:Conjure Seeker") spell tome.

Chapter III & IV

To reach Chapter IV, do not jump on the platforms. Instead, activate the scrye at the end of the moving passage to open the gate, and defeat any seekers that appear as you move forward. As soon as you reach the end of the next passage, it will move to the left and a bridge will lower, leading to a lurker. At the end of the path, there will be another move to the left, and you will approach the gates you activated before, but this time from the left side. Activate the scrye to open them again and continue on, avoiding the tentacles that reach out at you from the water. Eliminate the seekers as you walk down the path to Chapter IV.

### Chapter IV

A Daedric Prince wants to make a deal

Be prepared to move quickly; you may spawn in this level standing in a pool of the poison fluid. You may recognize the location below the platform as the setting of Chapter III. Loot the vessel to the left and activate the scrye. The large capsule containing the *Black Book: Epistolary Acumen* will open. Walk up to the Book and read it to summon Hermaeus Mora.

The following dialogue is dependent on the status of the quest [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane"). If the quest has been completed, Hermaeus Mora greets you in one of two ways:

:   - **If you respected Mora before:** *"Well done, my champion. Your journey towards enlightenment has finally led you here, to my realm, as I knew it would."*
    - **If you disrespected Mora before:** *"You thought to reject me, and yet here you are. Your journey towards enlightenment has finally led you here, to my realm, as I knew it would.*"

This presents two possible replies:

:   - **What do you want of me this time?:** *"You have entered my realm. You have sought out the forbidden knowledge that only one other has obtained. You are Dragonborn, like Miraak before you. A seeker of knowledge and power."*
    - **What do you want of me, my lord?:** *"Your progress since obtaining my Oghma Infinium has been rapid. And now, I find you here, following in my servant Miraak's footsteps. You also are Dragonborn. You also seek to learn how to bend the world to your will."*

Alternatively, if Discerning the Transmundane has not yet been completed, he will simply greet you with: *"All seekers of knowledge come to my realm, sooner or later."* Either way, the following set of dialogue choices becomes available, where he reveals that you cannot hope to surpass Miraak without the last word of power:

:   - **Yes, I came here to learn Miraak's secrets:** *"All that he knows he learned from me."*
    - **I won't serve you, monster. I just want to defeat Miraak:** *"You will serve me, willing or not. All who seek after the secrets of the world are my servants."*
    - **I don't need your help. I'll learn Miraak's secrets on my own:** *"No, look around. You have done nothing here on your own. You could spend a hundred lifetimes searching my library, and you will never find what you seek."*
    - **Tell me what you want my lord, and I will bring it to you:** *"You please me champion. Your loyalty will be richly rewarded. The Skaal have withheld their secrets from me for many long years. The time has come for this knowledge to be added to my library."*

Regardless of what option is chosen, Hermaeus Mora ends with: *"I know what you want: to use your power as Dragonborn to bend the world to your will. Here then is the knowledge you need, although you did not know you needed it. The second Word of Power. Use it to bend the wills of mortals to your purpose. But this is not enough. Miraak knows the final Word of Power. Without that, you cannot hope to surpass him. Miraak served me well, and he was rewarded. I can grant you the same power as he wields, but all knowledge has its price."*

Next, he reveals his price for the Word of Power, knowledge for knowledge:

:   - **Tell me what you want my lord, and I will bring it to you:** *"You please me champion. Your loyalty will be richly rewarded. The Skaal have withheld their secrets from me for many long years. The time has come for this knowledge to be added to my library."*
    - **So what's your price for the final Word of Power?:** *"Knowledge for knowledge. The Skaal have withheld their secrets from me for many long years. The time has come for this knowledge to be added to my library."*
    - **Why do I need this Word of Power to defeat Miraak?:** *"Even dragons submit to Miraak's Voice. Without that power, you cannot face him. So say I, Hermaeus Mora, master of the Tides of fate."*
    - **Isn't Miraak your ally? Why help me defeat him?:** *"He has served me long and well. But he grows restless under my guidance. His desire to return to your world will spread my influence more widely. But it will also set him free from my direct control. It may be time to replace him with a more loyal servant. One who still appreciates the gifts I have to offer."*

After this section, the conversation ends with the following set of options:

:   - **I will talk to the Skaal and bring you their secrets:** *"I know you will. And then I will give you the knowledge that you seek."*
    - **I will do as you command, my lord:** *"Yes, I know. And then Miraak's power will be yours as well."*
    - **What if the Skaal refuse to give up their secrets?:** *"My servant Miraak would have found a way to bring me what I want. So will you if you wish to surpass him."*
    - **How do I know I can trust you, demon?:** *"My word is as true as fate, as inevitable as destiny. Bring me what I want, and I will give you what you seek."*

Regardless of what option is chosen, Hermaeus Mora parts with: *"Send the Skaal shaman to me. He holds the secrets that will be mine."*, referring to [Storn Crag-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider").

Just before Hermaeus Mora fades away, he teaches you the second word to [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will"). After this, you may choose from one of three powers emanating from the Black Book:

- [Dragonborn Flame](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Flame "Skyrim:Dragonborn Flame") — When your [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath") shout kills an enemy, a [Fire Wyrm](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Wyrm "Skyrim:Fire Wyrm") emerges from the corpse to fight for you for 60 seconds.
- [Dragonborn Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Force "Skyrim:Dragonborn Force") — Your [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout does more damage and may disintegrate enemies.
- [Dragonborn Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Frost "Skyrim:Dragonborn Frost") — Your [Frost Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Breath "Skyrim:Frost Breath") shout encases foes in ice.

Only one ability from the book may be accepted at a time. To return to Solstheim, use the Black Book in front of you or access it from your inventory.

### Return to Solstheim

*"What happened? What did you see?"*

Krosulhah attacking upon your exit

After reading the book, you are returned to [Nchardak](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchardak "Skyrim:Nchardak"), where [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") will approach and ask: *"What happened? What did you see? Different people have very different experiences when reading these books."*

You can give him two possible answers:

:   - **I talked to Hermaeus Mora:** *"You're still acting surprisingly sane, too. What did he have to say? He must have wanted something from you."*
    - **I learned the second Word of the Bend Will shout:** *"No wonder the Dwemer were so interested in that book. It was indeed one that Miraak used to advance his power as Dragonborn. But I assume there's some bad news? It would be unlike Hermaeus Mora to allow anyone to gain such knowledge without exacting a price."*

If you explain to Neloth that Hermaeus Mora wants the "secrets of the Skaal" in exchange for the third word, Neloth replies: *"Hmph. What secrets could they have worth keeping from old Mora? Sounds like a bargain to me. Hermaeus Mora learns some fascinating new ways to skin a horker and you become the second most powerful Dragonborn that ever lived. Well, that gives me a lot to think about. I need to get back to Tel Mithryn. I have some ideas about how to locate more of these Black Books..."*

Alternatively, should you die within Apocrypha before speaking to Hermaeus Mora, a different option is presented:

:   **I found myself in another place:** *"That's a fairly common experience, at least for those who remain coherent enough to report what they've seen. You were in Apocrypha. Or at least your consciousness was - your body remained here of course. You should read the book again until you reach what appears to be the "end" - then you will have fully understood the knowledge it contains."*

After this, if you return to Apocrypha and come back, Neloth will ask with skepticism: *"Did you actually learn what you needed to know by reading that black book?"*

Regardless, when Neloth leaves, you can go back downstairs for the five cubes, which have a base value of 50 gold; they are just minor loot at this point.

After exiting Nchardak, it is revealed that Miraak has sent a dragon named [Krosulhah](/wiki/Skyrim:Krosulhah "Skyrim:Krosulhah") to ambush you. He hovers above the ruins and bellows: *"Miraak has commanded your death. So it shall be."* before attacking. Fight and defeat him, and once he is dead, travel to the [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") and talk to Storn, who can be found meditating outside his hut.

### The Secrets of the Skaal

*"So it falls to me to be the one to give up the secrets to our ancient enemy."*

If you have yet to cleanse the [All-Maker Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:All-Maker_Stones "Skyrim:All-Maker Stones"), Storn will say that he is too weak to face Hermaeus Mora, as the Oneness of the land is disrupted. You will need to complete the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones") to restore the shaman's connection to the All-Maker before he will agree to help you.

Once the Sacred Stones have been cleansed, return to Storn and ask him about the secrets of the Skaal, to which he replies: *"Hermaeus Mora... old Herma-Mora himself. So he is the source of Miraak's power. Of course. We have many tales of Herma-Mora trying to trick us into giving up our secrets to him. And now he comes again for what we have long kept from him."*

Next, three optional questions become available, each of which give additional insight into the relationship between the Skaal and Hermaeus Mora:

:   - **What are the "secrets of the Skaal"?:** *"Ancient lore, handed down from shaman to shaman since the All-Maker first gave Solstheim to the Skaal. How to talk to the wind, how to listen to the earth - these are our secrets. Nothing of power or mastery."*
    - **Why would Hermaeus Mora want your secrets?:** *"We know him as Herma-Mora, the Demon of Knowledge. It is in his nature to hoard secrets to himself. Their value to him is of no consequence. The very fact that the Skaal have kept knowledge from him has merely increased his desire to have it."*
    - **Herma-Mora? Why do you call him that?:** *"That is our name for him - the Demon of knowledge. He has always been our enemy."*

Back to the matter at hand, the following set of options are presented:

:   **He said it's the only way he'll teach me the final Word of Miraak's Shout:**

:   | Storn's Reply | Condition |
    | --- | --- |
    | *"So it falls to me to be the one to give up the secrets to our ancient enemy. I do not know if I have the strength to face him. The Tree Stone is still corrupted... the land is still out of balance. But with the other five restored... it may be enough. It will have to do."* | [Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones") is complete |
    | *"So it falls to me to be the one to give up the secrets to our ancient enemy. I do not know if I have the strength to face him. With Miraak's corruption of the Stones... the Oneness of the land is disrupted, and our connection to the All-Maker is broken."* | [Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones") is incomplete |

:   **You mean you'll give him what he wants?:**
:   *"Yes. The Skaal also tell of the day when we must finally give up our secrets. When Herma-Mora finally wins. As shaman, it is my duty to guard these secrets, but also to decide when it is necessary to give them up. I believe that time is now. If I am wrong, may my ancestors forgive me. Give me the book. I will read it, and speak to old Herma-Mora myself. I will make sure he lives up to his part of the bargain."*

:   **I hope you know what you're doing. (Give book):**
:   *"That is my hope as well. I am trusting you will make this sacrifice worthwhile."*

*"Father, you must not do this. That book is... wrong. Evil."*

When you hand him the book he will walk into the center of the village, while Frea will shout:

:   |  |  |
    | --- | --- |
    | **Frea:** | *"Father, you must not do this. That book is... wrong. Evil. Against everything that you have taught me my whole life."* |
    | **Storn:** | *"I must, Frea. It is the only way to free Solstheim forever from Miraak's shadow. There comes a time when everything must change. Nothing that lives remains the same forever. Do not fear for me, my daughter. This is the destiny that the All-Maker has laid out for me."* |
    | **Frea:** | *"I stand beside you, father, as always."* |
    | **Storn:** | *"I am ready for whatever the foul master of this book has in store for me."* |

*"You... liar... gah! ... I won't... not... for you..."*

While seemingly unconvinced about Hermaeus Mora's intentions and promises, Storn then opens the book. Seconds after, several tentacles shoot out from its pages and grab him, one of them piercing into his brain, while Mora gloats: *"At last, the Skaal yield up their secrets to me."* While the secrets of the Skaal are drained out of him, all Storn can utter is: *"You... liar... gah! ... I won't... not... for you..."*

Hermaeus Mora will then speak to you: *"Dragonborn, you have delivered me the gift I requested. In return, I keep my promise, as befits a Prince of Oblivion: I give you the Word of Power that you need to challenge Miraak. You will be either a worthy opponent or his successor, as the tides of fate decree."* When you finally receive your gift, Mora will let go of Storn who will shout: *"Nooo!"* and fall to the ground, dead.

Frea will rush to her father's lifeless body and cry out: *"Father! What have you done!"* She will then look directly at you: *"Go. My father sacrificed himself so that you could destroy Miraak and lift his master's shadow from the land. Go, then. Kill Miraak. Do not fail."*

If you don't take *[Epistolary Acumen](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Epistolary_Acumen_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Epistolary Acumen (book)")* back from [Storn Crag-Strider's](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider") body, [Frea](/wiki/Skyrim:Frea "Skyrim:Frea") will give it to you after you complete [At the Summit of Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha").

She will then stay by her father, while all the citizens of Skaal Village pay their final respect to their old shaman:

*"We won't forget what you did for us, Storn Crag-Strider."*

:   **Fanari Strong-Voice:** *"Goodbye, old friend. We will miss you, but do not worry. Frea will guide us well, thanks to you."*
:   **Edla:** *"We won't forget what you did for us, Storn Crag-Strider. Walk with the All-Maker."*
:   **Deor Woodcutter:** *"Frea... I'm sorry."*
:   **Aeta:** *"It can't be... please, All-Maker, send him back to us..."*
:   **Baldor Iron-Shaper:** *"I... uh... you'll be missed, old man."*
:   **Finna:** *"May the All-Maker guide your soul to the next life."*
:   **Nikulas:** *"Frea... what happened? What was that thing? I thought the village was safe now."*
:   **Wulf Wild-Blood:** *"Return to the All-Maker, old one. The Skaal will never forget your sacrifice."*
:   **Morwen:** *"I don't really understand what you did, but I trust you did it for the good of the village. So... thank you."*
:   **Tharstan:** *"By the gods... I've never seen anything like it... I, uh... I don't think this will go in my book."*

This ends the quest, and starts [At the Summit of Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha").

## Notes

- The name of this quest is taken from the Hermaeus Mora section of a [Michael Kirkbride](/wiki/General:Michael_Kirkbride "General:Michael Kirkbride") text called the *[Imperial Census of Daedra Lords](http://www.imperial-library.info/content/imperial-census-daedra-lords)*.
- If this is your first time entering Apocrypha, and you have previously encountered Hermaeus Mora during [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane"), he will recognize your previous encounter by saying, *"I know you, champion. The [Oghma Infinium](/wiki/Skyrim:Oghma_Infinium "Skyrim:Oghma Infinium") was only the beginning."*
- During the conversation with Hermaeus Mora at the end of Epistolary Acumen, if you choose "What do you want of me, my lord" at the beginning of the conversation, you will not be able to pick the option "Tell me what you want my lord, and I will bring it to you" in the next choice, instead it will only appear at the end of conversation.
- You may return to the previous chapters at any time during the quest by reading the book located behind each starting position.
- If you are having any problems with the tunnels that whip from side to side, make sure to strafe; this will prevent you from 'falling' through the tunnel floor. And if you do fall, look around; sometimes you are near enough land to save yourself before your health depletes all the way.

## Bugs

- When Storn is supposed to read the Black Book, he may instead just stand still and comment about being in the hands of the All-Maker.
  - Talking to Frea may fix this bug.
- Storn may continually be attacked by Hermaeus Mora through the book, but the quest will not progress.
  - This may be related to losing Frea. [*verification needed — What are the conditions for this bug?*]
- You may not be able to read the Black Book after talking to Hermaeus Mora at the end of Chapter IV to either get one of the three powers or return to Solstheim.
  - Attacking the book with a spell (such as fireball) has been shown to open up the three force bubbles and make the book readable. [*verification needed — What are the conditions for this bug?*]
- You may be unable to move after talking to Hermaeus Mora in Chapter IV
- You may not be able to continue dialogue when interacting with the Black Book if you have the craft/object interaction bug.
  - If you are encountering the crafting/object interaction bug, you may be unable to follow the dialogue when interacting with the Black Book [Epistolary Acumen](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Epistolary_Acumen_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Epistolary Acumen (book)"). Reloading to a save prior to having this bug may fix it. Another fix is to interact with the book, and while Hermaeus Mora is appearing to open the console and enter '*coc DLC2Book02DungeonNEW*". This will spawn you at the entrance of the dungeon and continue the dialogue. You will need to backtrack back to the black book.

## Quest Stages

| The Gardener of Men (DLC2MQ05) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | With Neloth's help, I gained access to the Black Book in Nchardak. Now to read it and learn more of Miraak's knowledge. *Objective 10:* Read the Black Book |
| 100 |  | *Objective 20:* Learn the hidden knowledge of "Epistolary Acumen" |
| 340 |  | With Neloth's help, I gained access to the Black Book in Nchardak. I read it and was transported to Hermaeus Mora's realm of Apocrypha, where I found the book's counterpart. Hermaeus Mora himself appeared and taught me the second Word of "Bend Will". He has promised to teach me the third Word but only in return for "the secrets of the Skaal." *Objective 30:* Talk to Storn |
| 500 |  | *Objective 40:* Wait for Storn to read the book |
| 1000 | ☑ | With Neloth's help, I gained access to the Black Book in Nchardak. I read it and was transported to Hermaeus Mora's realm of Apocrypha, where I found the book's counterpart. Hermaeus Mora himself appeared and taught me the second Word of Bend Will. He promised to teach me the third Word but only if in return for "the secrets of the Skaal." The Skaal shaman Storn agreed to give Hermaeus Mora what he wanted, but when Storn read the book, Hermaeus Mora killed him while teaching me the promised Word of Power. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 150, 200, 250, 290, 300, 310, 320, 325, 330, 350, 355, 360, 370, 390, 400, 450, 600, 610, 620, 630, 700, 750, 800, 1100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2MQ05 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2MQ05`.

# Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Put an [ancient ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") to rest.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Eydis](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis "Skyrim:Eydis") |
| Location(s): | [Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn"), random dungeon |
| Reward: | +1 in [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") and [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Eydis](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis "Skyrim:Eydis")) |
| ID: | FreeformOldHroldanB |

*"I've been waiting for you."*

This article is about the character. For Ghost of Old Hroldan, see The Ghost of Old Hroldan.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Sleep at the [Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn").
2. Speak to the ghost that appears.
3. Speak with [Eydis](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis "Skyrim:Eydis").
4. Go to the random dungeon and recover [Hjalti's Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjalti%27s_Sword "Skyrim:Hjalti's Sword").
5. Return the sword to the ghost for free training in [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") and [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block").

## Detailed Walkthrough

***"Hjalti was a shrewd tactician, and his small band of Colovian troops and Nord berserkers broke the Reachman line, forcing them back beyond the gates of Old Hrol'dan. A siege seemed impossible, as Hjalti could expect no reinforcements from Falkreath."***

### Tiber Septim's Bed

[Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn"), the remote inn along the shores of [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River") in [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), holds an important place in history, at least according to innkeeper, [Eydis](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis "Skyrim:Eydis"). As soon as you enter the taproom she will claim, *"Old Hroldan is the stone that the Empire's history is built on"* and will then ask if you want to rent [Tiber Septim](/wiki/Lore:Tiber_Septim "Lore:Tiber Septim")'s bed. When asked to elaborate Eydis will provide a lengthy description on the historical importance of Old Hroldan. She will explain the location marks Tiber Septim's first victorious battle when he liberated the area from barbarians during the Second Era. According to history, the victorious general then spent the night at the inn and his bed is still there, as good as new. Eydis charges a meager ten gold for renting out the venerable bed, so accept the offer and follow her to the room. Note the [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Battle of Sancre Tor](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Sancre_Tor "Skyrim:Battle of Sancre Tor")* on the nightstand, then go to bed.

### Ghost of Old Hroldan

*"You promised me, Hjalti."*

When you wake up, you will hear Eydis scream in terror as the inn has received an unexpected visitor, namely the [Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan"). An alarmed Eydis will tell tales about Old Hroldan being haunted, but will not have definitive answers about the ghost or his purpose. Instead, go talk to the ghost who will confuse you with someone else:

*"Hjalti? Is that you? I've been waiting."*
*"I fought by your side. To take back the Reach from the savages."*
*"Do you remember me now, Hjalti?"*

When asked about why he is referring to you as 'Hjalti' he will remind you that the two of you fought together to free Hroldan, and that you promised to be his sworn brother. He then explains that he has waited an eternity for the sword that will fulfill the promise, but will not reveal anything else.

### Hjalti's Sword

Ask Eydis about the sword, and once again, she knows her history. She will recall a legend about Tiber Septim attacking a camp right before heading to Hroldan. Her guess is that the sword will be at the camp. She will then mark a random location on your map, choosing from the following list:

**Possible Locations**: [Broken Tower Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt") • [Bruca's Leap Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bruca%27s_Leap_Redoubt "Skyrim:Bruca's Leap Redoubt") • [Deepwood Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt") • [Dragon Bridge Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge_Overlook "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge Overlook") • [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt") • [Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt") • [Red Eagle Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Redoubt "Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt") • [Serpent's Bluff Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Serpent%27s_Bluff_Redoubt "Skyrim:Serpent's Bluff Redoubt")

If asked further, Eydis will speculate on the name 'Hjalti' and guess that it was one of the many names of Tiber Septim. She suggests that the ghost is one of Tiber Septim's dead soldiers.

### Sworn Brothers

Luckily, Eydis' map marker will show you all the way to the boss-leveled chest in the depths of the random location. Once you have [Hjalti's Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjalti%27s_Sword "Skyrim:Hjalti's Sword") return to Old Hroldan Inn and present the sword to the ghost. He will be most honored to become your 'sworn brother' after hundreds of years and reward you with a few lessons from the sword masters of [Alcaire](/wiki/Lore:Alcaire "Lore:Alcaire"): a one-point bonus to your [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") and [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") skills. He will then disappear into thin air, confident that you travel along with him.

***"That night a storm came and visited Hjalti's camp. It spoke with him in his tent. At dawn, Hjalti went up to the gates, and the storm followed just above his head. Arrows could not penetrate the winds around him. He shouted down the walls of Old Hrol'dan, and his men poured in. After their victory, the Nords called Hjalti Talos, or Stormcrown."***

## Notes

- A single internal name for a dialogue topic with Eydis, called `FreeformOldHroldanBCuhlecainBranch`, implies that at one point, the Ghost might've been meant to see you as [Cuhlecain](/wiki/Lore:Cuhlecain "Lore:Cuhlecain"), rather than Hjalti Early-Beard.
- It is possible to acquire Hjalti's Sword in one of the potential spawn zones even before sleeping at Old Hroldan and starting the quest. The sword is flagged as a quest item until it is turned in.
- After the quest is finished, Eydis will comment on the ghost's disappearance.
- For more information about Hjalti and the Battle of Old Hrol'dan, see *[The Arcturian Heresy](/wiki/Lore:The_Arcturian_Heresy "Lore:The Arcturian Heresy")*.

## Bugs

- Eydis may still behave as though she has seen the ghost even after the quest has been completed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- Despite the "Say Once" flag, Eydis may repeat her initial line about being frightened by the ghost even after the quest is finished.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.4, fixes this bug.
- If [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") is set to transport you to the [Abandoned Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack") while this one is about to begin, this quest may be interrupted and potentially broken by the kidnapping scene.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, addresses this issue. The fact that these happen to be the only two quests in the vanilla game that require you to sleep is likely why this went unnoticed for so long.

## Quest Stages

| The Ghost of Old Hroldan (FreeformOldHroldanB) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Bring Hjalti's Sword to the Ghost of Old Hroldan |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5, 10, 15, 100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformOldHroldanB stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformOldHroldanB`.

# Skyrim:The Gift

## Overview

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | Your spouse should be non-vampire | | ← Previous | [The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony") (Finish [The Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice") first) | | |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Do a few side missions for the vampires (must have a spouse).
2. Speak to [Vingalmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Vingalmo "Skyrim:Vingalmo") to ask to help out.
3. Use [Vampire's Seduction](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Seduction "Skyrim:Vampire's Seduction") on your spouse and feed.
4. Return to Vingalmo.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After a few side missions with the vampires, you will be directed to [Vingalmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Vingalmo "Skyrim:Vingalmo") (if you have a spouse as a mortal). He will talk about how he knows you have a spouse and then set you off on a quest to give your spouse [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon")'s gift.

## Notes

- Your spouse will not gain any vampiric abilities; completing the quest will only change their eye color.
- This quest will not be offered if you are married to any of the following people:

:   |  |  |  |  |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") [Argis the Bulwark](/wiki/Skyrim:Argis_the_Bulwark "Skyrim:Argis the Bulwark") [Athis](/wiki/Skyrim:Athis "Skyrim:Athis") [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund") [Benor](/wiki/Skyrim:Benor "Skyrim:Benor") [Borgakh the Steel Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Borgakh_the_Steel_Heart "Skyrim:Borgakh the Steel Heart") [Cosnach](/wiki/Skyrim:Cosnach "Skyrim:Cosnach") | [Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus") [Dravynea the Stoneweaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_the_Stoneweaver "Skyrim:Dravynea the Stoneweaver") [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol") [Jenassa](/wiki/Skyrim:Jenassa "Skyrim:Jenassa") [Octieve San](/wiki/Skyrim:Octieve_San "Skyrim:Octieve San") [Omluag](/wiki/Skyrim:Omluag "Skyrim:Omluag") | [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") [Perth](/wiki/Skyrim:Perth "Skyrim:Perth") [Romlyn Dreth](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth") [Scouts-Many-Marshes](/wiki/Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes "Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes") [Shahvee](/wiki/Skyrim:Shahvee "Skyrim:Shahvee") [Sondas Drenim](/wiki/Skyrim:Sondas_Drenim "Skyrim:Sondas Drenim") [Stenvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Stenvar "Skyrim:Stenvar") | [Torvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Torvar "Skyrim:Torvar") [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") [Viola Giordano](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano "Skyrim:Viola Giordano") [Vorstag](/wiki/Skyrim:Vorstag "Skyrim:Vorstag") |

- Your spouse will turn hostile if you turn into a vampire lord in front of them.
- There is a chance you'll accidentally make your spouse a vampire by feeding from them while they sleep, before actually receiving the quest. This makes them hostile and triggers the quest with a blank description, with the instruction to return to [Vingalmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Vingalmo "Skyrim:Vingalmo").
- It is advised *not* to turn your spouse if they are a follower and currently following you, as they will turn hostile to you as soon as the Vampire's Seduction wears off. Part ways with them first at your house, get the quest, then turn them at your home and quickly leave, otherwise they still will turn hostile if you linger after the seduction power wanes.
- You can also skip this quest, if spouse are already as a Vampire, if you married by using console commands

## Bugs

- The actual dialogue does not match up with subtitles after the spouse is turned into a vampire.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.
- If your spouse is reserved for use in another quest, this quest will not run until the other one completes. In some cases, this may mean the quest will never run at all, since some reservations are permanent.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.
- Even when you turn your spouse into a vampire, they will not be detectable by the [Detect Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Undead "Skyrim:Detect Undead") spell and will still be affected by the [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") spell.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- The spouse's eyes may remain unchanged.
- Sometimes if you speak to your spouse before using Vampire's Seduction on them, you may not be given the option to feed on them. **?**
  - Reload to a previous save and use Vampire's Seduction on your spouse before speaking to them to fix this.
- If you turn Senna into a vampire, her eyes may disappear. **?**

## Quest Stages

I should first render <Alias.PronounObj=Spouse> pliant through the use of Vampire's Seduction then embrace and bite <Alias.PronounObj=Spouse> on the neck. If I currently lack the power, I should forego feeding for a day as I will gain the ability. I should then return to Vingalmo while <Alias=Spouse> undergoes the change. *Objective 10:* Mesmerize and turn <Alias=Spouse> into a vampire. |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Return to Vingalmo |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 50, 70.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1RV06 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1RV06`.

# Skyrim:The Golden Claw

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **A [shopkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius") wants you to retrieve his [prized possession](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw") from a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvel_the_Swift "Skyrim:Arvel the Swift").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Lucan Valerius](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius") *or* Overheard from bandits during Bleak Falls Barrow quest |
| Location(s): | [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)") |
| Reward: | Leveled Gold, Word for the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Lucan Valerius](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius")) =1 ([Camilla Valerius](/wiki/Skyrim:Camilla_Valerius "Skyrim:Camilla Valerius")) |
| ID: | MS13 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | |  | **Concurrent** [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Concurrent | [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)") | | |

Back where it belongs!

## Quick Walkthrough

1. *(Optional)* Find [Lucan Valerius](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius") at the [Riverwood Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood_Trader "Skyrim:Riverwood Trader") and talk to him.
2. Retrieve the [golden claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw") from [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)").
3. Find the secret of Bleak Falls Barrow.
4. Return the claw to Lucan.

**Note**: The events of this quest are closely related to those in the quest [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)"), at times taking over important objectives. It can be triggered right after entering Riverwood, but it is recommended to follow the intended path and initiate the Bleak Falls Barrow quest in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). Otherwise, you may miss a few story-related events and details. See [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest)#Notes "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)") for details.

### A Stolen Ornament

In Riverwood, you may hear concerned townsfolk talk about a recent robbery at Riverwood Trader. When you pay a visit to the store you will find proprietor Lucan Valerius and his sister [Camilla](/wiki/Skyrim:Camilla_Valerius "Skyrim:Camilla Valerius") in the middle of a hefty argument, both of them frustrated with recent events. Talking to Camilla will not help much, while Lucan will be more informative, although puzzled: *"Yes, we did have a bit of a... break-in. But we still have plenty to sell. Robbers were only after one thing. An ornament, solid gold. In the shape of a dragon's claw."* If you offer to help him get the claw back, he will offer a gold reward and will then continue debating with Camilla. She will argue that you may need a pointer in the right direction and will then get up and leave. Follow her outside and she will point out [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)"), barely visible in the distance behind [Alvor and Sigrid's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor_and_Sigrid%27s_House "Skyrim:Alvor and Sigrid's House"), and lead you to the bridge northeast of town. She will provide some sparse directions, but follow her advice and pick the northwestern trail up the mountain. At this point, make sure you have the [concurrent quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)") in your journal. If not, you can go to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and activate it.

If you don't want to go through the introduction at Riverwood Trader, go straight to Bleak Falls Barrow and you will receive the quest when you overhear two bandits in the first room.

### Retrieving the Claw

*"Cut me down before that thing gets us!"*

When you arrive at [Bleak Falls Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Temple "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Temple"), you may overhear two bandits talking about a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") that's gone on ahead. If you did not speak to Valerius in Riverwood, this moment serves as the start of the quest. After killing these two bandits and progressing further into the barrow, you will see another bandit approaching a gate. Upon activating the lever for the gate, the bandit is killed by [poisonous darts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") and the gate remains closed, blocking your progress. Notice the broken piece of rock next to the lever. It has the image of a snake. Notice the [spinning symbols](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Symbol "Skyrim:Spinning Symbol") behind you to the left. These rocks must be rotated to the correct position to activate the lever. Look up to see the carvings on the wall that denote the correct sequence: *Snake, Snake, Whale*. (The middle rock has fallen off the wall and onto the ground, hence the snake being the right solution.)

Continue through the gate and descend the wooden spiral staircase to your left. Three skeevers will emerge and attack, but they shouldn't pose a problem. As you progress further, you will hear [Arvel the Swift](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvel_the_Swift "Skyrim:Arvel the Swift") calling out for help. Some webs block your path; cut through them to proceed.

When you find the thief, Arvel the Swift, he will be trapped in a spider web by a [Wounded Frostbite Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Wounded_Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Wounded Frostbite Spider"). Kill the spider and talk to Arvel. Arvel claims that he will give you the claw if you free him from the web. Once you free him, Arvel will flee, forcing you to pursue him deeper into the dungeon. Alternatively, if the spider is too strong for you, you can just free him from the web and pursue the fleeing Arvel. You can also retreat out of the room to recover, as the spider is too big to leave. If you overtake Arvel quickly, you can kill him yourself; otherwise, he will soon run into a group of draugr, who will likely eliminate him easily. If you protect him from the draugr, he may be killed by the [spike trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") up ahead. The spike trap will reset after use, and can be activated again to help deal with the draugr. You can loot the claw and a [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvel%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Arvel's Journal") from Arvel's body. The journal hints that the claw is actually a key of some sort.

### Find the Secret of Bleak Falls Barrow

The palm of your hand

Although you have found the golden claw, you cannot return it to Lucan until you find the secret of Bleak Falls Barrow, so continue through the chambers. After a while you will find yourself in what appears to be a burial tomb and you will have to fight your way through a group of draugr. If you have not killed Arvel by the time he reaches this room, the draugr will likely kill him. Continue on until you find a [puzzle door](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Door "Skyrim:Puzzle Door") with three animal seals on it. The claw is the key, however it will not open the door like a regular key would. Instead, [examine](/wiki/Skyrim:Controls#Change_View "Skyrim:Controls") the claw in your inventory and you will see several symbols engraved in it, palm side up. Set each ring to the correct seal and open the door. From the outermost to the innermost ring, the solution is **Bear—Moth—Owl**.

When you enter the door, follow the tunnel until you find yourself in a large, open room with waterfalls. You will see a [Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"). When you approach it, one word will stand out, and your character will learn a Word of Power, *[Fus](/wiki/Skyrim:Fus "Skyrim:Fus")*. A level-dependent creature (at low levels a [Draugr Overlord](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr_Overlord "Skyrim:Draugr Overlord") and at higher levels a [Dragon Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest")) will then rise out of a coffin and you will have to kill it. Leave the dungeon and return to the village. To leave the dungeon, climb to the top of the stairs and activate the lever on the pedestal.

There are three chests in this room where you obtain the Word of Power; one centered by the sleeping draugr is quite well seen and unlocked. The second is behind the waterfall on the left. The third has a novice lock and is located to your right behind the waterfall. To find it, go across the bridge but not up the steps leading to the wall, go right along the river path to the bigger waterfall, you will have to jump around on the large stones to the right of the waterfall to gain access to the chest. You will see the chest nesting among the rocks behind the waterfall when in third person view.

### Return the Claw

If you return the Golden Claw, Lucan or Camilla will give you a leveled amount of gold, increase their [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") toward you to "friend" (assuming you previously were not), and return the item to its home on the counter.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 400 |
| 10–19 | 600 |
| 20–29 | 800 |
| 30–39 | 1,000 |
| 40+ | 1,200 |

## Notes

- This quest counts towards the [Sideways](/wiki/Skyrim:Sideways "Skyrim:Sideways") [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") regardless of whether you do the quest for Lucan or Camilla (i.e., both quest stages 100 and 110 qualify).
- You cannot return the claw to Lucan until [this part of the concurrent quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest)#The_Secret_of_Bleak_Falls_Barrow "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)") is complete.
- [The shop](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood_Trader "Skyrim:Riverwood Trader") is open 24 hours if you don't finish this quest.
- While guiding you to the bridge, Camilla frequently gets stuck in place. Walking a few steps exactly behind her in line with the road prevents this, and if already stopped, returning yourself to that exact position will usually make her start walking again. If all fails, just go on and leave her; she will return to Lucan and her directions are not needed for the quest.
- Arvel is immune to any damage before you cut the webs he is trapped into.
- If Camilla is somehow killed Lucan will exclaim how he wishes Camilla was here to see this.
- \* If you don't return the golden claw to Lucan, it will remain a weightless quest item in the inventory, but if you display it on the claw displays of additional houses added by the Creation Club, you can remove it without returning it to Lucan. If you return it to Lucan, it will be placed on the counter and taking it will always be a steal. If you steal a golden claw, you can make the stolen tag invisible while the player is holding it or putting it in the box, but if you display it as a physical object, the stolen tag will not disappear in any way. This affects the display of the golden claw, making it fall all the time when the player re-enters the house.

## Bugs

- If the puzzle door does not work, check [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Totems#Bugs "Skyrim:Puzzle Totems") for possible fixes.
- If you kill Arvel before he turns against you, then you cannot check your next objective. However, this can be fixed by reading his journal and skipping to the last step of returning it to Lucan once the dungeon is finished.
- Casting any [frenzy spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Frenzy_(effect)#Spells "Skyrim:Frenzy (effect)") on the Wounded Frostbite Spider will cause Arvel to run free and begin to fight it. After it dies or the effect wears off, he will stand where he is and engage in the normal dialogue with you. You still have to go cut the webs, and after you do so, he will begin his sprint down the hall like normal.
- If you don't speak to Lucan before going into Bleak Falls Barrow, you may trigger a bug which will prevent you from completing the quest if you attempt to give him the claw after you have obtained it in the dungeon during the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"). You can fix this by loading a save from before the beginning of the quest.
- Even if you finish the quest, the chest in the first floor of the Riverwood Trader may still need to be stolen from. **?**

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.

# Skyrim:The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. | Location(s): | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), [Silverdrift Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Lair "Skyrim:Silverdrift Lair") |

| Added by: | [The Gray Cowl Returns!](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!") |

Follow a series of dead drops in search of the Gray Cowl

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Kill the [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(The_Gray_Cowl_Returns!) "Skyrim:Thief (The Gray Cowl Returns!)") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") graveyard and read his [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief%27s_Note "Skyrim:Thief's Note").
2. Speak to a Riften [beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggars "Skyrim:Beggars") and break into the strongbox in [Bolli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House").
3. Obtain the [deed](/wiki/Skyrim:Land_Title_and_Deed "Skyrim:Land Title and Deed") from [Erikur's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur%27s_House "Skyrim:Erikur's House") and find the barrel behind [The Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever").
4. Locate the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Silverdrift Chest Key") in [Silverdrift Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Lair "Skyrim:Silverdrift Lair") and retrieve the [Ancestral Sword of Clan Ice-Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestral_Sword_of_Clan_Ice-Blade "Skyrim:Ancestral Sword of Clan Ice-Blade").
5. Bring the deed and the sword back to the Riften graveyard for your reward.

### The Gray Cowl

To begin this quest, you must make your way to the [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") graveyard and defend yourself from a confused [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(The_Gray_Cowl_Returns!) "Skyrim:Thief (The Gray Cowl Returns!)") who will attack you on sight (or, if the guards see him before you do, they may kill him and you will get the quest notification to loot his body before you ever found him). He has apparently come to the graveyard following rumors that the Gray Fox, the legendary leader of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), is buried there together with the [Gray Cowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:Gray Cowl of Nocturnal"), a Daedric artifact stolen from [Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nocturnal "Skyrim:Nocturnal") herself. Kill the thief and read the [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief%27s_Note "Skyrim:Thief's Note") on his body to learn that he was an acquaintance of the previous Gray Fox, who had died and therefore passed on his Cowl. It seems this thief had the same idea as you and sought to check the grave. The note also mentions a code phrase to use on the town [beggars](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggars "Skyrim:Beggars"): "Shadow hide you."

Track down either [Edda](/wiki/Skyrim:Edda "Skyrim:Edda") or [Snilf](/wiki/Skyrim:Snilf "Skyrim:Snilf") and say the phrase to be passed a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Stranger%27s_Note "Skyrim:Stranger's Note") from a Stranger. This individual is offering you a job, provided you can break into the strongbox upstairs in [Bolli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House") for further instructions. You can try to [Persuade](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") or Intimidate his wife [Nivenor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nivenor "Skyrim:Nivenor") into giving you the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Nivenor%27s_Strongbox_Key "Skyrim:Nivenor's Strongbox Key") by telling her a thief planted something inside, or you can just pick the lock yourself. Within, you will find a [forged deed](/wiki/Skyrim:Forged_Deed "Skyrim:Forged Deed"), *[Nivenor's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nivenor%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Nivenor's Journal")*, and *[Stranger's Instructions](/wiki/Skyrim:Stranger%27s_Instructions "Skyrim:Stranger's Instructions")*. You can also find a note labeled *[Requested Report](/wiki/Skyrim:Requested_Report "Skyrim:Requested Report")* on an end table in his house for more insight to what is happening. You will need to read the instructions to begin the next stage of the job.

### The Solitude Job

You are instructed to take the forged deed to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and break into [Erikur's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur%27s_House "Skyrim:Erikur's House"), where you will steal the real [land title and deed](/wiki/Skyrim:Land_Title_and_Deed "Skyrim:Land Title and Deed") and replace it with the fake one. However, with a little snooping around the house, you will be pointed towards a *[Letter to Gisli](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_to_Gisli "Skyrim:Letter to Gisli")*, which reveals that [Gisli](/wiki/Skyrim:Gisli "Skyrim:Gisli") and her associates used a young boy as a political puppet in [Jehanna](/wiki/Lore:Jehanna "Lore:Jehanna") to approve land transfers as the most senior member of the Ice-Blade clan, before shipping him off to Riften. If you confront Gisli with this information, you can offer to buy the deed off her for 8,000 gold, or you can attempt to Persuade her with high [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill, without ever needing the forged document. You can also simply pickpocket her.

A stranger in the flesh

Once you have the original deed in hand, head to a barrel behind [The Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever") for your next set of instructions. *[Stranger's Final Instructions](/wiki/Skyrim:Stranger%27s_Final_Instructions "Skyrim:Stranger's Final Instructions")* promises to introduce you to the Gray Fox if you enter [Silverdrift Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Lair "Skyrim:Silverdrift Lair") and recover the [Ancestral Sword of Clan Ice-Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestral_Sword_of_Clan_Ice-Blade "Skyrim:Ancestral Sword of Clan Ice-Blade"). The sword can be found in a locked chest deep inside the dungeon. Though you can just pick open the lock, you can find the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Silverdrift Chest Key") in the next room to the north on the body of a dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). This corpse is distinguished by a lit lantern placed behind it, as well as two "Loot" [shadowmarks](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") above it. The chest also contains a [document](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sword_of_Clan_Ice-Blade "Skyrim:The Sword of Clan Ice-Blade") describing the sword, as well as boss-level loot. You do not have to continue exploring Silverdrift Lair.

### Meeting with a Stranger

After you have exited the dungeon with the Ancestral Sword, you will need to return to the Riften graveyard and locate the Gray Fox's tombstone. There, you will find the *[Stranger's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Stranger%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Stranger's Journal")*, revealing that the current Gray Fox is in fact the true heir of the Ice-Blade clan. After Gisli's associates poisoned his sister and endangered her orphan son, he knew he had to pass on the Cowl to someone else and return to his old life. The journal ends there, but after reading it you will be immediately confronted by none other than the [Gray Fox](/wiki/Skyrim:Stranger "Skyrim:Stranger") himself. He will take the sword and the deed from your possession, granting you the [Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:Gray Cowl of Nocturnal") in return. Having passed on the mantle, the Stranger's true identity is revealed to be [Pjofr Ice-Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Pjofr_Ice-Blade "Skyrim:Pjofr Ice-Blade"), accompanied by his now-rescued nephew [Smaref Ice-Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Smaref_Ice-Blade "Skyrim:Smaref Ice-Blade"). On the promise that you not breathe a word of these events to anyone, Pjofr and his charge depart for Jehanna, leaving you with a powerful enchanted [light](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet").

Just be sure not to equip the Cowl in the middle of town, as it will turn all [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") hostile if they see you wearing it.

## Notes

- This quest would originally begin automatically upon installing [The Gray Cowl Returns!](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). This was changed with the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition") update.
- The thief may be attacked and killed by a patrolling guard off screen without your involvement. That makes the quest appear to start randomly by itself. In that case, just go to the graveyard and locate the body by yourself.
- Using some Thief skills such as Pickpocketing and Lockpicking will cause you to fail Optional objectives to use Speech (Bribery, Persuasion, or Intimidation) with Nivenor and Gisli. Similarly, in Silverdrift Lair, the quest objective is shown to be the chest, which you encounter before finding the relevant corpse.
- The Ancestral Sword never goes into Pjofr Ice-Blade's inventory, so you can't see if it is more powerful when equipped by its rightful owner.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE020_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE020_Quest`.
