# Skyrim:The Guardian Stones

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png) | Standing Stone: The Guardian Stones ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Guardian+Stones)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| GuardianStones | |
| Region | |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | |
| Location | |
| East of [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"), along the road between [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") and [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Clay Deposits](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay "Skyrim:Clay")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | 1 |

The Three Guardian Stones

**The Guardian Stones** is a location which marks three [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") located directly outside of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") and [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood").

They are likely the first standing stones you will encounter, since they are on the path taken while being escorted by [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof") or [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") to Riverwood. The stones are The Mage Stone, The Thief Stone, and The Warrior Stone. If selected, they allow you to specialize in magic, stealth or combat [skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") respectively, by gaining 20% more experience in those skills. [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") is considered a stealth skill in this context.

|  |
| --- |
| - The Mage Stone: *Those under the sign of The Mage will learn all [magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Overview "Skyrim:Magic Overview") skills 20% faster.* - The Thief Stone: *Those under the sign of The Thief will learn all [stealth](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealth "Skyrim:Stealth") skills 20% faster.* - The Warrior Stone: *Those under the sign of The Warrior will learn all [combat](/wiki/Skyrim:Combat "Skyrim:Combat") skills 20% faster.* |

### Achievements

[Achievements](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") related to the Standing Stones are:

-  **Blessed** (10 points/Bronze) — Select a [Standing Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stone "Skyrim:Standing Stone") blessing
-  **Standing Stones** (30 points/Silver) — Find 13 [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stone "Skyrim:Standing Stone")

## Notes

- If you activate one of the Stones while [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof") or [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") are present during [Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm"), they will comment on the Stone you activated.
- Using the [Aetherial Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherial_Crown "Skyrim:Aetherial Crown")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") makes it possible to increase the benefits of The Guardian Stones by using it with [The Lover Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lover_Stone "Skyrim:The Lover Stone"). Do this along with [Rested](/wiki/Skyrim:Rested "Skyrim:Rested") bonuses to obtain the maximum XP boost.
  - Note that you cannot receive a Rested bonus from sleeping while The Lover Stone is active. Therefore, to obtain the maximum XP boost, you must store The Lover Stone in the Crown, unequip it before sleeping, and then re-equip it to apply The Lover Stone while maintaining the Rested bonus.
- Experience gained from [training](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") will benefit from The Guardian Stones and any other XP bonuses. Since one session of training gives exactly one level's worth of XP to a skill, the Guardian Stones will effectively increase this to 1.25 levels of XP for any associated skill. In other words, every 4 sessions of training will grant a free level of XP. Note that the training session itself will not award the bonus level--you must manually level the skill up once the XP bar is nearly full. Any "overflow" XP will be lost.
- There is an [unmarked](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") [shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines") to the southwest of the Guardian Stones location. At the base of the shrine is a dead [Thalmor Justiciar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Justiciar "Skyrim:Thalmor Justiciar") carrying a random piece of enchanted armor.
- Further west is an unmarked necromancer's site close to road that runs along south shore of [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"), connected to the road by short track going south. The site is occupied by a leveled [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer"). Between eight pillars is an altar with lootable skeleton, [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Hearth Fire, v9](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Hearth_Fire,_v9 "Skyrim:2920, Hearth Fire, v9")*, one-handed sword, two gold coins and embalming tool. Next to the altar is a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), some skeletal remains and very close is a patch of [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade").
- Three leveled [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") have established a camp directly south of the Guardian Stones, just south of the road that runs along the south shore of [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=3195&y=-66333&zoom=17&legacy=true). Their belongings include a satchel containing random alchemical ingredients, a black mage robe, a [treasure map](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_I "Skyrim:Treasure Map I") and a copy of the [one-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Night Falls on Sentinel](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Falls_on_Sentinel "Skyrim:Night Falls on Sentinel")*.
- A Thief Stone also appears in the [playroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Playroom "Skyrim:Playroom") for [Skyrim VR](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_VR "Skyrim:Skyrim VR").

## Bugs

- [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") benefits from the Thief Stone's bonus, though it is otherwise considered a combat skill (in internal game data, for the [Oghma Infinium](/wiki/Skyrim:Oghma_Infinium "Skyrim:Oghma Infinium"), and for the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College") sidequests.)
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, addresses this issue. It now benefits from the Warrior Stone's bonus.
- Returning to the Guardian Stones after waiting for the location to respawn (by waiting 10 in game days) will cause the number of discovered Standing Stones to increase by 3, allowing you to earn the "Standing Stones" achievement faster. **?**

# Skyrim:The Guardian Vault

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |

The Guardian Vault

**The Guardian Vault** is a dungeon in [the Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway").

It consists of 2 zones: [(?)](/wiki/Category:Pages_Missing_Data "Category:Pages Missing Data").

## Related Quests

- **[A Soul Divided](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Soul_Divided "Skyrim:A Soul Divided")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnfang_%26_Duskfang "Skyrim:Dawnfang & Duskfang"): Seek out a cursed Tsaesci blade in the Ratway.
- **[Bloodthirst](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodthirst_(quest) "Skyrim:Bloodthirst (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnfang_%26_Duskfang "Skyrim:Dawnfang & Duskfang"): Find a cursed blood-drinking sword.

## Walkthrough

This quest can be triggered in a couple of ways. The official way to begin this quest is to head to Riften and find the "Public Notice" that should be held via dagger to the exterior entrance door to the Ratway on the lower walkway. Sometimes this note will be on the ground or even clipping into the door bottom. It can be found by searching with the cursor. Reading this note begins the quest. The other way to start it is to explore the Ratway until you run into the ghost. She's in the same location as the Skeever cage that holds "Skritch", the tamed Skeever from the [Pets of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim") creation. Not far from this chamber is the location of the Shadowfoot Sanctum entrance.

The ghost will be seen entering The Guardian Vault. Before following her, examine the dead mage named Vellonus and find *[Sellonus's Confession](/wiki/Skyrim:Sellonus%27s_Confession "Skyrim:Sellonus's Confession")*. Upon entering the vault, an alcove on the left holds a skeleton that can be looted of a note entitled, *[Guild Mage's Last Words](/wiki/Skyrim:Guild_Mage%27s_Last_Words "Skyrim:Guild Mage's Last Words")*. Further in, a huge sewer chamber is revealed with a sword floating within some sort of magical field that glows red. There are doors in every direction. The door to the west is open while the rest are sealed shut. Head through that way and you'll face the first of three guardians. Defeat him and explore the chamber. Make your way around the wooden platforms. The first gap across the room can be reached by scaling the wall above the doorway. A guild mage skeleton is visible in the first upper room. Now, leap on the hand railing and make a running jump across to the boards leading to the front of the chamber. Make your way up to find a smuggler's skeleton and loot.

Return to the sword chamber and the magic field changes to Green as the Northern door opens up. Go through that door and go up first to face the second guardian within a small torture chamber. In one of the jails on the left side, you'll see a skeleton sitting. This is [Verrick Tilwald](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Verrick_Tilwald&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Verrick Tilwald (page does not exist)"). He'll immediately attack, so be ready to knock him into a bone pile. *[Verrick's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Verrick%27s_Note "Skyrim:Verrick's Note")* sits on the table with a dagger through it. Reading it adds the side quest [Bloodthirst](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodthirst "Skyrim:Bloodthirst"). Head back out and follow the ramp to the bottom where three Cursed Smugglers emerge from the waters to attack you. Finish them off and return to the sword chamber once more.

This time, you will witness the magic sword turning green, with a mighty rumble. The final door opens for you to enter. Inside is a waterlogged pit type area with steps on the other side leading up to a sarcophagus. Examine some of the numerous skeletons to find some loot and the Guild Mage's Missive. Touch the Tomb of the Guardian's Wife and prepare to fight off hordes of skeletons and cursed smugglers along with the final guardian. Once the guardian's health is diminished, it transforms into [Lorant Bouchard](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Lorant_Bouchard&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Lorant Bouchard (page does not exist)"), who returns with from the dead at full health. Defeat him in corporeal form and loot his corpse for the Letter from Home, along with a [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") sword, shield and entire armor set.

Return to the sword chamber one last time to see the ghosts of Lorant and his wife Emma reuniting. The sword can now be taken.

*This [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")-related article is a [stub](/wiki/UESPWiki:Stub "UESPWiki:Stub"). You can help by [expanding it](https://en.uesp.net/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:The_Guardian_Vault&action=edit).*

# Skyrim:The Hag's Cure

## Overview

The Hag's Cure

**The Hag's Cure** is an apothecary in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") owned and operated by [Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela").

To find it, enter the city gate and turn left, turn right at the first bridge, turn left before going up the stairs at water wheel, cross the bridge, and ascend the stairs to the right, then to the left.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela") (Owner) [Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Apothecary")  [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") (Assistant) |

## Related Quests

- **[Bothela's Discreet Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela%27s_Discreet_Delivery "Skyrim:Bothela's Discreet Delivery")**: Deliver the [Stallion's Potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stallion%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Stallion's Potion") to [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek") or [Reburrus](/wiki/Skyrim:Reburrus_Quintilius "Skyrim:Reburrus Quintilius").
- **[Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes")**: Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## The Hag's Cure

There is a [juniper berry tree](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") outside, at the top of the stairs leading up to the store from [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"). Like most buildings in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") it is built back into the hill and is of Dwemer design and style. Upon entering there is a short corridor leading to stairs down into the store. It consists of a stone counter built across in front of the east wall with a wall to the left separating it from the entry stairs with a few barrels of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks around the building. On the counter are several ingredients and [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") that are [displayed merchandise](#Displayed_Merchandise) along with a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), a single [septim](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a couple of [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), a [cup](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup") and a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"). On the wall between the stairs and counter is a basket containing a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). While under the counter is the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger") and a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Herbalist's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbalist%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:Herbalist's Guide to Skyrim")*. Behind the counter against the east wall is a set of shelves holding a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a plate and [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") as well as several items of displayed merchandise. To the right of the shelves is a small unit holding a copy of *[The Firmament](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firmament "Skyrim:The Firmament")* and a bowl, with two racks hanging from the ceiling above holding a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). Against the south wall, in an alcove is a fireplace with an L-shaped sideboard to the right of it. On the sideboard is a [platter](/wiki/Skyrim:Platter "Skyrim:Platter") holding a [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), with a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and bowl beside it. To the right still against the south wall, in a second alcove is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"). Another alcove is to the west with a large stone table holding various displayed merchandise items. In the middle of the west wall is a flight of stairs up to their sleeping quarters, with a food barrel to the left and on top of it is a piece of bread and cheese. To the right of the stairs is a set of shelves filled with displayed merchandise, in addition to a [tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") and potato. There is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") in the northwest corner with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand between the shelves and chest. There is a small square stone table against the north wall with two wooden chairs pulled up to it. On the table is a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a loaf of bread, a red apple and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"). With another set of shelves to the east separating the entry stairs from the table. These also hold displayed merchandise.

The stairs to the west lead directly into a twin bedroom containing a dresser to the south as you enter containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") with a steel dagger on top. There are two owned single beds opposite each other, one coming out from a curved south wall and the other coming out from a curved north wall. To the left of the one to the south is an end table with an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") and a copy of *[Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbane%27s_Bestiary:_Ice_Wraiths "Skyrim:Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths")*. To the left of this is a round wooden table and chair, with a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine and two loaves of bread on top. To the west is another curved wall with a raised area holding a bowl and plate, with a wash basin to the left and on the floor is a basket containing two gourds and a potato. At the foot of the bed to the north is an unlocked chest. While to the north as you enter the room is an end table with a tomato and medium coin purse on top and a basket containing a few pieces of cheese on the floor beside it.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example on the store counters. They can be purchased from the merchant, or else can be stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

- Ingredients: 2 [Bleeding Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), 7 [Bone Meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), 5 [Chaurus Eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), 3 [Deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), 2 [Dragon's Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue"), 1 [Elves Ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), 1 [Frost Mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), 2 [Garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), 2 [Giant Lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen"), 1 [Glowing Mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom"), 2 [Hagraven Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw"), 1 [Hagraven Feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), 2 [Imp Stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), 3 [Juniper Berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"), 2 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), 1 [Nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade"), 1 [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), 1 [Scaly Pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), 5 [Slaughterfish Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), 3 [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), 1 [Troll Fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat")
- Poisons: 1 [Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), 1 [Weak Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison")
- Potions: 1 [Draught of Extra Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Draught of Extra Magicka"), 1 [Draught of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), 1 [Potion of Extra Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"), 2 [Potion of Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), 1 [Potion of Minor Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), 3 [Potion of Minor Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), 2 [Potion of Plentiful Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing"), 2 [Potion of Plentiful Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Magicka"), 1 [Potion of Resist Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), 1 [Potion of Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), 3 [Potion of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), 1 [Potion of Ultimate Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Ultimate_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Ultimate Magicka"), 1 [Stallion's Potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stallion%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Stallion's Potion")

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the store's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

## Notes

- [Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela") gave the shop its name because she thought "[hag](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag")" suited her in both its sense as an epithet and its sense as denoting an old woman who dabbles in mysterious and misunderstood magic.
- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the bottom left of the entrance door. There are several alchemical ingredients, potions, and poisons found around the store.
- If anything happens to Bothela, her assistant, [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri"), will take over running the store.

The Temple of Dibella

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to the city of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").
2. *(Optional)* Start the [Speak to Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Speak_to_Degaine "Skyrim:Speak to Degaine") quest.
3. Enter the Inner Sanctum of the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").
4. Help the priestesses of [Dibella](/wiki/Lore:Dibella "Lore:Dibella") find a new Sybil.
5. Travel to [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") and learn the location of [Fjotra](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra").
   - *(Optional)* Escort [Enmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Enmon "Skyrim:Enmon") to [Broken Tower Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt").
6. Rescue Fjotra from the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").
7. Escort Fjotra back to the Temple of Dibella.
8. Pray at Dibella's Altar in the Temple of Dibella.

### The Temple of Dibella

The temple located in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") is dedicated to [Dibella](/wiki/Lore:Dibella "Lore:Dibella"), the goddess of love, beauty, and artistry. It is maintained by several priestesses and [Hamal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamal "Skyrim:Hamal"). Upon entering the temple, you will find the priestess [Senna](/wiki/Skyrim:Senna "Skyrim:Senna"), who will inform you that: *"The sisters are communing with Dibella. They can't be disturbed. You'll have to come back another time."* In order to access the Inner Sanctum, you can either try to pick the expert-lock, or steal the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_the_Dibella_Inner_Sanctum "Skyrim:Key to the Dibella Inner Sanctum") from Senna. Note that if you choose to pick the lock and do not accept the deal from the Priestess, you'll have to do it twice—once to get into the Sanctum, and once to get out.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Communing with Dibella  **Exalted Protocol of the Dibellan Sybil** If you are caught by one of the priestesses, they will exclaim: *"What are you doing in here? Stay where you are. The mother will deal with you."* If you ask who their "mother" is, they will direct you to speak with [Hamal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamal "Skyrim:Hamal"). She will then initiate conversation by saying: *"And just what do you think you're doing?"* If you tell her that you were curious about the temple, she will tell you: *"Unfortunately for you, we don't allow men/the uninitiated into the inner sanctum."* Hamal will then continue: *"You have committed a breach, and must pay the penalty."* Asking what the penalty is, she will elaborate: *"Normally, a quick death/period of servitude. Luckily for you, there are more pressing matters. We could make an example of you, but perhaps you could be put to better use."* Also asking what use that would be, she will explain: *"The ceremony you so rudely interrupted was the Exalted Protocol of the Dibellan Sybil. I don't expect you to know what that means. Suffice to say that our Sybil was recently lost to us. Through the Protocol, we have seen the home of the next Sybil, to the north, in a small village pressed against the stone. If you can travel there, and retrieve our young Sybil, your transgression will be forgiven."* | The [Statue of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Statue of Dibella")  **Stealing the Statue of Dibella** If you chose to try to steal the statue for Degaine, and get caught by one of the priestesses, she will inform [Hamal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamal "Skyrim:Hamal"). At this point, if you threaten them, the priestess will say: *"If that's how you choose to end your life, so be it."* If you allow yourself to speak with Hamal, you can tell her that you only came here for the statue. She will then reply with: *"So be it. We gave you a choice."* Both responses result in the priestesses becoming hostile and attacking you. Since none of them are [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") (with the exception of Senna), they can die as a result, causing you to be unable to complete The Heart of Dibella quest. Once you have retrieved the statue, you can turn it over to Degaine who will hastily say: *"Give it to me quickly, before they see us together. You've riled up the priestesses, and the guards don't take kindly to that. Here's your share. Nicely done."* He then gives you 150 gold in exchange for the statue. However, if you managed to steal the statue unnoticed, you may return to the temple and purposely get noticed in order to start the quest The Heart of Dibella. |

### Karthwasten

A distraught [Enmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Enmon "Skyrim:Enmon") working at the smelter

If you choose to help the priestesses find the new Sybil, you are directed to visit [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") and locate the young girl's father, [Enmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Enmon "Skyrim:Enmon"), who may be found working in the mine or at the smelter. If you speak to any of the local residents, they will all direct you to speak to him as well. If you tell him that you are looking for his daughter, he will retort: *"Damn it, man/woman, are you trying to taunt us?"* Asking him what he meant, he will explain: *"Our daughter, [Fjotra](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra"), was taken from here. The [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") descended and... they didn't touch anything else. Just our little girl."* Also asking where they took her, he will continue: *"It was the Forsworn from [Broken Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt"). Never been much trouble before. What's it to you?"* You can now respond to him in two different ways:

If you tell Enmon that you just want his daughter to be safe, he will remark: *"That's... that's good of you. If you were to save her, I would be very grateful. I don't think there's anything I could give you, though..."* However, if you tell Enmon that Fjotra is the new Sybil of Dibella, he will say: *"She... really? That's... I wouldn't have dreamed. Of course, we need her in Markarth, then. I'll come with you."* If you agree that he should travel with you, he will thank you and accompany you to Broken Tower Redoubt. Note that if you take him along with you, he is a non-essential NPC, and can die. You can also tell him that he should stay, and he will reply with urgency: *"You're... probably right. Just hurry, please. Who knows what those things are doing to her."* You are now directed to travel to the Broken Tower Redoubt and rescue Fjotra from the Forsworn holding her captive.

### Touched by the Gods

A [Forsworn Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart") guarding Fjotra's cell

Making your way through the Broken Tower Redoubt, you can find Fjotra in her cell, guarded by a Forsworn Briarheart. After you have defeated the Briarheart and freed her, she will ask: *"Are you one of them? Please don't hurt me."* When you tell her that you are to bring her to the Temple in Markarth, she will exclaim: *"Then it is true what they said? I am touched by the gods?"* Her suspicions confirmed, Fjotra will then accept her title as the new Sybil of Dibella: *"I've heard stories about the wonders of the great Temple in Markarth. But I never dreamed that I would even get to see it. I am honored to be called for this duty. Please, lead on."*

A final farewell

You must now return Fjotra to the Temple to become the new Sybil of Dibella, but you also can take a detour to Karthwasten, so Fjotra can say goodbye to her parents, Enmon and [Mena](/wiki/Skyrim:Mena "Skyrim:Mena"), who will give her a very heart-warming farewell:

**Enmon:** *"Fjotra!"*
**Fjotra:** *"Father!"*
**Enmon:** *"Fjotra, dear. Did they hurt you?"*
**Fjotra:** *"Of course not. My spirit remains strong."*
**Enmon:** *"My little girl. Always strong. Do you know where you have to go?"*
**Fjotra:** *"I'm to go to the temple in Markarth. I... I'll have to leave you and mother."*
**Enmon:** *"It's our honor to have you there. This man/woman is going to take you to Markarth. Are you ready?"*
**Fjotra:** *"Of course."*

Afterwards, Enmon will approach and thank you: *"Thank you for getting her back from the Forsworn. Dibella was smart to have sent you."* You can now return to Hamal in the Temple of Dibella in Markarth to complete the quest.

### A New Sybil

A new Sybil in the Temple of Dibella

Upon arriving back at the temple, Hamal will be grateful for the safe return of Fjotra: *"You... you found her? I can't believe it. Let the girl come with me and we can begin her preparation. I will send word to her family that she is in good hands. You've truly earned the Blessing of Dibella, child. Prostrate yourself before her altar, and she will bestow her gift."* You are now directed to kneel before and then drink the blessed water, which will bestow the [Agent of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Agent_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Agent of Dibella") passive ability. This grants an additional 10% physical damage against enemies of the opposite sex, and the quest will now be marked as complete.

## Notes

- Priestesses Senna, Orla, and Anwen become [marriageable](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") upon completion of this quest.
- If you have previously entered Broken Tower Redoubt and left the door to Fjotra's cell open, it will still be open when you return to rescue her.
- During [The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors") quest for [Molag Bal](/wiki/Skyrim:Molag_Bal "Skyrim:Molag Bal"), [Logrolf the Willful](/wiki/Skyrim:Logrolf_the_Willful "Skyrim:Logrolf the Willful") may also be held captive within Broken Tower Redoubt. If so, and if both of these quests have been started, Fjotra will be in the same prison cell as Logrolf.
- Once you have completed this quest and received the ability [Agent of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Agent_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Agent of Dibella"), you can take almost everything inside the temple, both upstairs and in the Inner Sanctum (excluding higher value potions, poisons, jewelry, soul gems, and gems).
- Originally, [Speak to Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Speak_to_Degaine "Skyrim:Speak to Degaine") was part of this quest. There are several stages in the quest related to it, though they're now unused.

## Bugs

- Being caught inside the Inner Sanctum before stealing the statue may cause the priestesses to turn hostile without triggering any dialogue. **?**
- The quest marker may be displayed incorrectly while at the bottom floor of Broken Tower Redoubt, instructing to go outside while inside and to go inside while outside **?**
- The conclusion scene when returning the Sybil may never play, and after you receive your reward the quest may never actually finish.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- It is possible to tell Hamal you heard there was a valuable statue even if you had already stolen it previously and given it to Degaine.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.8, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| The Heart of Dibella (T01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 60 |  | To appease the priestesses of Dibella, I have agreed to find the young girl who will be their next Sybil. It's been prophesied that she lives in the village of Karthwasten, to the north of Markarth. *Objective 60:* Find the future Sybil of Dibella |
| 70 |  | To appease the priestesses of Dibella, I have agreed to find the young girl who will be their next Sybil. The girl must be rescued from the Forsworn who have kidnapped her. *Objective 70:* Rescue Fjotra from the Forsworn |
| 80 |  | *Objective 80:* Bring Fjotra to the Temple |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Pray at Dibella's Altar |
| 200 | ☑ | After offending the priestesses of Dibella, I paid for my offense by rescuing their new Sybil from the Forsworn. |
| 205 | ☑ | I stole a statue from the Temple of Dibella and sold it to the beggar Degaine. |
| 210 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 10, 20, 30.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage T01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest T01`.

# Skyrim:The Heist Job

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Dwarfmp](/wiki/User:Dwarfmp "User:Dwarfmp"), checked by [Riliane](/wiki/User:Riliane "User:Riliane") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Steal a particular item from a store.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Reward) |
| ID: | TGRSL |

A store's strongbox

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") about heist jobs.
2. Enter the targeted store and break into its strongbox.
3. Return the item to Vex.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After joining the Thieves Guild, [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") will tell you that she handles all the [burglary](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job"), [shill](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shill_Job "Skyrim:The Shill Job"), [sweep](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sweep_Job "Skyrim:The Sweep Job") and heist jobs. Ask her for a heist job and she will ask you to retrieve a single item from a store.

The item is a randomly-selected [gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") or unenchanted piece of [jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry") ([circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Circlet "Skyrim:Circlet"), [necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Necklace "Skyrim:Necklace"), or [ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring "Skyrim:Ring")); see [Leveled Lists](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Thieves_Guild_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") for full details. It is always found in the store's strongbox, which is protected with a leveled lock. The strongbox will also contain a random amount of gold (if you have not previously looted it), which can also be stolen to supplement your quest reward.

The quest can send you any one of 28 possible stores. You may be assigned the same location more than once.

| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Arnleif and Sons Trading Company](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnleif_and_Sons_Trading_Company "Skyrim:Arnleif and Sons Trading Company") [The Hag's Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hag%27s_Cure "Skyrim:The Hag's Cure") [Markarth Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Stables "Skyrim:Markarth Stables") [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") | [The Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb") [Elgrim's Elixirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim%27s_Elixirs "Skyrim:Elgrim's Elixirs") [Haelga's Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse") [Pawned Prawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawned_Prawn "Skyrim:Pawned Prawn") [Riften Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Stables "Skyrim:Riften Stables") [The Scorched Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Scorched_Hammer "Skyrim:The Scorched Hammer") | [Angeline's Aromatics](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline%27s_Aromatics "Skyrim:Angeline's Aromatics") [Bits and Pieces](/wiki/Skyrim:Bits_and_Pieces "Skyrim:Bits and Pieces") [Fletcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Fletcher_(place) "Skyrim:Fletcher (place)") [Radiant Raiment](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant_Raiment "Skyrim:Radiant Raiment") [Solitude Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Stables "Skyrim:Solitude Stables") [The Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever") | [Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Arcadia's Cauldron") [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") [Belethor's General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Belethor%27s_General_Goods "Skyrim:Belethor's General Goods") [The Drunken Huntsman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Drunken_Huntsman "Skyrim:The Drunken Huntsman") [Warmaiden's](/wiki/Skyrim:Warmaiden%27s "Skyrim:Warmaiden's") [Whiterun Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables") | [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") [East Empire Company](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_(place) "Skyrim:East Empire Company (place)") [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub") [Sadri's Used Wares](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Used_Wares "Skyrim:Sadri's Used Wares") [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(place) "Skyrim:The White Phial (place)") [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables") |

You must not be caught and sent to jail while the quest is active, for any reason, otherwise you will fail the quest; you also cannot kill anyone living in the store (successfully completing a brawl is considered a killing). Once you have retrieved the item, return to Vex for a leveled gold reward.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |
| 16-20 | 200 |
| 21-26 | 250 |
| 27-31 | 300 |
| 32-36 | 350 |
| 37-41 | 400 |
| 42+ | 500 |

## Notes

- If one of the store's occupants dies for any reason while the quest is active (even if you are not responsible), you will fail the quest.
- If you complete [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine") while this quest is active in Markarth, you will fail the quest because it counts as an arrest.

## Bugs

- If the stolen item has the same FormID as another item in your inventory, it is possible for the wrong item to be removed from the inventory upon quest completion. For example, if the quest object is a stolen emerald ring and you are also wearing an enchanted emerald ring, the enchanted ring may be removed instead of the stolen ring upon handing in the quest. You may also be stuck with stolen item that is marked as a "quest item", making all such items undroppable and unsellable (although, if you get arrested, it will be taken along with all other stolen items).

Be cautious when you advance the quest using console, it might cause glitch to Vex, that she won't provide any quest anymore. To avoid this glitch make sure to start conversation with Vex before using console (don't quit the dialogue option), then use console command, then tell Vex that you have finished the Quest.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGRSL stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGRSL`.

# Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by multiple users, checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Main.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Main.png) | **Retrieve a [Greybeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") artifact from [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav").** |

| Reward: | Final word of [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force"), Word for the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout, Formal recognition as Dragonborn, Free access to High Hrothgar |

| --- | |

The final chamber for the Horn

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Attempt to retrieve the [Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:Horn of Jurgen Windcaller") from [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav").
2. Meet with whoever took the Horn in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood").
3. Return the Horn to [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir").
4. Learn the Word of Power from [Wulfgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulfgar "Skyrim:Wulfgar").
5. Receive the Greybeards' formal recognition.

### Ustengrav

After completing [The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice"), [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir") will assign you one last task to prove you are Dragonborn: retrieve the [Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:Horn of Jurgen Windcaller"), so named after the [founder](/wiki/Skyrim:Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:Jurgen Windcaller") of the Greybeards. The Horn is located in the ruin of [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav"), which Arngeir marks on your map.

The simplest way to reach Ustengrav is to take a carriage to the town of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), then travel the marshes on foot. The ruins are due northeast of the town. If you wish to walk, the fastest route from the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World") is to pass through the fields around [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and follow the route northwest directly through [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian"). However, this route will require you to deal with the multiple [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") that roam the exterior of Labyrinthian. When you arrive at Ustengrav, you'll encounter some bandits who have been enthralled by a necromancer. You may also encounter a mudcrab. Once the danger has passed, travel into the ruin.

The first level of the ruin is fairly straightforward, with a few bandits, warlocks, and [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") to deal with, or let them kill each other. The groups here are often small enough to be handled alone. They are also hostile to each other, so sneaking and following the mages deeper into the ruin will allow for the groups to thin each other. Deal with any remaining draugr and descend into the second zone of the ruin.
*Note: More detailed information about Ustengrav can be found on [this page](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav").*

### Into the Depths

Skeletons dwell in the depths.

Upon entering Ustengrav Depths, you will see a sparsely forested chasm with a waterfall and a bridge far below. To descend, navigate the winding path through the rest of the ruin. You will encounter several draugr and a fire trap along the way. The outdoor area itself hosts several [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") archers, both on the ground by the bridge and in the somewhat higher level with the wooden barricade. These can be easily defeated with ranged attacks. In the room with the tall pillars, a skeleton seated on a throne will come to life at your approach. If you jump to the rocks on the left at the top of the ramp leading down into the room, then jump and use [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") between the circular platforms on the pillars, you will reach a secret room with a soul gem and a chest.

Near the bottom of the waterfall is a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") with a word for the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout. It can be seen from the bridge, and is reachable by a small path carved from the side of the cave wall. Behind the waterfall is a hidden area containing a draugr and small amounts of loot. The Horn, however, lies on the other side of the bridge. After gaining the word, return up the path and cross the bridge. On the way back up, on the right side, there is a ramp leading up to a ledge with a chest; a corundum and a silver vein can be found nearby.

Red glowing runes

Across the bridge, a lone skeleton can be found. It can easily be dispatched. The main feature, of the area, are the three outcrops of rock carved with runes. There is also a tunnel with all of its gates down. Each of the rocks glows red at your approach and lifts one of the gates barring passage through the tunnel. However, the gates will often shut soon upon opening. The easiest solution is to use the Whirlwind Sprint shout, using it to sprint through the stones opens the gates long enough to walk through them all. Once you are clear, the gates will remain fully open, allowing any followers to catch up. With only one word of the shout learned, getting all three gates to stay open long enough is trickier. The gate can be opened by starting at the rock closest to the bridge, sprint by each of them until you get close to the tunnel entrance, and from there use Whirlwind Sprint to clear all the gates at once. It is also possible to stand in front of the first rock, use Whirlwind Sprint, and then run through the rest of the tunnel. It is also possible to stand between the first two rocks to open the first two gates, use Whirlwind Sprint and then run; the third gate should stay open by then. Use Whirlwind Sprint just as the third rock lights up. If you become trapped between gates inside the tunnel, you will find pull chains that will allow you to return to the rocks and try again.

The floors of the next few chambers are covered with fire traps. There are two [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") on the cobwebbed arch. The pair of spiders can be lured onto the traps. It's possible to avoid the traps by staying close to the walls. The traps have a slightly delayed reaction to your passing over them, so if you're on your own, you can get away by using the Whirlwind Sprint shout, or the Become Ethereal shout, or just sprinting forward and you won't be badly burned. The sides also contain some areas of trap free space (The lighter tiles are safe to step on, while the darker ones will trigger flame traps). The Sneak perk, Light Foot, will also work for bypassing the trap. Another solution is to shoot the tiles with a spell such as Firebolt or Ice Spike. Flames/Sparks, etc. do not work. The impact of a bolt or spike is enough to set off the trap if it is not a safe tile. Any follower brought here may be in danger as long as you are in the trapped area. They will continuously take damage from the traps.

After walking through here, you will find a large room. This room contains a more powerful giant spider hiding in the ceiling, as well as smaller spiders. The giant spider will attempt to ambush you when you get close. Using [resist poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Poison "Skyrim:Resist Poison") and [resist frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Frost "Skyrim:Resist Frost") potions may help you survive this encounter.

After dispatching the spiders, cut or burn through the two sets of cobwebs covering the tunnel. If you are collecting [alchemical ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), you will find three [spider eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg") in the egg sacs in the spiders' nest. Otherwise, go right ahead and enter the final chamber.

### Note for the Dragonborn

A mysterious note?

As you make your way through the final room, four Nordic dragon carvings rise out of pools of water. On the pedestal where the Horn should be resting, you will instead find [a mysterious note](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Note_(Delphine) "Skyrim:Mysterious Note (Delphine)") addressed to "the Dragonborn". It states that the Horn has been removed, and requests that you meet the note's anonymous author by renting an attic room at the [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn") in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). The anonymous "friend" has politely left the treasure room undisturbed.

Having failed the task, do as the note says and go to Riverwood. When you speak to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") about renting the appropriate room, she will tell you that there is no attic room, but that you can take the one on the left. Delphine follows you, reveals that she was the one who took the Horn, and gives the Horn to you. She asks to speak privately, and she will lead you to the room across from yours. Delphine opens the wardrobe door, revealing a secret room beneath the inn. In this room, she tells you that [her organization](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") has been looking for someone like you, and that she took the Horn in order to get your attention. This exchange with her begins the quest [A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark"). After speaking with her, you are free to return the Horn to High Hrothgar and complete the quest.

### Return to High Hrothgar

Return to High Hrothgar with the Horn and present it to Arngeir, completing the task he originally gave you. Arngeir will go to the main hall, where the other Greybeards are assembled, and Wulfgar will teach you the final word of the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout. There the Greybeards will speak to you at once in the dragon language, formally recognizing you as Dragonborn. (You are not harmed by this exchange.)

| Dragon Tongue | Direct translation | According to Arngeir |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Lingrah krosis saraan Strundu'ul, voth nid balaan klov praan nau.** | Long (in) sorrow (has) waited (the) Stormcrown, with no worthy head to rest on. | *Long has the Stormcrown languished, with no worthy brow to sit upon.* |
| **Naal Thu'umu, mu ofan nii nu, Dovahkiin, naal suleyk do Kaan, naal suleyk do Shor, ahrk naal suleyk do Atmorasewuth.** | By our Voice we give it now (to you), Dragonborn, by (the) power of Kyne, by (the) power of Shor, and by (the) power of Atmora-of-old. | *By our breath we bestow it now to you in the name of Kyne, in the name of Shor, and in the name of Atmora of Old.* |
| **Meyz nu Ysmir, Dovahsebrom. Dahmaan daar rok.** | (You have) become now Ysmir, Dragon of the North. Remember these words. | *You are Ysmir now, the Dragon of the North, hearken to it.* |

This completes the quest, and from now on, any item in High Hrothgar can be taken.

### Achievement

Although not directly tied to completing this quest, most players will unlock the following achievement during this quest, when the final word of [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") is learned:

-  **Words of Power** (10 points/Bronze) — Learn all three words of a [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts")

## Notes

- With the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") add-on installed, [cultists](/wiki/Skyrim:Cultist "Skyrim:Cultist") will begin to track you down once the quest has begun. They will be hostile no matter what you tell them. Refusing to speak to them will also make them hostile. This will start the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)") questline as well.
- If you return to Jurgen Windcaller's coffin in Ustengrav after completing the quest, you can activate it to gain a dragon soul.
  - It is possible to gain two or more dragon souls if you rapidly use the Activate button on the altar.
- If you read Delphine's note immediately after discovering that the Horn is missing from the altar, the objective to do so won't appear in your journal. It will instead directly jump to having you meet Delphine. You will still fail the objective to retrieve the Horn from Ustengrav, though, and your journal will still say "Meet with whoever took the Horn".
- Delphine's secret room contains several [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and useful [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), as well as books and some weapons on the wall racks, all of which are free to take.
- Upon completion of this quest, you can ask Arngeir for additional training in the dragon tongue. He will say that it would be dangerous for you to grow your power too quickly, but that finding words of power would provide a way to temper your power with experience. From then on, you can ask Arngeir if the Greybeards have heard any ["whisperings of the words"](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Words_of_Power "Skyrim:The Words of Power"), which will tell you where one of the words of power can be found in Skyrim. Your map will also be updated accordingly.
  - If no more words of power can be found, Arngeir will instead say *"There is only silence right now. Perhaps later we will hear one of the lost Words."*
- It is possible to reach the base of the waterfall by climbing down the chasm near the entrance. You can do this by carefully jumping on the overhanging rock on the edge of the overlook, then sliding down the large pillar. In this way, you can cut the length of the trip by half.
- The Daedric script on the stone pedestal, where you find Delphine's note instead of the horn, reads "Windcaller".
- If you miss the Word Wall for the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout in Ustengrav during this quest, Arngeir may send you back there later. Likewise, the [Letter from a Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_a_Friend "Skyrim:Letter from a Friend") may do the same.
- If you take a follower to High Hrothgar when you return the horn, they don't take damage though they do move and are affected by the shouting. However, a follower standing in close proximity to you may prevent the Greybeards from initiating their shouts; if this happens, lead the follower well away from them or order your follower to wait somewhere out of the way, then return to the spot in the center of the room between the Greybeards.
- Once Wulfgar teaches you the final word of Unrelenting Force, you won't be able to move until the shouting ceremony is finished.
- If you activate third-person camera during the shouting ceremony, your character will be seen being partially ragdolled a couple of times.
- If you tell Delphine "I don't have time for this" and it doesn't trigger the bug below, this will disable random dragon encounters until you return to her to start the next quest.
- If Wulfgar refuses to teach you the next word of power to the Unrelenting Force shout after collecting the horn from Delphine and handing it over to Arngeir, this may be because you proceeded too fast through the sprinting section. As such, the Greybeards will be waiting for you to get close to and succeed or fail the Whirlwind Sprint test. Doing so will reset the Greybeards and they'll then proceed inside where you can learn your next word of Unrelenting Force from them. This does not impede quest progress beyond being a minor nuisance.

## Bugs

- The Greybeards may stay in the courtyard of High Hrothgar, standing in the places where they taught you the Whirlwind Sprint shout, and won't move to teach you the last word of Unrelenting Force, breaking the rest of the main quest.
  - Possible fixes include using Whirlwind Sprint through the gate, or closing the gate.
- Delphine may not be at the inn when you get there.
- If you tell Delphine *"I don't have time for this."* and leave to return the horn (or tab out of the conversation and just leave once you have the horn), Arngeir might not talk to you to receive the horn, breaking the main quest.
- You may not be able to pass the puzzle room with the red glowing stones. After using Whirlwind shout while activating the gates, there may be an invisible wall that keeps you from proceeding.
- Wulfgar might not be in High Hrothgar but might be off the mountain. If you find him the quest will continue but he will not be in High Hrothgar to complete the greeting. This problem is on Skyrim Special Edition. **?**
  -  While in High Hrothgar, in the console, type `prid 886B6` and then Enter. Then type `moveto player`. Wulfgar will appear and the quest will continue.
- When speaking to Einarth, Borri, or Wulfgar after the quest is finished, the rumble as each one says "Dovahkiin" starts before the word is spoken.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, addresses this issue. It will now start AFTER the word is spoken.

## Quest Stages

| The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller (MQ105Ustengrav) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | After demonstrating my ability to learn Words of Power and to Shout, the Greybeard Arngeir has sent me on a final trial - retrieving the Horn of Jurgen Windcaller from his tomb in Ustengrav, a burial mound in the marshes of Hjaalmarch. *Objective 10:* Retrieve the Horn of Jurgen Windcaller |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Read the note |
| 20 |  | After demonstrating my ability to learn Words of Power and to Shout, the Greybeard Arngeir sent me on a final trial - retrieving the Horn of Jurgen Windcaller from his tomb in Ustengrav. Unfortunately, when I reached the tomb, I found that someone had replaced the Horn of Jurgen Windcaller with a note asking me to meet them in the Sleeping Giant Inn in Riverwood. *Objective 20:* Meet with whoever took the horn |
| 30 |  | After demonstrating my ability to learn Words of Power and to Shout, the Greybeard Arngeir sent me on a final trial - retrieving the Horn of Jurgen Windcaller from his tomb in Ustengrav. When I arrived, the horn was missing, and in its place was a note from Delphine asking me to meet her in Riverwood. Delphine has given me the horn, so I can now return to Arngeir and complete my training. *Objective 30:* Return the horn to Arngeir |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Learn the Word of Power from Wulfgar |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Receive the Greybeards' greeting |
| 60 | ☑ | After demonstrating my ability to learn Words of Power and to Shout, the Greybeard Arngeir sent me on a final trial - retrieving the Horn of Jurgen Windcaller from his tomb in Ustengrav. When I arrived, the Horn was missing, and in its place was a note from Delphine asking me to meet her in Riverwood. Delphine gave me the Horn, and I returned it to Arngeir to complete my trial. The Greybeards then greeted me formally as Dragonborn, and High Hrothgar is now open to me. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MQ105Ustengrav stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MQ105Ustengrav`.
